Metadata ▶

  • Title: Śukasaptati, “Textus Simplicior”
  • Author: (Unknown)
  • Source File: Word document by Viliam Gostishchev, obtained directly from creator through private email exchange.
  • Edition Short: Schmidt 1893
  • Edition:

    Schmidt, Richard. “Die Çukasaptati. Textus Simplicior.” Abhandlungen für die Kunde des Morgenlandes, Band X, No. 1. Leipzig, 1893.

    NB: Band X as a whole (Nos. 1–4) was published in 1897.

  • PDFs:
    • 1897 Band X on Archive (DLI & public.resource.org)
    • 1893 Band X, No. 1 (improved by V. Gostishchev) on Archive, to be uploaded soon...
  • Digitization Notes:
    • (202_–2025): V. Gostishchev: Typed up from edition, intensively proofread and structured.
    • (July 2025): Tyler Neill: Restructured for HANSEL.
  • Extent:
    • Complete (with small lacunae).
    • 205pp in edition.
  • File Size (KB): 174
  • Genres:
    • Kāvya
    • Kathā
  • Structure: The work consists of 70 stories in a frame story. The frame story's introduction and conclusion are not explicitly distinguished with distinct sections.
  • Translations:
    • German, editor = R. Schmidt, 1894, on HathiTrust
    • German, editor = R. Schmidt, 1913, on Archive
  • Additional Notes:
    • The Simplicior is believed to be older than the Ornatior.
    • Indian editions (e.g. Ramakant Tripathi, Vārāṇasī, 1966, basis of the GRETIL text) are based on this Simplicior text by Schmidt.
    • V. Gostishchev's original version of the file contains added chāyās from the Indian editions and other useful notes.
    • See also the editor's: “Anmerkungen zu dem Textus simplicior der Śukasaptati”, ZDMG 48, 1894, 580-628.
    • This text still needs a final proofread.

§ 1

(p.1, l.1)

p.1, l.1

|| śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ || (p.1, l.2)

|| śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ ||

p.1, l.2

praṇamya śāradāṃ devīṃ divyavijñānaśālinīm |(p.1, l.3)
 vacmi cetovinodārtham uddhāraṃ kīrasaṃmateḥ || 1.1 (= 1) ||(p.1, l.4)
praṇamya śāradāṃ devīṃ divyavijñānaśālinīm | vacmi cetovinodārtham uddhāraṃ kīrasaṃmateḥ || 1.1 (= 1) ||

p.1, l.4

asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vikramaseno nāma rājā babhūva | (p.1, l.5)
tasmin nagare haridatto nāma śreṣṭhī | tasya bhāryā śṛṅgārasundarīnāmnī | (p.1, l.6)
tatputro madanavinodanāmā babhūva | tasya patnī prabhāvatī | sā somadattaśreṣṭhinaḥ (p.1, l.7)
kanyā | madanavinodas tu atīva viṣayāsaktaḥ kuputraḥ (p.1, l.8)
pituḥ śikṣāṃ na śṛṇoti | tasya dyūtamṛgayāveśyāmadyādiṣu atīva āsaktiḥ | (p.1, l.9)
kumārgacāriṇaṃ taṃ kuputraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpitā haridattaḥ sapatnīkaḥ (p.1, l.10)
atīva duḥkhitaḥ saṃjātaḥ | taṃ haridattaṃ kuputraduḥkhena pīḍitaṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.1, l.11)
tasya sakhā trivikramanāmā dvijaḥ svagṛhato nītinipuṇaṃ śukaṃ sārikāṃ (p.1, l.12)
ca gṛhītvā tadgṛhe gatvā prāha | sakhe haridatta enaṃ śukaṃ sapatnīkaṃ (p.1, l.13)
putravat tvaṃ paripālaya | etatsaṃrakṣaṇena tava duḥkhaṃ dūrībhaviṣyati | haridattas (p.1, l.14)
tu taṃ śukaṃ gṛhītvā putrāya samarpayām āsa | madanavinodena śayanamandire (p.2, l.1)
svarṇapañjarasthaḥ sthāpitaḥ paripoṣitaś ca | athaikadā rahasi (p.2, l.2)
śuko madanaṃ prāha | he sakhe (p.2, l.3)

asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vikramaseno nāma rājā babhūva | tasmin nagare haridatto nāma śreṣṭhī | tasya bhāryā śṛṅgārasundarīnāmnī | tatputro madanavinodanāmā babhūva | tasya patnī prabhāvatī | sā somadattaśreṣṭhinaḥ kanyā | madanavinodas tu atīva viṣayāsaktaḥ kuputraḥ pituḥ śikṣāṃ na śṛṇoti | tasya dyūtamṛgayāveśyāmadyādiṣu atīva āsaktiḥ | kumārgacāriṇaṃ taṃ kuputraṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpitā haridattaḥ sapatnīkaḥ atīva duḥkhitaḥ saṃjātaḥ | taṃ haridattaṃ kuputraduḥkhena pīḍitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasya sakhā trivikramanāmā dvijaḥ svagṛhato nītinipuṇaṃ śukaṃ sārikāṃ ca gṛhītvā tadgṛhe gatvā prāha | sakhe haridatta enaṃ śukaṃ sapatnīkaṃ putravat tvaṃ paripālaya | etatsaṃrakṣaṇena tava duḥkhaṃ dūrībhaviṣyati | haridattas tu taṃ śukaṃ gṛhītvā putrāya samarpayām āsa | madanavinodena śayanamandire svarṇapañjarasthaḥ sthāpitaḥ paripoṣitaś ca | athaikadā rahasi śuko madanaṃ prāha | he sakhe

p.2, l.3

pitros te duḥkhinor duḥkhāt pataty aśrucayo bhuvi |(p.2, l.4)
 tena pāpena te vatsa patanaṃ devaśarmavat || 1.2 (= 2) ||(p.2, l.5)
pitros te duḥkhinor duḥkhāt pataty aśrucayo bhuvi | tena pāpena te vatsa patanaṃ devaśarmavat || 1.2 (= 2) ||

p.2, l.5

sa prāha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | (p.2, l.6)
tatra satyaśarmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tadbhāryā dharmaśīlānāmnī putras tu devaśarmā | (p.2, l.7)
sa ca adhītavidyaḥ pitṛpracchannavṛttyā deśāntaraṃ gatvā bhāgīrathītīre (p.2, l.8)
tapaḥ kṛtavān | ekadā sa tapasvī gaṅgātīre japārtham upaviṣṭaḥ | tasmin (p.2, l.9)
kāle kayācit balākayā uḍḍīyamānayā tadaṅgopari purīṣotsargaḥ (p.2, l.10)
kṛtaḥ | sa ca tapasvī krodhākulitanetraḥ yāvad ūrdhvaṃ paśyati tāvat tatkrodhāgninā (p.2, l.11)
bhasmībhūtāṃ balākāṃ bhūmau patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā (balākāṃ dagdhvā) (p.2, l.12)
nārāyaṇadvijagṛhe bhikṣārthaṃ yayau | svabhartṛśuśrūṣāparayā tatpatnyā kopābhiviṣṭo (p.2, l.13)
nirbhartsitaḥ satpakṣihāyam uktaś ca | nāhaṃ balākeva tvatkopasthānam | (p.2, l.14)
sa ca pracchannapātakajñānād bhīto vismitaś ca preṣitaś ca tayā (p.3, l.1)
dharmavyādhapārśve vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ yayau | tatra raktāktahastaṃ yamapratibhaṃ (p.3, l.2)
māṃsavikrayaṃ vidadhānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛśām ante sthitaḥ | vyādhena svāgatapraśnapūrvakaṃ (p.3, l.3)
svagṛhaṃ nītvā nijapitarau sabhaktikaṃ bhojayitvā paścāt tasya bhojanaṃ (p.3, l.4)
dattam | tadanantaraṃ sa ca vyādhaṃ jñānakāraṇaṃ papraccha | kathaṃ satī (p.3, l.5)
jñānavatī kathaṃ ca tvaṃ jñānavān | tena vyādhenoktam | (p.3, l.6)

sa prāha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra satyaśarmā brāhmaṇaḥ | tadbhāryā dharmaśīlānāmnī putras tu devaśarmā | sa ca adhītavidyaḥ pitṛpracchannavṛttyā deśāntaraṃ gatvā bhāgīrathītīre tapaḥ kṛtavān | ekadā sa tapasvī gaṅgātīre japārtham upaviṣṭaḥ | tasmin kāle kayācit balākayā uḍḍīyamānayā tadaṅgopari purīṣotsargaḥ kṛtaḥ | sa ca tapasvī krodhākulitanetraḥ yāvad ūrdhvaṃ paśyati tāvat tatkrodhāgninā bhasmībhūtāṃ balākāṃ bhūmau patitāṃ dṛṣṭvā (balākāṃ dagdhvā) nārāyaṇadvijagṛhe bhikṣārthaṃ yayau | svabhartṛśuśrūṣāparayā tatpatnyā kopābhiviṣṭo nirbhartsitaḥ satpakṣihāyam uktaś ca | nāhaṃ balākeva tvatkopasthānam | sa ca pracchannapātakajñānād bhīto vismitaś ca preṣitaś ca tayā dharmavyādhapārśve vārāṇasīṃ nagarīṃ yayau | tatra raktāktahastaṃ yamapratibhaṃ māṃsavikrayaṃ vidadhānaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛśām ante sthitaḥ | vyādhena svāgatapraśnapūrvakaṃ svagṛhaṃ nītvā nijapitarau sabhaktikaṃ bhojayitvā paścāt tasya bhojanaṃ dattam | tadanantaraṃ sa ca vyādhaṃ jñānakāraṇaṃ papraccha | kathaṃ satī jñānavatī kathaṃ ca tvaṃ jñānavān | tena vyādhenoktam |

p.3, l.6

nijānvayapraṇītaṃ yaḥ samyag dharmaṃ niṣevate |(p.3, l.7)
 uttamādhamamadhyeṣu vikāreṣu parāṅmukhaḥ || 1.3 (= 3) ||(p.3, l.8)
nijānvayapraṇītaṃ yaḥ samyag dharmaṃ niṣevate | uttamādhamamadhyeṣu vikāreṣu parāṅmukhaḥ || 1.3 (= 3) ||
sa gṛhī sa muniḥ sādhuḥ sa ca yogī sa dhārmikaḥ |(p.3, l.9)
 pitṛśuśrūṣako nityaṃ jantuḥ sādhāraṇaś ca yaḥ || 1.4 (= 4) ||(p.3, l.10)
sa gṛhī sa muniḥ sādhuḥ sa ca yogī sa dhārmikaḥ | pitṛśuśrūṣako nityaṃ jantuḥ sādhāraṇaś ca yaḥ || 1.4 (= 4) ||

p.3, l.10

ahaṃ sāpi ca evaṃ jñāninau tvaṃ ca nijapitarau parityajya bhraman mādṛśāṃ (p.3, l.11)
na sambhāṣaṇārhaḥ | param atithiṃ matvā jalpitaḥ | evam uktaḥ sa brāhmaṇo (p.3, l.12)
vinayaparaṃ vyādhaṃ papraccha | tenoktam | (p.3, l.13)

ahaṃ sāpi ca evaṃ jñāninau tvaṃ ca nijapitarau parityajya bhraman mādṛśāṃ na sambhāṣaṇārhaḥ | param atithiṃ matvā jalpitaḥ | evam uktaḥ sa brāhmaṇo vinayaparaṃ vyādhaṃ papraccha | tenoktam |

p.3, l.13

na pūjayanti ye pūjyān mānyān no mānayanti ye |(p.4, l.1)
 jīvanti nindyamānās te mṛtāḥ svargaṃ na yānti ca || 1.5 (= 5) ||(p.4, l.2)
na pūjayanti ye pūjyān mānyān no mānayanti ye | jīvanti nindyamānās te mṛtāḥ svargaṃ na yānti ca || 1.5 (= 5) ||
vyādhena bodhitas tena sa yayau gṛham ātmanaḥ |(p.4, l.3)
 abhavat kīrtimān loke parataḥ kīrtibhājanam || 1.6 (= 6) ||(p.4, l.4)
vyādhena bodhitas tena sa yayau gṛham ātmanaḥ | abhavat kīrtimān loke parataḥ kīrtibhājanam || 1.6 (= 6) ||

p.4, l.4

tasmād vaṇigdharmaṃ svakulodbhavaṃ smara pitroś ca vinayaparo bhava | evam uktaḥ (p.4, l.5)
sa madanaḥ pitarau namaskṛtya tadanujñāto bhāryāṃ cāpṛcchya pravahaṇam adhirūḍhavān (p.4, l.6)
gato deśāntaram | paścāt tatpatnī katicid dināni śokayuktā (p.4, l.7)
nirvāhya svairiṇībhiḥ sakhībhiḥ pratibodhitā puruṣāntarābhilāṣukābhavat | (p.4, l.8)
yatas tābhir evam uktam | (p.4, l.9)

tasmād vaṇigdharmaṃ svakulodbhavaṃ smara pitroś ca vinayaparo bhava | evam uktaḥ sa madanaḥ pitarau namaskṛtya tadanujñāto bhāryāṃ cāpṛcchya pravahaṇam adhirūḍhavān gato deśāntaram | paścāt tatpatnī katicid dināni śokayuktā nirvāhya svairiṇībhiḥ sakhībhiḥ pratibodhitā puruṣāntarābhilāṣukābhavat | yatas tābhir evam uktam |

p.4, l.9

tāvat pitā tathā bandhur yāvaj jīvati mānavaḥ |(p.4, l.10)
 mṛto mṛta iti jñātvā kṣaṇāt sneho nivartate || 1.7 (= 7) ||(p.5, l.1)
tāvat pitā tathā bandhur yāvaj jīvati mānavaḥ | mṛto mṛta iti jñātvā kṣaṇāt sneho nivartate || 1.7 (= 7) ||

p.5, l.1

atas tvaṃ svapatim aprāpyamānā nijaśarīrasya katiciddinasthāyiyauvanasya (p.5, l.2)
puruṣāntararamaṇād gṛhāṇa phalam | tatas tāsāṃ vacanena puruṣāntarasya guṇacandrasaṃjñasya (p.5, l.3)
ramaṇāya śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya yāvat pracalitā tāvat sārikayā (p.5, l.4)
mā gacchety ādivacanair nirbhartsitā | tato yāvat sā tāṃ sārikāṃ galamoṭanapūrvaṃ (p.5, l.5)
vināśayati tāvad uḍḍīya yayau | tataḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā sveṣṭadevatāṃ (p.5, l.6)
hṛdi smṛtvā tāmbūlaṃ pragṛhya yāvac calitā tāvat śukaḥ prāha | (p.5, l.7)
siddhir astu | kva gantavyam ity ādivākyaiḥ pṛṣṭā | sā ca śukavacanaṃ śakunam (p.5, l.8)
iti kṛtvā prahasya tam āha | he śukarāja narāntarāsvādaṃ vijñātuṃ (p.5, l.9)
pracalitāsmi | śuka uvāca | yuktam idaṃ kartavyam eva paraṃ duṣkaraṃ ninditaṃ (p.5, l.10)
ca kulastrīṇām | kiṃ ca | tadā gamyatāṃ yadi viparīte samāyāte (p.5, l.11)
sati tava buddhir asti | yadi nāsti tadā parābhavapadaṃ bhaviṣyasi | (p.6, l.1)

atas tvaṃ svapatim aprāpyamānā nijaśarīrasya katiciddinasthāyiyauvanasya puruṣāntararamaṇād gṛhāṇa phalam | tatas tāsāṃ vacanena puruṣāntarasya guṇacandrasaṃjñasya ramaṇāya śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya yāvat pracalitā tāvat sārikayā mā gacchety ādivacanair nirbhartsitā | tato yāvat sā tāṃ sārikāṃ galamoṭanapūrvaṃ vināśayati tāvad uḍḍīya yayau | tataḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā sveṣṭadevatāṃ hṛdi smṛtvā tāmbūlaṃ pragṛhya yāvac calitā tāvat śukaḥ prāha | siddhir astu | kva gantavyam ity ādivākyaiḥ pṛṣṭā | sā ca śukavacanaṃ śakunam iti kṛtvā prahasya tam āha | he śukarāja narāntarāsvādaṃ vijñātuṃ pracalitāsmi | śuka uvāca | yuktam idaṃ kartavyam eva paraṃ duṣkaraṃ ninditaṃ ca kulastrīṇām | kiṃ ca | tadā gamyatāṃ yadi viparīte samāyāte sati tava buddhir asti | yadi nāsti tadā parābhavapadaṃ bhaviṣyasi |

p.6, l.1

yataḥ |

kautukānveṣiṇo nityaṃ durjanā vyasanāgame |(p.6, l.2)
 māsopavāsinī yadvad vaṇikputrakacagrahe || 1.8 (= 8) ||(p.6, l.3)

yataḥ |

kautukānveṣiṇo nityaṃ durjanā vyasanāgame | māsopavāsinī yadvad vaṇikputrakacagrahe || 1.8 (= 8) ||
papraccha sā tadā sārdhaṃ puṃścalībhiḥ kṛtādarā |(p.6, l.4)
 sasaṃbhramā jagādedaṃ kim idaṃ bhāṣitaṃ śuka || 1.9 (= 9) ||(p.6, l.5)
papraccha sā tadā sārdhaṃ puṃścalībhiḥ kṛtādarā | sasaṃbhramā jagādedaṃ kim idaṃ bhāṣitaṃ śuka || 1.9 (= 9) ||
yadi te kautukaṃ subhru parārthaṃ gaccha sundari |(p.6, l.6)
 sthirībhūya tvayā paścāt śrāvyeyaṃ mahatī kathā || 1.10 (= 10) ||(p.6, l.7)
yadi te kautukaṃ subhru parārthaṃ gaccha sundari | sthirībhūya tvayā paścāt śrāvyeyaṃ mahatī kathā || 1.10 (= 10) ||

p.6, l.7

evaṃ śukoktaṃ śrutvā yadā sā kautukākulacetasā nijagṛha āsīnāsti (p.6, l.8)
tadā śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti candrāvatī purī | tasyāṃ bhīmanāmā (p.6, l.9)
nṛpaḥ | tatra sudhano nāma mohanaśreṣṭhisutaḥ tannagaravāsino haridattasya (p.6, l.10)
kalatraṃ lakṣmīṃ rantum īhate | tadvat sā na manyate | tato māsopavāsinīṃ (p.6, l.11)
pūrṇābhidhānāṃ gatvā pūrṇadhanāvarjitāṃ kṛtvā haridatte nagarād bahir gate (p.6, l.12)
tadgṛhe dūtītvena preṣayām āsa | sāpi cāṭūktibhir lakṣmīṃ prasādayām āsa | (p.6, l.13)
prasannayā ca tayety uktam | yat tvaṃ yācase tat karomi | pūrṇayoktam | (p.7, l.1)
tarhi manmataṃ naraṃ bhaja | tayoktam | kulastrīṇāṃ naitad yujyate paraṃ yat tavāgre (p.7, l.2)
pratipannaṃ tat karomi | (p.7, l.3)

evaṃ śukoktaṃ śrutvā yadā sā kautukākulacetasā nijagṛha āsīnāsti tadā śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti candrāvatī purī | tasyāṃ bhīmanāmā nṛpaḥ | tatra sudhano nāma mohanaśreṣṭhisutaḥ tannagaravāsino haridattasya kalatraṃ lakṣmīṃ rantum īhate | tadvat sā na manyate | tato māsopavāsinīṃ pūrṇābhidhānāṃ gatvā pūrṇadhanāvarjitāṃ kṛtvā haridatte nagarād bahir gate tadgṛhe dūtītvena preṣayām āsa | sāpi cāṭūktibhir lakṣmīṃ prasādayām āsa | prasannayā ca tayety uktam | yat tvaṃ yācase tat karomi | pūrṇayoktam | tarhi manmataṃ naraṃ bhaja | tayoktam | kulastrīṇāṃ naitad yujyate paraṃ yat tavāgre pratipannaṃ tat karomi |

p.7, l.3

uktaṃ ca |

chijjaü sīsaṃ aha hou bandhaṇaṃ caaü savvahā lacchī |(p.7, l.4)
 paḍivaṇṇapālaṇe supurisāṇa jaṃ hou taṃ hou || 1.11 (= 11) ||

(•)

uktaṃ ca |

chijjaü sīsaṃ aha hou bandhaṇaṃ caaü savvahā lacchī | paḍivaṇṇapālaṇe supurisāṇa jaṃ hou taṃ hou || 1.11 (= 11) ||

(•)

tathā ca |

diḍhalohasiṅkhalāṇaṃ assāṇa vi vihapāsabandhāṇaṃ |(p.7, l.6)
 tāṇaṃ cia ahiaraaro vāābandho supurisassa || 1.12 (= 12) ||

(•)

tathā ca |

diḍhalohasiṅkhalāṇaṃ assāṇa vi vihapāsabandhāṇaṃ | tāṇaṃ cia ahiaraaro vāābandho supurisassa || 1.12 (= 12) ||

(•)

adyāpi nojjhati haraḥ kila kālakūṭaṃ(p.7, l.8)
kūrmo bibharti dharaṇīṃ khalu cātmapṛṣṭhe |(p.7, l.9)
 ambhonidhir vahati duḥsahavāḍavāgnim(p.7, l.10)
aṅgīkṛtaṃ sukṛtinaḥ paripālayanti || 1.13 (= 13) ||(p.7, l.11)
adyāpi nojjhati haraḥ kila kālakūṭaṃ kūrmo bibharti dharaṇīṃ khalu cātmapṛṣṭhe | ambhonidhir vahati duḥsahavāḍavāgnim aṅgīkṛtaṃ sukṛtinaḥ paripālayanti || 1.13 (= 13) ||

p.7, l.11

tac chrutvā hṛṣṭā pūrṇā | evam evaitat | tatas tāṃ lakṣmīṃ pratividhāya guṇamohanārthe (p.7, l.12)
pradoṣe svagṛhe nināya | tataḥ sa mohanaḥ kathitavelopari (p.7, l.13)
nāgataḥ kiṃcitkāryādivaiyagryeṇa | tato lakṣmyā sakāmayoktam | (p.8, l.1)
yat kam api naraṃ samānaya | tataḥ pūrṇayā mūḍhayā tatpatir eva samānītaḥ | (p.8, l.2)
svabhartari samāyāte sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti kathaṃ gṛhaṃ yātv iti tvaṃ sakhyas (p.8, l.3)
tava vā kathayantu | tā āhuḥ | na jānīmaḥ | tvam eva kathaya | śuka (p.8, l.4)
āha | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayoktam | na yāsyāmi | (p.8, l.5)
śukaḥ | sā āgacchann eva svapatir iti jñātvā taṃ kacagrahaṃ pragṛhyaivam uvāca | (p.8, l.6)
he śaṭha sarvadā tvam iti mamāgre jalpasi yan me tvāṃ vinā nānyā (p.8, l.7)
vallabhā asti | adhunā tu mayā parīkṣito jñātaś ceti kopaṃ cakre | (p.8, l.8)
sa ca tāṃ kaṣṭena sukomalavacanair anunīya svagṛhaṃ ninye | (p.8, l.9)

tac chrutvā hṛṣṭā pūrṇā | evam evaitat | tatas tāṃ lakṣmīṃ pratividhāya guṇamohanārthe pradoṣe svagṛhe nināya | tataḥ sa mohanaḥ kathitavelopari nāgataḥ kiṃcitkāryādivaiyagryeṇa | tato lakṣmyā sakāmayoktam | yat kam api naraṃ samānaya | tataḥ pūrṇayā mūḍhayā tatpatir eva samānītaḥ | svabhartari samāyāte sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti kathaṃ gṛhaṃ yātv iti tvaṃ sakhyas tava vā kathayantu | tā āhuḥ | na jānīmaḥ | tvam eva kathaya | śuka āha | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayoktam | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | sā āgacchann eva svapatir iti jñātvā taṃ kacagrahaṃ pragṛhyaivam uvāca | he śaṭha sarvadā tvam iti mamāgre jalpasi yan me tvāṃ vinā nānyā vallabhā asti | adhunā tu mayā parīkṣito jñātaś ceti kopaṃ cakre | sa ca tāṃ kaṣṭena sukomalavacanair anunīya svagṛhaṃ ninye |

p.8, l.9

kathāṃ śrutvā śukenoktāṃ bhayavismayakāriṇīm |(p.8, l.10)
 puṃścalīvṛndasaṃyuktā suptā rātrau vaṇikpriyā || 1.14 (= 14) ||(p.8, l.11)
kathāṃ śrutvā śukenoktāṃ bhayavismayakāriṇīm | puṃścalīvṛndasaṃyuktā suptā rātrau vaṇikpriyā || 1.14 (= 14) ||

§ 2

(p.9, l.1)

p.9, l.1

sā tathaiva samaṃ tābhir dvitīye 'hni niśāmukhe |(p.9, l.2)
 śukam āpṛcchya calitā śukas tām idam abravīt || 2.1 (= 15) ||(p.9, l.3)
sā tathaiva samaṃ tābhir dvitīye 'hni niśāmukhe | śukam āpṛcchya calitā śukas tām idam abravīt || 2.1 (= 15) ||
yatheṣṭaṃ gaccha suśroṇi yadi jānāsi duḥkṛte |(p.9, l.4)
 pratyuttaraṃ samāyāte yaśodevīva saṃkaṭe || 2.2 (= 16) ||(p.9, l.5)
yatheṣṭaṃ gaccha suśroṇi yadi jānāsi duḥkṛte | pratyuttaraṃ samāyāte yaśodevīva saṃkaṭe || 2.2 (= 16) ||

p.9, l.5

tataḥ prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kā yaśodevī | kadā kasmin saṃkaṭe tayā (p.9, l.6)
ka upāyaḥ kṛta iti | śukaḥ | yadā kathayāmi tadā mayi suratavighātena (p.9, l.7)
tava kopaḥ prāṇanisūdanaḥ syāt | sā āha | suhṛdāṃ sādhv (p.9, l.8)
asādhv api śrotavyam eva | ity anujñātaḥ śuka āha | asti nandanaṃ nāma (p.9, l.9)
nagaram | tatra nandano nāma rājā | tatputro rājaśekharaḥ | tadvadhūḥ (p.9, l.10)
śaśiprabhā | tāṃ dhanasenasuto vīranāmā dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ san jvarapīḍito (p.9, l.11)
'bhūt | bhojanādi na vidhatte | sa ca mātrā yaśodevyā pṛṣṭaḥ (p.9, l.12)
san sagadgadaṃ kāraṇam āha | sā ca rājakanyā durlabhā | sa kathaṃ jīvatu | (p.9, l.13)
iti praśnaḥ | tayoktam | tvam eva kathaya | śukaḥ | yadi prabhāvati adya (p.9, l.14)
na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | ity ukte sā āha | kathayeti | atha śukaḥ | (p.10, l.1)
sā yaśodevī ekāṃ śunīṃ bhojanādyair āvarjayitvā ābharaṇāni paridhāyātmanā (p.10, l.2)
sārdhaṃ gṛhītvā śaśiprabhāpārśve gatvā tāṃ vijane sagadgadā (p.10, l.3)
jagāda | ahaṃ ca tvaṃ ca iyaṃ ca pūrvabhave bhaginyo 'bhūvan | mayā (p.10, l.4)
niḥśaṅkayā tvayā tu saśaṅkayā paranarābhilāṣaḥ pūritaḥ | anayā tu (p.10, l.5)
naiva | ato 'syāḥ śīlaprabhāvāt kevalaṃ jātismaraṇam eva na bhogāḥ śunikā (p.10, l.6)
ca saṃjātā | saṃbhogavighnāj jātismaraṇaṃ ca na te vartate | mama (p.10, l.7)
punar bhogān nirvighnān nirvighnajātismaraṇaṃ ca | ato 'ham anukampayā imāṃ (p.10, l.8)
śunakīṃ tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kathayitum āgatā | atas tvayārthināṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ dātavyam (p.10, l.9)
eva | yo dānaṃ kuryāt sa bhavet sarvasaṃpadāṃ sthānam | (p.10, l.10)

tataḥ prabhāvatī pṛcchati | kā yaśodevī | kadā kasmin saṃkaṭe tayā ka upāyaḥ kṛta iti | śukaḥ | yadā kathayāmi tadā mayi suratavighātena tava kopaḥ prāṇanisūdanaḥ syāt | sā āha | suhṛdāṃ sādhv asādhv api śrotavyam eva | ity anujñātaḥ śuka āha | asti nandanaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra nandano nāma rājā | tatputro rājaśekharaḥ | tadvadhūḥ śaśiprabhā | tāṃ dhanasenasuto vīranāmā dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ san jvarapīḍito 'bhūt | bhojanādi na vidhatte | sa ca mātrā yaśodevyā pṛṣṭaḥ san sagadgadaṃ kāraṇam āha | sā ca rājakanyā durlabhā | sa kathaṃ jīvatu | iti praśnaḥ | tayoktam | tvam eva kathaya | śukaḥ | yadi prabhāvati adya na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | ity ukte sā āha | kathayeti | atha śukaḥ | sā yaśodevī ekāṃ śunīṃ bhojanādyair āvarjayitvā ābharaṇāni paridhāyātmanā sārdhaṃ gṛhītvā śaśiprabhāpārśve gatvā tāṃ vijane sagadgadā jagāda | ahaṃ ca tvaṃ ca iyaṃ ca pūrvabhave bhaginyo 'bhūvan | mayā niḥśaṅkayā tvayā tu saśaṅkayā paranarābhilāṣaḥ pūritaḥ | anayā tu naiva | ato 'syāḥ śīlaprabhāvāt kevalaṃ jātismaraṇam eva na bhogāḥ śunikā ca saṃjātā | saṃbhogavighnāj jātismaraṇaṃ ca na te vartate | mama punar bhogān nirvighnān nirvighnajātismaraṇaṃ ca | ato 'ham anukampayā imāṃ śunakīṃ tvāṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kathayitum āgatā | atas tvayārthināṃ kāṅkṣitaṃ dātavyam eva | yo dānaṃ kuryāt sa bhavet sarvasaṃpadāṃ sthānam |

p.10, l.10

uktaṃ ca |

kathayanti na yācante bhikṣāhārā gṛhe gṛhe |(p.10, l.11)
 arthibhyo dīyatāṃ nityam adātuḥ phalam īdṛśam || 2.3 (= 17) ||(p.10, l.12)

uktaṃ ca |

kathayanti na yācante bhikṣāhārā gṛhe gṛhe | arthibhyo dīyatāṃ nityam adātuḥ phalam īdṛśam || 2.3 (= 17) ||

p.10, l.12

tataḥ śaśiprabhā sakaṇṭhagrāhaṃ ruditvā prāha | mām api kalyāṇi puruṣāntareṇa (p.10, l.13)
yojaya | tato yaśodevī tāṃ svasthīkṛtya bhartṛviditāṃ svagṛhaṃ (p.10, l.14)
nītvā svaputreṇa yojayām āsa | sa ca rājaśekharo dravyādidānatoṣitaḥ (p.10, l.15)
sakhīyam iti kṛtvā na nivārayām āsa | (p.11, l.1)

tataḥ śaśiprabhā sakaṇṭhagrāhaṃ ruditvā prāha | mām api kalyāṇi puruṣāntareṇa yojaya | tato yaśodevī tāṃ svasthīkṛtya bhartṛviditāṃ svagṛhaṃ nītvā svaputreṇa yojayām āsa | sa ca rājaśekharo dravyādidānatoṣitaḥ sakhīyam iti kṛtvā na nivārayām āsa |

p.11, l.1

rājaputraṃ rājaputrīṃ pratāryaivaṃ ca bhāmini |(p.11, l.2)
 yaśodevyā mahadbuddhyā nijakāryam anuṣṭhitam || 2.4 (= 18) ||(p.11, l.3)
rājaputraṃ rājaputrīṃ pratāryaivaṃ ca bhāmini | yaśodevyā mahadbuddhyā nijakāryam anuṣṭhitam || 2.4 (= 18) ||
buddhir asti yadaiṣā te vraja subhru parāntikam |(p.11, l.4)
 bhaja nidrāṃ viśālākṣi mānyathā svaṃ viḍambaya || 2.5 (= 19) ||(p.11, l.5)
buddhir asti yadaiṣā te vraja subhru parāntikam | bhaja nidrāṃ viśālākṣi mānyathā svaṃ viḍambaya || 2.5 (= 19) ||

p.11, l.5

iti śukakathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || (p.11, l.6)
iti śukasaptatau dvitīyā kathā || (p.11, l.7)

iti śukakathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau dvitīyā kathā ||

§ 3

p.11, l.7

athānyadine prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.11, l.8)

athānyadine prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.11, l.8

gaccha devi kim āścaryaṃ yatra te ramate manaḥ |(p.11, l.9)
 nṛpavad yadi jānāsi paritrāṇaṃ tvam ātmanaḥ || 3.1 (= 20) ||(p.11, l.10)
gaccha devi kim āścaryaṃ yatra te ramate manaḥ | nṛpavad yadi jānāsi paritrāṇaṃ tvam ātmanaḥ || 3.1 (= 20) ||

p.11, l.10

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā (p.11, l.11)
nagarī | tatra sudarśano rājā | tatra ca vimalo nāma vaṇik | (p.11, l.12)
tasya ca patnīdvayaṃ subhagaṃ rūpasaṃpannaṃ dṛṣṭvā kuṭilanāmā dhūrtas tadbhāryādvayagrahaṇecchayā (p.11, l.13)
ambikāṃ devīm ārādhya vimalarūpaṃ yayāce | labdhvā (p.11, l.14)
ca tatprakṛtiṃ vimale bahir gate tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prabhutvaṃ cakāra | prasādadhanadānair (p.11, l.15)
vaśīkṛto 'khilo 'pi parijanavargaḥ | tadbhāryādvayaṃ bahumānadānādinā (p.12, l.1)
saṃtoṣya svecchayā bhuṅkte | vimalo 'yaṃ dhanādyanityatāṃ śrutvā (p.12, l.2)
dātā babhūveti parijano anavarataṃ cintayati | atha satyavimalo 'pi (p.12, l.3)
dvāram āgataḥ kuṭilājñayā dvārapālena niṣiddhaḥ | tato bahiḥsthaḥ phūtkaroti | (p.12, l.4)
vañcito 'haṃ dhūrtarājena | tasya caivaṃ krandato gotrajā janāḥ (p.12, l.5)
kautukāc ca militāḥ | tatkṣaṇāt haṭṭāni muktvā vaṇiksārtho militvā (p.12, l.6)
ārakṣikamantrimukhyānāṃ purataḥ phūccakre | rājan vañcito 'smi dhūrtarājena | (p.12, l.7)
tato rājñā tadavalokanāya prahitāḥ puruṣāḥ | tenāpi te dravyādidānena (p.12, l.8)
sānukūlāḥ kṛtāḥ | taṃ dhanadāyakaṃ gṛhe dṛṣṭvā jano vadati | (p.12, l.9)
svāmin vimalo gṛhe vidyate | ayaṃ ca dhūrtarāṭ dvārasthaḥ | tato nṛpeṇa (p.12, l.10)
dvāv apy ekatra kṛtau | tato dvayor madhyān na ko 'pi dhūrtetarayor vyaktiṃ jānāti | (p.12, l.11)
jātaḥ kolāhalo 'khilalokavyavahāranāśakaraḥ rājñaś cāpavādaḥ | (p.12, l.12)
yato rājñāṃ duṣṭanigrahaḥ śiṣṭapālanaṃ ca svargāya | (p.12, l.13)

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā nagarī | tatra sudarśano rājā | tatra ca vimalo nāma vaṇik | tasya ca patnīdvayaṃ subhagaṃ rūpasaṃpannaṃ dṛṣṭvā kuṭilanāmā dhūrtas tadbhāryādvayagrahaṇecchayā ambikāṃ devīm ārādhya vimalarūpaṃ yayāce | labdhvā ca tatprakṛtiṃ vimale bahir gate tadgṛhaṃ gatvā prabhutvaṃ cakāra | prasādadhanadānair vaśīkṛto 'khilo 'pi parijanavargaḥ | tadbhāryādvayaṃ bahumānadānādinā saṃtoṣya svecchayā bhuṅkte | vimalo 'yaṃ dhanādyanityatāṃ śrutvā dātā babhūveti parijano anavarataṃ cintayati | atha satyavimalo 'pi dvāram āgataḥ kuṭilājñayā dvārapālena niṣiddhaḥ | tato bahiḥsthaḥ phūtkaroti | vañcito 'haṃ dhūrtarājena | tasya caivaṃ krandato gotrajā janāḥ kautukāc ca militāḥ | tatkṣaṇāt haṭṭāni muktvā vaṇiksārtho militvā ārakṣikamantrimukhyānāṃ purataḥ phūccakre | rājan vañcito 'smi dhūrtarājena | tato rājñā tadavalokanāya prahitāḥ puruṣāḥ | tenāpi te dravyādidānena sānukūlāḥ kṛtāḥ | taṃ dhanadāyakaṃ gṛhe dṛṣṭvā jano vadati | svāmin vimalo gṛhe vidyate | ayaṃ ca dhūrtarāṭ dvārasthaḥ | tato nṛpeṇa dvāv apy ekatra kṛtau | tato dvayor madhyān na ko 'pi dhūrtetarayor vyaktiṃ jānāti | jātaḥ kolāhalo 'khilalokavyavahāranāśakaraḥ rājñaś cāpavādaḥ | yato rājñāṃ duṣṭanigrahaḥ śiṣṭapālanaṃ ca svargāya |

p.12, l.13

uktaṃ ca |

prajāpīḍanasaṃtāpāt samudbhūto hutāśanaḥ |(p.13, l.1)
 rājñaḥ kulaṃ śriyaṃ prāṇān nādagdhvā vinivartate || 3.2 (= 21) ||(p.13, l.2)

uktaṃ ca |

prajāpīḍanasaṃtāpāt samudbhūto hutāśanaḥ | rājñaḥ kulaṃ śriyaṃ prāṇān nādagdhvā vinivartate || 3.2 (= 21) ||

p.13, l.2

tato rājā ekānte tayor nirṇayam acintayat | tat kathaya kathaṃ niścayaḥ (p.13, l.3)
syād iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | sa rājā labdhopāyas tadvimalabhāryādvayaṃ pṛthak (p.13, l.4)
pṛthak saṃsthāpya pṛṣṭavān | kiṃ yuvayoḥ pāṇigrahaṇe bhartrā vibhūṣaṇaṃ pradattaṃ (p.13, l.5)
dhanaṃ ca | paścāt kiṃ jalpitaṃ prathamasaṅge ca kā vārttā bhartrā sahābhūt | (p.13, l.6)
kā mātā kaś ca pitā | kiṃ kulam | kā jātiḥ | ity evaṃ pṛṣṭābhyāṃ (p.13, l.7)
yathālabdhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāproktaṃ yathāsuptaṃ sarvaṃ tābhyāṃ kathitam | paścāt tu (p.13, l.8)
tau puruṣau pṛṣṭau parasparaṃ visaṃvadantau | tato bhāryādvayasya rukmiṇīsundarīnāmadheyasya (p.13, l.9)
yaḥ saṃvādaṃ vadati sa satyaḥ | itaras tu dhūrto rājñā (p.13, l.10)
nirvāsitaḥ | satyas tu rājñā sabhāryaḥ satkṛtaḥ svagṛhaṃ gataḥ | iti mahārājabuddhiḥ | (p.13, l.11)
iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || (p.13, l.12)
iti śukasaptatau tṛtīyā kathā ||

tato rājā ekānte tayor nirṇayam acintayat | tat kathaya kathaṃ niścayaḥ syād iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | sa rājā labdhopāyas tadvimalabhāryādvayaṃ pṛthak pṛthak saṃsthāpya pṛṣṭavān | kiṃ yuvayoḥ pāṇigrahaṇe bhartrā vibhūṣaṇaṃ pradattaṃ dhanaṃ ca | paścāt kiṃ jalpitaṃ prathamasaṅge ca kā vārttā bhartrā sahābhūt | kā mātā kaś ca pitā | kiṃ kulam | kā jātiḥ | ity evaṃ pṛṣṭābhyāṃ yathālabdhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāproktaṃ yathāsuptaṃ sarvaṃ tābhyāṃ kathitam | paścāt tu tau puruṣau pṛṣṭau parasparaṃ visaṃvadantau | tato bhāryādvayasya rukmiṇīsundarīnāmadheyasya yaḥ saṃvādaṃ vadati sa satyaḥ | itaras tu dhūrto rājñā nirvāsitaḥ | satyas tu rājñā sabhāryaḥ satkṛtaḥ svagṛhaṃ gataḥ | iti mahārājabuddhiḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau tṛtīyā kathā ||

§ 4

(p.14, l.1)

p.14, l.1

athānyadā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | māṃ kṛtāvajñaṃ kṛtvā mā (p.14, l.2)
gaccha | yato bālakād api hitaṃ vākyaṃ grāhyam | (p.14, l.3)

athānyadā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | māṃ kṛtāvajñaṃ kṛtvā mā gaccha | yato bālakād api hitaṃ vākyaṃ grāhyam |

p.14, l.3

kṛtāvajñaḥ purā devi vṛddhavākyaparāṅmukhaḥ |(p.14, l.4)
 patito brāhmaṇo 'narthe viṣakanyāvivāhane || 4.1 (= 22) ||(p.14, l.5)
kṛtāvajñaḥ purā devi vṛddhavākyaparāṅmukhaḥ | patito brāhmaṇo 'narthe viṣakanyāvivāhane || 4.1 (= 22) ||

p.14, l.5

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti somaprabhaṃ nāma dvijasthānam | (p.14, l.6)
tatra vidvān dhārmikaḥ somaśarmā nāma vipraḥ | tatputrī rūpaudāryaguṇopetā (p.14, l.7)
viṣakanyeti vijñātābhūt | tena tāṃ bhayena ko 'pi na (p.14, l.8)
vivāhayati | tataḥ somaśarmā varārthaṃ bhuvaṃ paryaṭan saṃprāpto dvijasthānaṃ (p.14, l.9)
janasthānaṃ nāma | tatra govindanāmā brāhmaṇo jaḍo nirdhanaś ca | tasmai (p.14, l.10)
kanyā pradattā | tena suhṛdāṃ nivārayatām api kṛtāvajñenoḍhā sarvarūpalāvaṇyaguṇopetā (p.14, l.11)
mohinī viṣakanyā | sā vidagdhā govindas tu mūrkhaḥ (p.14, l.12)
laghuvayāś ca | tataś ca sā ātmano rūpalāvaṇyayauvanaṃ śuśoca | (p.14, l.13)

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti somaprabhaṃ nāma dvijasthānam | tatra vidvān dhārmikaḥ somaśarmā nāma vipraḥ | tatputrī rūpaudāryaguṇopetā viṣakanyeti vijñātābhūt | tena tāṃ bhayena ko 'pi na vivāhayati | tataḥ somaśarmā varārthaṃ bhuvaṃ paryaṭan saṃprāpto dvijasthānaṃ janasthānaṃ nāma | tatra govindanāmā brāhmaṇo jaḍo nirdhanaś ca | tasmai kanyā pradattā | tena suhṛdāṃ nivārayatām api kṛtāvajñenoḍhā sarvarūpalāvaṇyaguṇopetā mohinī viṣakanyā | sā vidagdhā govindas tu mūrkhaḥ laghuvayāś ca | tataś ca sā ātmano rūpalāvaṇyayauvanaṃ śuśoca |

p.14, l.13

avidagdhaḥ patiḥ strīṇāṃ prauḍhāṇāṃ nāyako 'guṇī |(p.14, l.14)
 guṇināṃ tyāgināṃ stoko vibhavaś ceti duḥkhakṛt || 4.2 (= 23) ||(p.15, l.1)
avidagdhaḥ patiḥ strīṇāṃ prauḍhāṇāṃ nāyako 'guṇī | guṇināṃ tyāgināṃ stoko vibhavaś ceti duḥkhakṛt || 4.2 (= 23) ||
pāusasamaapavāso jovvaṇadiahe tahā a dāliddaṃ |(p.15, l.2)
 paḍhamasiṇehavioo tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.3 (= 24) ||

(•)

 mā mā bhaṇantisuraaṃ tiṇṇi vi garuāi dukkhāiṃ || 4.4 (= 25) ||

p.15, l.5

sānyadā govindaṃ patim ity abravīt | mama pitur gehāt samāgatāyā bahūni (p.15, l.6)
dināni saṃjātāni | tato 'haṃ tvayaiva saha gamiṣye nānyathā | tataḥ (p.15, l.7)
śakaṭaṃ mārgayitvā sabhāryakaḥ sa calitaḥ | yāvat prayāti tāvat pathi (p.16, l.1)
eko yuvā vāgmī surūpaḥ śūraś ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo militaḥ | (p.16, l.2)
tasya brāhmaṇasya tasyāś cānyonyam anurāgaḥ saṃjātaḥ | (p.16, l.3)

sānyadā govindaṃ patim ity abravīt | mama pitur gehāt samāgatāyā bahūni dināni saṃjātāni | tato 'haṃ tvayaiva saha gamiṣye nānyathā | tataḥ śakaṭaṃ mārgayitvā sabhāryakaḥ sa calitaḥ | yāvat prayāti tāvat pathi eko yuvā vāgmī surūpaḥ śūraś ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo militaḥ | tasya brāhmaṇasya tasyāś cānyonyam anurāgaḥ saṃjātaḥ |

p.16, l.3

uktaṃ ca |

prītiḥ syād darśanādyaiḥ prathamam atha manaḥsaṅgasaṃkalpabhāvo(p.16, l.4)
nidrācchedas tanutvaṃ vapuṣi kaluṣatā cendriyāṇāṃ nivṛttiḥ |(p.16, l.5)
 hrīnāśonmādamūrcchāmaraṇam iti jagad yāty avasthā daśaitāḥ(p.16, l.6)
lagnair yat puṣpabāṇaiḥ sa jayati madanaḥ saṃnirastānyadhanvī || 4.5 (= 26) ||(p.16, l.7)

uktaṃ ca |

prītiḥ syād darśanādyaiḥ prathamam atha manaḥsaṅgasaṃkalpabhāvo nidrācchedas tanutvaṃ vapuṣi kaluṣatā cendriyāṇāṃ nivṛttiḥ | hrīnāśonmādamūrcchāmaraṇam iti jagad yāty avasthā daśaitāḥ lagnair yat puṣpabāṇaiḥ sa jayati madanaḥ saṃnirastānyadhanvī || 4.5 (= 26) ||

p.16, l.7

sa pathiko dampatyoḥ pūgapattroccayaṃ dadāti | ity evaṃ grāmyabrāhmaṇo viṣṇor (p.16, l.8)
viśvastaḥ ātmano nirodhasaṅgabhayād uttīrya (?) taṃ gantrīvāham ārohayati | (p.16, l.9)
viṣṇunā ca patyau vṛkṣāntaragate sā mohinī bhuktā ātmavaśīkṛtā | (p.16, l.10)
tayā cātmīyaṃ nāma gotraṃ kulakramaṃ cājñāpitaḥ | patyuś ca samāgatasya (p.16, l.11)
tvaṃ cauro 'sīti gantryārohaṇaṃ kurvato niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ | viṣṇur api tāṃ (p.16, l.12)
gṛhītvā govindaṃ dharṣitavān | tatas tayoḥ keśākeśi saṃvṛttam | (p.17, l.1)
govindas tu viṣṇunā viṣakanyāprabhāveṇa nirjitaḥ | tatas tāṃ gṛhītvā (p.17, l.2)
viṣṇuḥ svagṛhaṃ praticalitaḥ | govindaḥ pṛṣṭhastho mārgāsanne grāme gatvā (p.17, l.3)
phūtkṛtavān | yad anena caureṇa mama bhāryā gṛhītā | trāyatāṃ tām | mama (p.17, l.4)
śaraṇaṃ bho janāḥ | atha grāmādhipena viṣṇur mohinīyuto dhṛtaḥ | pṛṣṭenottaraṃ (p.17, l.5)
dattaṃ viṣṇunā yatheyaṃ mayā pariṇītā | madīyāṃ ca bhāryām eṣa (p.17, l.6)
pathiko mārge dṛṣṭvā grahilo babhūva | govindenāpi pṛṣṭena idam evottaritam | (p.17, l.7)
tato mantrī tayor ekam evottaraṃ śrutvā jātyādikaṃ pṛṣṭavān | (p.17, l.8)
trayam api tu saṃvadati tataḥ kathaṃ niścayaḥ | (p.17, l.9)
iti śukapraśnaḥ | tatas tayā (p.17, l.10)
pṛṣṭaḥ śuka āha | mantriṇoktam | kiyanti dināni saṃgamasya yuṣmākaṃ (p.17, l.11)
prayāṇe | tair uktam | kalye bhojanāntaraṃ saṃvṛttaḥ samāgamaḥ | tato (p.17, l.12)
mantriṇā brāhmaṇau pṛthak pṛthak pṛṣṭau | kim anayā kalye bhojanavelāyāṃ (p.17, l.13)
bhuktam | yac ca tayā bhuktaṃ tad govindo jānāti itaras tu na | tataḥ sa (p.17, l.14)
viḍambitaḥ sacivena | govindaḥ śikṣitaḥ | dhig imāṃ brāhmaṇīṃ paratreha (p.17, l.15)
ca duḥkhadāṃ muñca śīghram | (p.18, l.1)

sa pathiko dampatyoḥ pūgapattroccayaṃ dadāti | ity evaṃ grāmyabrāhmaṇo viṣṇor viśvastaḥ ātmano nirodhasaṅgabhayād uttīrya (?) taṃ gantrīvāham ārohayati | viṣṇunā ca patyau vṛkṣāntaragate sā mohinī bhuktā ātmavaśīkṛtā | tayā cātmīyaṃ nāma gotraṃ kulakramaṃ cājñāpitaḥ | patyuś ca samāgatasya tvaṃ cauro 'sīti gantryārohaṇaṃ kurvato niṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ | viṣṇur api tāṃ gṛhītvā govindaṃ dharṣitavān | tatas tayoḥ keśākeśi saṃvṛttam | govindas tu viṣṇunā viṣakanyāprabhāveṇa nirjitaḥ | tatas tāṃ gṛhītvā viṣṇuḥ svagṛhaṃ praticalitaḥ | govindaḥ pṛṣṭhastho mārgāsanne grāme gatvā phūtkṛtavān | yad anena caureṇa mama bhāryā gṛhītā | trāyatāṃ tām | mama śaraṇaṃ bho janāḥ | atha grāmādhipena viṣṇur mohinīyuto dhṛtaḥ | pṛṣṭenottaraṃ dattaṃ viṣṇunā yatheyaṃ mayā pariṇītā | madīyāṃ ca bhāryām eṣa pathiko mārge dṛṣṭvā grahilo babhūva | govindenāpi pṛṣṭena idam evottaritam | tato mantrī tayor ekam evottaraṃ śrutvā jātyādikaṃ pṛṣṭavān | trayam api tu saṃvadati tataḥ kathaṃ niścayaḥ | iti śukapraśnaḥ | tatas tayā pṛṣṭaḥ śuka āha | mantriṇoktam | kiyanti dināni saṃgamasya yuṣmākaṃ prayāṇe | tair uktam | kalye bhojanāntaraṃ saṃvṛttaḥ samāgamaḥ | tato mantriṇā brāhmaṇau pṛthak pṛthak pṛṣṭau | kim anayā kalye bhojanavelāyāṃ bhuktam | yac ca tayā bhuktaṃ tad govindo jānāti itaras tu na | tataḥ sa viḍambitaḥ sacivena | govindaḥ śikṣitaḥ | dhig imāṃ brāhmaṇīṃ paratreha ca duḥkhadāṃ muñca śīghram |

p.18, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

vaidyaṃ pānarataṃ naṭaṃ kupaṭhitaṃ mūrkhaṃ parivrājakaṃ(p.18, l.2)
yodhaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ viṭaṃ vivayasaṃ svādhyāyahīnaṃ dvijam |(p.18, l.3)
 rājyaṃ bālanarendramantrirahitaṃ mitraṃ chalānveṣi ca(p.18, l.4)
bhāryāṃ yauvanagarvitāṃ pararatāṃ muñcanti ye paṇḍitāḥ || 4.6 (= 27) ||(p.18, l.5)

uktaṃ ca |

vaidyaṃ pānarataṃ naṭaṃ kupaṭhitaṃ mūrkhaṃ parivrājakaṃ yodhaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ viṭaṃ vivayasaṃ svādhyāyahīnaṃ dvijam | rājyaṃ bālanarendramantrirahitaṃ mitraṃ chalānveṣi ca bhāryāṃ yauvanagarvitāṃ pararatāṃ muñcanti ye paṇḍitāḥ || 4.6 (= 27) ||
tathāpi kāminīlubdho dhikkṛtaḥ sādhubhis tadā |(p.18, l.6)
 tām evādāya calitas tatkṛte nihataḥ pathi || 4.7 (= 28) ||(p.18, l.7)
tathāpi kāminīlubdho dhikkṛtaḥ sādhubhis tadā | tām evādāya calitas tatkṛte nihataḥ pathi || 4.7 (= 28) ||
tad devi yaḥ karoty evam avajñāṃ vṛddhaśikṣitaḥ |(p.18, l.8)
 sa parābhavam āpnoti govindo brāhmaṇo yathā || 4.8 (= 29) ||(p.18, l.9)
tad devi yaḥ karoty evam avajñāṃ vṛddhaśikṣitaḥ | sa parābhavam āpnoti govindo brāhmaṇo yathā || 4.8 (= 29) ||

p.18, l.9

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || (p.18, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau caturthī kathā || (p.18, l.11)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau caturthī kathā ||

p.18, l.11

punar anyadine sā gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.18, l.12)

punar anyadine sā gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.18, l.12

gaccha devi vijānāsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram |(p.18, l.13)
 sabhāyāṃ nṛpater yadvad viṣame bālapaṇḍitā || 5.1 (= 30) ||(p.19, l.1)
gaccha devi vijānāsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram | sabhāyāṃ nṛpater yadvad viṣame bālapaṇḍitā || 5.1 (= 30) ||

p.19, l.1

prabhāvatīpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti ujjayinī nāma nagarī | (p.19, l.2)
tatra vikramādityo rājā | tasya rājñī kāmalīlā nāma uttamakulajātā | (p.19, l.3)
sā ca rājño 'tīva vallabhā | ekadā nṛpas tayā sārdhaṃ bhojanaṃ (p.19, l.4)
kurvan bhṛṣṭamatsyāṃs tasyai dāpayām āsa | sā āha | svāmin nāham etān puruṣān (p.19, l.5)
avalokayitum api samarthā kiṃ punaḥ sparśanam | iti śrutvā tena (p.19, l.6)
matsyā aṭṭāṭṭahāsena tathā jahasur yathā nāgarikalokena śrutam | rājā (p.19, l.7)
ca tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ mantrijyotirvicchākunikakovidān pṛcchati | yadā (p.19, l.8)
na ko 'pi jānāti tadā sarvadvijāgresaraṃ purohitaṃ prāha yathā tvayaiva (p.19, l.9)
matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ kathanīyam anyathā tvaṃ deśān nirvāsaṃ prāpnoṣi | purodhāpy etad (p.19, l.10)
vacaḥ śrutvā dinapañcakaṃ vyavadhāne yācayitvā saviṣādo gṛham āgamat | (p.19, l.11)
sa purohitaḥ tad uttaram ajānan purastād rājñā nirvāsyate | sa kathaṃ bhavatv (p.19, l.12)
iti praśnaḥ | uttaram apy āha śukaḥ | sa brāhmaṇo viṣādāpannaḥ putryā (p.19, l.13)
bālapaṇḍitayā babhāṣe | tāta katham udvignacitta iva lakṣyase | kathaya (p.19, l.14)
viṣādasya kāraṇam | vidvadbhir vipady apy uccaiḥ sthātavyam | (p.20, l.1)

prabhāvatīpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti ujjayinī nāma nagarī | tatra vikramādityo rājā | tasya rājñī kāmalīlā nāma uttamakulajātā | sā ca rājño 'tīva vallabhā | ekadā nṛpas tayā sārdhaṃ bhojanaṃ kurvan bhṛṣṭamatsyāṃs tasyai dāpayām āsa | sā āha | svāmin nāham etān puruṣān avalokayitum api samarthā kiṃ punaḥ sparśanam | iti śrutvā tena matsyā aṭṭāṭṭahāsena tathā jahasur yathā nāgarikalokena śrutam | rājā ca tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ mantrijyotirvicchākunikakovidān pṛcchati | yadā na ko 'pi jānāti tadā sarvadvijāgresaraṃ purohitaṃ prāha yathā tvayaiva matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ kathanīyam anyathā tvaṃ deśān nirvāsaṃ prāpnoṣi | purodhāpy etad vacaḥ śrutvā dinapañcakaṃ vyavadhāne yācayitvā saviṣādo gṛham āgamat | sa purohitaḥ tad uttaram ajānan purastād rājñā nirvāsyate | sa kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | uttaram apy āha śukaḥ | sa brāhmaṇo viṣādāpannaḥ putryā bālapaṇḍitayā babhāṣe | tāta katham udvignacitta iva lakṣyase | kathaya viṣādasya kāraṇam | vidvadbhir vipady apy uccaiḥ sthātavyam |

p.20, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

saṃpadi yasya na harṣo vipadi viṣādo raṇe ca dhīratvam |(p.20, l.2)
 taṃ bhuvanatrayatilakaṃ jananī janayati sutaṃ viralam || 5.2 (= 31) ||(p.20, l.3)

uktaṃ ca |

saṃpadi yasya na harṣo vipadi viṣādo raṇe ca dhīratvam | taṃ bhuvanatrayatilakaṃ jananī janayati sutaṃ viralam || 5.2 (= 31) ||

p.20, l.3

tato brāhmaṇo 'viralaṃ vṛttāntam ācaṣṭe | anena kāraṇena rājā māṃ (p.20, l.4)
nagarān nirvāsayati | (p.20, l.5)

tato brāhmaṇo 'viralaṃ vṛttāntam ācaṣṭe | anena kāraṇena rājā māṃ nagarān nirvāsayati |

p.20, l.5

yataḥ |

na sauhṛdaṃ na viśvāso na sneho na ca bandhutā |(p.20, l.6)
 kenāpi saha saṃsāre kuto rājñā chalārthinā || 5.3 (= 32) ||(p.20, l.7)

yataḥ |

na sauhṛdaṃ na viśvāso na sneho na ca bandhutā | kenāpi saha saṃsāre kuto rājñā chalārthinā || 5.3 (= 32) ||

uktaṃ ca |

kāke śaucaṃ dyūtakāre ca satyaṃ sarpe kṣāntiḥ strīṣu kāmopaśāntiḥ |(p.20, l.8)
 klībe dhairyaṃ madyape tattvacintā rājā mitraṃ kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā || 5.4 (= 33) ||(p.20, l.9)

uktaṃ ca |

kāke śaucaṃ dyūtakāre ca satyaṃ sarpe kṣāntiḥ strīṣu kāmopaśāntiḥ | klībe dhairyaṃ madyape tattvacintā rājā mitraṃ kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā || 5.4 (= 33) ||

kiṃ ca |

nadīnāṃ nakhināṃ caiva śṛṅgiṇāṃ śastrapāṇinām |(p.20, l.10)
 viśvāso naiva kartavyaḥ strīṣu rājakuleṣu ca || 5.5 (= 34) ||(p.20, l.11)

kiṃ ca |

nadīnāṃ nakhināṃ caiva śṛṅgiṇāṃ śastrapāṇinām | viśvāso naiva kartavyaḥ strīṣu rājakuleṣu ca || 5.5 (= 34) ||
bhoginaḥ kañcukāsaktāḥ krūrāḥ kuṭilagaminaḥ |(p.20, l.12)
 duḥkhopasarpaṇīyāś ca rājāno bhujagā iva || 5.6 (= 35) ||(p.20, l.13)
bhoginaḥ kañcukāsaktāḥ krūrāḥ kuṭilagaminaḥ | duḥkhopasarpaṇīyāś ca rājāno bhujagā iva || 5.6 (= 35) ||
hasann api nṛpo hanti mānayann api durjanaḥ |(p.21, l.1)
 spṛśann api gajo hanti jighrann api bhujaṅgamaḥ || 5.7 (= 36) ||(p.21, l.2)
hasann api nṛpo hanti mānayann api durjanaḥ | spṛśann api gajo hanti jighrann api bhujaṅgamaḥ || 5.7 (= 36) ||

p.21, l.2

eṣa rājā ā bālyāt sevito 'pi mayi viparīto babhūva | tasmān mayā (p.21, l.3)
jīvitum icchatā dvijaiḥ saha paradeśaṃ gantavyam | (p.21, l.4)

eṣa rājā ā bālyāt sevito 'pi mayi viparīto babhūva | tasmān mayā jīvitum icchatā dvijaiḥ saha paradeśaṃ gantavyam |

p.21, l.4

tyajed ekaṃ kulasyārthe grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet |(p.21, l.5)
 grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet || 5.8 (= 37) ||(p.21, l.6)

uktaṃ ca |

tyajed ekaṃ kulasyārthe grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet | grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet || 5.8 (= 37) ||

p.21, l.6

tataḥ sā bālikā tātavacanaṃ śrutvā prāha | tāta tvayā yuktam uktam | (p.21, l.7)
paraṃ svāmirahitānāṃ na kvāpi pūjā | (p.21, l.8)

tataḥ sā bālikā tātavacanaṃ śrutvā prāha | tāta tvayā yuktam uktam | paraṃ svāmirahitānāṃ na kvāpi pūjā |

p.21, l.8

yata uktam |

apradhānaḥ pradhānaḥ syād yadi seveta pārthivam |(p.21, l.10)
 pradhāno 'py apradhānaḥ syād yadi sevāvivarjitaḥ || 5.9 (= 38) ||(p.21, l.11)

yata uktam |

apradhānaḥ pradhānaḥ syād yadi seveta pārthivam | pradhāno 'py apradhānaḥ syād yadi sevāvivarjitaḥ || 5.9 (= 38) ||
āsannam eva nṛpatir bhajate manuṣyaṃ(p.21, l.12)
vidyāvihīnam akulīnam asaṃstutaṃ vā |(p.21, l.13)
 prāyeṇa bhūmipatayaḥ pramadā latāś ca(p.21, l.14)
yaḥ pārśvato bhavati taṃ pariveṣṭayanti || 5.10 (= 39) ||(p.21, l.15)
āsannam eva nṛpatir bhajate manuṣyaṃ vidyāvihīnam akulīnam asaṃstutaṃ vā | prāyeṇa bhūmipatayaḥ pramadā latāś ca yaḥ pārśvato bhavati taṃ pariveṣṭayanti || 5.10 (= 39) ||
ārohanti śanair bhṛtyā dhunvantam api pārthivam |(p.21, l.16)
 kopaprasādavastūnāṃ vicinvanti samīpagāḥ || 5.11 (= 40) ||(p.22, l.1)
ārohanti śanair bhṛtyā dhunvantam api pārthivam | kopaprasādavastūnāṃ vicinvanti samīpagāḥ || 5.11 (= 40) ||

p.22, l.1

tathā ca |

vidyāvatāṃ mahecchānāṃ śilpavikramaśālinām |(p.22, l.2)
 sevāvṛttividāṃ caiva nāśrayaḥ pārthivaṃ vinā || 5.12 (= 41) ||(p.22, l.3)

tathā ca |

vidyāvatāṃ mahecchānāṃ śilpavikramaśālinām | sevāvṛttividāṃ caiva nāśrayaḥ pārthivaṃ vinā || 5.12 (= 41) ||
ye jātyādimahotsāhā nopagacchanti pārthivam |(p.22, l.4)
 teṣām āmaraṇaṃ bhikṣā prāyaś cittaṃ vinirmitam || 5.13 (= 42) ||(p.22, l.5)
ye jātyādimahotsāhā nopagacchanti pārthivam | teṣām āmaraṇaṃ bhikṣā prāyaś cittaṃ vinirmitam || 5.13 (= 42) ||
rogair grahair nṛpair grasto yo na vetti jaḍakriyaḥ |(p.22, l.6)
 madhyamantram upāyaṃ ca so 'vaśyaṃ tāta na sthiraḥ || 5.14 (= 43) ||(p.22, l.7)
rogair grahair nṛpair grasto yo na vetti jaḍakriyaḥ | madhyamantram upāyaṃ ca so 'vaśyaṃ tāta na sthiraḥ || 5.14 (= 43) ||

uktaṃ ca |

sarpān vyāghrān gajān siṃhān dṛṣṭvopāyair vaśīkṛtān |(p.22, l.8)
 rājeti kiyatī mātrā dhīmatām apramādinām || 5.15 (= 44) ||(p.22, l.9)

uktaṃ ca |

sarpān vyāghrān gajān siṃhān dṛṣṭvopāyair vaśīkṛtān | rājeti kiyatī mātrā dhīmatām apramādinām || 5.15 (= 44) ||

tathā ca |

rājānam eva saṃśritya vidvān yāti paronnatim |(p.22, l.10)
 vinā malayam anyatra candanaṃ na vivardhate || 5.16 (= 45) ||(p.22, l.11)

tathā ca |

rājānam eva saṃśritya vidvān yāti paronnatim | vinā malayam anyatra candanaṃ na vivardhate || 5.16 (= 45) ||
dhavalāny ātapatrāṇi vājinaś ca manoramāḥ |(p.22, l.12)
 sadā mattāś ca mātaṅgāḥ prasanne sati bhūpatau || 5.17 (= 46) ||(p.22, l.13)
dhavalāny ātapatrāṇi vājinaś ca manoramāḥ | sadā mattāś ca mātaṅgāḥ prasanne sati bhūpatau || 5.17 (= 46) ||

p.22, l.13

tasmāt tāta tvaṃ rājñā mānyaḥ prasādapātraṃ ca | tataḥ saṃdehe 'smin mā (p.22, l.14)
viṣādībhava | (p.22, l.15)

p.22, l.15

yataḥ |

rājagrahe samāyāte viṣame kāryasaṃśaye |(p.23, l.1)
 saṃdigdhamanasāṃ rājñāṃ pradhānāḥ saṃśayacchidaḥ || 5.18 (= 47) ||(p.23, l.2)

yataḥ |

rājagrahe samāyāte viṣame kāryasaṃśaye | saṃdigdhamanasāṃ rājñāṃ pradhānāḥ saṃśayacchidaḥ || 5.18 (= 47) ||

p.23, l.2

tato he tāta sthirībhava | matsyahasanottaraṃ rājñaḥ purato mayābhidheyam (p.23, l.3)
iti | snāhi bhuṅkṣva | tataḥ sa evaṃ kṛtvā rājño 'grato gatvā sarvaṃ (p.23, l.4)
nivedayām āsa | nṛpo 'pi tuṣṭas tām ājuhāva | sā āśīrvādaṃ dattvā (p.23, l.5)
rājānam abravīt | rājan mā mudhā viprān viḍambaya | kiṃ tvayā evaṃvidhaṃ (p.23, l.6)
matsyānāṃ hāsyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā | kathaṃ mām abalājanaṃ pṛcchan na vilajjase | (p.23, l.7)

tato he tāta sthirībhava | matsyahasanottaraṃ rājñaḥ purato mayābhidheyam iti | snāhi bhuṅkṣva | tataḥ sa evaṃ kṛtvā rājño 'grato gatvā sarvaṃ nivedayām āsa | nṛpo 'pi tuṣṭas tām ājuhāva | sā āśīrvādaṃ dattvā rājānam abravīt | rājan mā mudhā viprān viḍambaya | kiṃ tvayā evaṃvidhaṃ matsyānāṃ hāsyaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā | kathaṃ mām abalājanaṃ pṛcchan na vilajjase |

p.23, l.7

yataḥ |

itaro 'pi na sāmānyo nṛpatir divyarūpabhṛt |(p.23, l.8)
 tvaṃ punar vikramādityo yathārtho 'si paraṃtapa || 5.19 (= 48) ||(p.23, l.9)

yataḥ |

itaro 'pi na sāmānyo nṛpatir divyarūpabhṛt | tvaṃ punar vikramādityo yathārtho 'si paraṃtapa || 5.19 (= 48) ||

uktaṃ ca |

indrāt prabhutvaṃ jvalanāt pratāpaṃ krodhaṃ yamād vaiśravaṇāc ca vittam |(p.23, l.10)
 sattvasthire rāmajanārdanābhyām ādāya rājñaḥ kriyate śarīram || 5.20 (= 49) ||(p.23, l.11)

uktaṃ ca |

indrāt prabhutvaṃ jvalanāt pratāpaṃ krodhaṃ yamād vaiśravaṇāc ca vittam | sattvasthire rāmajanārdanābhyām ādāya rājñaḥ kriyate śarīram || 5.20 (= 49) ||

p.23, l.11

tathā ca bhārate |

mā vṛkodara pādena ekādaśacamūpatim |(p.23, l.13)
 pañcānām api yo bharttā nāsāprakṛtimāninī (?) || 5.21 (= 50) ||(p.23, l.14)

tathā ca bhārate |

mā vṛkodara pādena ekādaśacamūpatim | pañcānām api yo bharttā nāsāprakṛtimāninī (?) || 5.21 (= 50) ||

p.23, l.14

svāmin kathaṃ na tvaṃ svayam eva vicārayasi | yatas tvam eva sarvasaṃśayacchettā | (p.23, l.15)
athānyebhyaś cet śrotuṃ kautukaṃ tarhi śṛṇu | (p.24, l.1)

svāmin kathaṃ na tvaṃ svayam eva vicārayasi | yatas tvam eva sarvasaṃśayacchettā | athānyebhyaś cet śrotuṃ kautukaṃ tarhi śṛṇu |

p.24, l.1

iyaṃ rājñī na spṛśati hy asmān matsyān mahāsatī |(p.24, l.2)
 puruṣākhyān ato rājan hasitāḥ śapharā dhruvam || 5.22 (= 51) ||(p.24, l.3)
iyaṃ rājñī na spṛśati hy asmān matsyān mahāsatī | puruṣākhyān ato rājan hasitāḥ śapharā dhruvam || 5.22 (= 51) ||
paribhāvyas tvayā rājan ślokārtho 'yaṃ sadā hṛdi |(p.24, l.4)
 mūḍhadhīr anyathā deva yadi pṛcchasi māṃ punaḥ || 5.23 (= 52) ||(p.24, l.5)
paribhāvyas tvayā rājan ślokārtho 'yaṃ sadā hṛdi | mūḍhadhīr anyathā deva yadi pṛcchasi māṃ punaḥ || 5.23 (= 52) ||

p.24, l.5

rājan rājapatnyāḥ sūryam apaśyantyās tat katham asatītvaśaṅkā syāt | (p.24, l.6)

rājan rājapatnyāḥ sūryam apaśyantyās tat katham asatītvaśaṅkā syāt |

p.24, l.6

ślokārthe prastutārthe ca matsyānāṃ hasanaṃ budhāḥ |(p.24, l.7)
 sanṛpā na vijānanti api sarvārthakovidāḥ || 5.24 (= 53) ||(p.24, l.8)
ślokārthe prastutārthe ca matsyānāṃ hasanaṃ budhāḥ | sanṛpā na vijānanti api sarvārthakovidāḥ || 5.24 (= 53) ||

p.24, l.8

tataḥ sado mūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bālapaṇḍitā utthāya yayau | śuko 'py āha | (p.24, l.9)
ahaṃ prātaḥ kathayiṣye | iti kīroktiṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || (p.24, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau pañcamī kathā || (p.24, l.11)

tataḥ sado mūḍhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bālapaṇḍitā utthāya yayau | śuko 'py āha | ahaṃ prātaḥ kathayiṣye | iti kīroktiṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau pañcamī kathā ||

§ 6

p.24, l.11

athāparasmin divase prabhāvatī śukaṃ prāha | śuka sa matsyahāsyavyatikaro (p.24, l.12)
rājñā jñāto na veti | śuka āha | sa nṛpaḥ ślokārtham ajānan na (p.24, l.13)
nidrāṃ lebhe | (p.25, l.1)

athāparasmin divase prabhāvatī śukaṃ prāha | śuka sa matsyahāsyavyatikaro rājñā jñāto na veti | śuka āha | sa nṛpaḥ ślokārtham ajānan na nidrāṃ lebhe |

p.25, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

nidrā bhadre kutas teṣāṃ ye ṛṇavyādhipīḍitāḥ |(p.25, l.2)
 avidheyakalatrāś ca ye cānye kṛtavairiṇaḥ || 6.1 (= 54) ||(p.25, l.3)

uktaṃ ca |

nidrā bhadre kutas teṣāṃ ye ṛṇavyādhipīḍitāḥ | avidheyakalatrāś ca ye cānye kṛtavairiṇaḥ || 6.1 (= 54) ||

p.25, l.3

rājā nidrābhāve kaṣṭena niśāṃ nītvā prātar bālapaṇḍitām ākārya prāha | (p.25, l.4)
bālike ślokārtho na jñāto mayā | tasmān matsyahāsyakāraṇe nivedaya | (p.25, l.5)

rājā nidrābhāve kaṣṭena niśāṃ nītvā prātar bālapaṇḍitām ākārya prāha | bālike ślokārtho na jñāto mayā | tasmān matsyahāsyakāraṇe nivedaya |

p.25, l.5

sā āha | rājan māṃ mā pṛccha | (p.25, l.6)

sā āha | rājan māṃ mā pṛccha |

p.25, l.6

yataḥ |

paścāttāpo 'tra bhavitā bhāryāyā vaṇijo yathā |(p.25, l.7)
 āgraheṇa kṛtaḥ patyau maṇḍakāgamanaṃ prati || 6.2 (= 55) ||(p.25, l.8)

yataḥ |

paścāttāpo 'tra bhavitā bhāryāyā vaṇijo yathā | āgraheṇa kṛtaḥ patyau maṇḍakāgamanaṃ prati || 6.2 (= 55) ||

p.25, l.8

rājā | katham etat | śukaḥ | asty atra jayantī nāma nagarī | tatra (p.25, l.9)
vaṇikputraḥ sumatir nāma | tasya priyā padminī nāma | tasya ca vaṇijaḥ (p.25, l.10)
puṇyakṣayād dhanaṃ kṣīṇam | sa ca janaiḥ parityaktaḥ | yato jano dhanamitraḥ | (p.25, l.11)

rājā | katham etat | śukaḥ | asty atra jayantī nāma nagarī | tatra vaṇikputraḥ sumatir nāma | tasya priyā padminī nāma | tasya ca vaṇijaḥ puṇyakṣayād dhanaṃ kṣīṇam | sa ca janaiḥ parityaktaḥ | yato jano dhanamitraḥ |

p.25, l.11

uktaṃ ca |

yasyārthās tasya mitrāṇi yasyārthās tasya bāndhavāḥ |(p.26, l.1)
 yasyārthāḥ sa pumāṁl loke yasyārthāḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ || 6.3 (= 56) ||(p.26, l.2)

uktaṃ ca |

yasyārthās tasya mitrāṇi yasyārthās tasya bāndhavāḥ | yasyārthāḥ sa pumāṁl loke yasyārthāḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ || 6.3 (= 56) ||

p.26, l.2

tathā ca bhārate |

jīvanto 'pi mṛtāḥ pañca śrūyante kila bhārata |(p.26, l.4)
 daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ pravāsī nityasevakaḥ || 6.4 (= 57) ||(p.26, l.5)

tathā ca bhārate |

jīvanto 'pi mṛtāḥ pañca śrūyante kila bhārata | daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ pravāsī nityasevakaḥ || 6.4 (= 57) ||

tathā ca |

iha loke hi dhanināṃ paro 'pi svajanāyate |(p.26, l.6)
 svajano 'pi daridrāṇāṃ tatkṣaṇād durjanāyate || 6.5 (= 58) ||(p.26, l.7)

tathā ca |

iha loke hi dhanināṃ paro 'pi svajanāyate | svajano 'pi daridrāṇāṃ tatkṣaṇād durjanāyate || 6.5 (= 58) ||

p.26, l.7

so 'pi ca tṛṇakāṣṭhādikam ānīya purīmadhye vikrīṇāti | anyadā (p.26, l.8)
anena tṛṇakāṣṭhādikaṃ kim api vane na prāptam | dṛḍhakāṣṭhamayo 'pi vighnavināyakaḥ (p.26, l.9)
prāptaḥ | tataś cintitam | kim asau mama vidhāsyati | (p.26, l.10)

so 'pi ca tṛṇakāṣṭhādikam ānīya purīmadhye vikrīṇāti | anyadā anena tṛṇakāṣṭhādikaṃ kim api vane na prāptam | dṛḍhakāṣṭhamayo 'pi vighnavināyakaḥ prāptaḥ | tataś cintitam | kim asau mama vidhāsyati |

p.26, l.10

uktaṃ ca |

bubhukṣitaḥ kiṃ na karoti pāpaṃ kṣīṇā narā niḥkaruṇā bhavanti |(p.26, l.11)
 prāṇārtham ete hi samācaranti mataṃ satāṃ yan na mataṃ tad eṣām || 6.6 (= 59) ||(p.27, l.1)

uktaṃ ca |

bubhukṣitaḥ kiṃ na karoti pāpaṃ kṣīṇā narā niḥkaruṇā bhavanti | prāṇārtham ete hi samācaranti mataṃ satāṃ yan na mataṃ tad eṣām || 6.6 (= 59) ||

p.27, l.1

yāvat sa tasya vināyakasya pāṭanāyottiṣṭhati tāvat tuṣṭaḥ san jagāda | (p.27, l.2)
ahaṃ tava pratidinaṃ pañca pañca maṇḍakān dāsye khaṇḍaghṛtayutān | mamālaye (p.27, l.3)
prātar yāyāḥ | paraṃ kasyāpi idaṃ rahasyaṃ na kathanīyam | kathite tu (p.27, l.4)
madvaco vitathaṃ bhaviṣyati | so 'pi ca tatheti pratipadya nityaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ (p.27, l.5)
bhāryāyā arpayati | tad daivaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ ghṛtakhaṇḍayuktam ādāya (p.27, l.6)
tadbhāryā nijakuṭumbaṃ tṛptīkaroti | nityaṃ ca tānmaṇḍakān gotriṇāṃ (p.27, l.7)
gṛhe vāhayām āsa | nijasakhyā mandodaryās tṛptyarthaṃ nityaṃ prāhiṇot | (p.27, l.8)
anyadā sā sakhī tāṃ papraccha | padminy api maṇḍakāgamanam idaṃ na jānāti | (p.28, l.1)
tatas tasyāḥ purā sā sakhī kapaṭād brūte | sakhi yadi tvaṃ mama purato (p.28, l.2)
guhyaṃ na kathayasi tat kaḥ snehaḥ | (p.28, l.3)

yāvat sa tasya vināyakasya pāṭanāyottiṣṭhati tāvat tuṣṭaḥ san jagāda | ahaṃ tava pratidinaṃ pañca pañca maṇḍakān dāsye khaṇḍaghṛtayutān | mamālaye prātar yāyāḥ | paraṃ kasyāpi idaṃ rahasyaṃ na kathanīyam | kathite tu madvaco vitathaṃ bhaviṣyati | so 'pi ca tatheti pratipadya nityaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ bhāryāyā arpayati | tad daivaṃ maṇḍakapañcakaṃ ghṛtakhaṇḍayuktam ādāya tadbhāryā nijakuṭumbaṃ tṛptīkaroti | nityaṃ ca tānmaṇḍakān gotriṇāṃ gṛhe vāhayām āsa | nijasakhyā mandodaryās tṛptyarthaṃ nityaṃ prāhiṇot | anyadā sā sakhī tāṃ papraccha | padminy api maṇḍakāgamanam idaṃ na jānāti | tatas tasyāḥ purā sā sakhī kapaṭād brūte | sakhi yadi tvaṃ mama purato guhyaṃ na kathayasi tat kaḥ snehaḥ |

p.28, l.3

uktaṃ ca |

dadāti pratigṛhṇāti guhyam ākhyāti pṛcchati |(p.28, l.4)
 bhuṅkte bhojayati caiva ṣaḍvidhaṃ prītilakṣaṇam || 6.7 (= 60) ||(p.28, l.5)

uktaṃ ca |

dadāti pratigṛhṇāti guhyam ākhyāti pṛcchati | bhuṅkte bhojayati caiva ṣaḍvidhaṃ prītilakṣaṇam || 6.7 (= 60) ||

p.28, l.5

tataḥ padminy āha | madīyaḥ patir idaṃ guhyaṃ mamāgre katham api na brūte (p.28, l.6)
mayā śataśaḥ pṛṣṭo 'pi | tayoktam | tarhi tvadīyaṃ jīvitaṃ rūpaṃ yauvanaṃ (p.28, l.7)
sarvam api nirarthakam eva yad idaṃ nājñāyi | tataḥ padminī patiṃ (p.28, l.8)
pṛcchati | kathaṃ maṇḍakaprāptiḥ | patir āha | vidheḥ prasādāt | (p.28, l.9)

tataḥ padminy āha | madīyaḥ patir idaṃ guhyaṃ mamāgre katham api na brūte mayā śataśaḥ pṛṣṭo 'pi | tayoktam | tarhi tvadīyaṃ jīvitaṃ rūpaṃ yauvanaṃ sarvam api nirarthakam eva yad idaṃ nājñāyi | tataḥ padminī patiṃ pṛcchati | kathaṃ maṇḍakaprāptiḥ | patir āha | vidheḥ prasādāt |

p.28, l.9

uktaṃ ca |

dvīpād anyasmād api madhyād api jalanidher diśo 'py antāt |(p.28, l.10)
 ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhir abhimatam abhimukhībhūtaḥ || 6.8 (= 61) ||(p.28, l.11)

uktaṃ ca |

dvīpād anyasmād api madhyād api jalanidher diśo 'py antāt | ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhir abhimatam abhimukhībhūtaḥ || 6.8 (= 61) ||

p.28, l.11

kiṃ ca |

kṣutkṣāmasya karaṇḍapiṇḍitatanor mlānendriyasya kṣudhā(p.28, l.12)
kṛtvākhur vivaraṃ svayaṃ nipatito naktaṃ mukhe bhoginaḥ |(p.28, l.13)
 tṛptas tatpiśitena satvaram asau tenaiva yātaḥ pathā(p.29, l.1)
svasthās tiṣṭhata daivam eva hi nṛṇāṃ vṛddhau kṣaye kāraṇam || 6.9 (= 62) ||(p.29, l.2)

kiṃ ca |

kṣutkṣāmasya karaṇḍapiṇḍitatanor mlānendriyasya kṣudhā kṛtvākhur vivaraṃ svayaṃ nipatito naktaṃ mukhe bhoginaḥ | tṛptas tatpiśitena satvaram asau tenaiva yātaḥ pathā svasthās tiṣṭhata daivam eva hi nṛṇāṃ vṛddhau kṣaye kāraṇam || 6.9 (= 62) ||

p.29, l.2

yadā na kathayati tadānaśanaṃ cakre | patir āha | asmin kathite mahatī (p.29, l.3)
hāniḥ paścāttāpaś ca bhaviṣyati | evaṃ bodhitāpi sā yāvan nāgrahaṃ muñcati (p.29, l.4)
tadā tena daivopahatacittena kathitam | (p.29, l.5)

yadā na kathayati tadānaśanaṃ cakre | patir āha | asmin kathite mahatī hāniḥ paścāttāpaś ca bhaviṣyati | evaṃ bodhitāpi sā yāvan nāgrahaṃ muñcati tadā tena daivopahatacittena kathitam |

p.29, l.5

uktaṃ ca |

yasmai devāḥ prayacchanti puruṣāya parābhavam |(p.29, l.6)
 buddhiṃ tasyāpakarṣanti na sa vetty ātmano hitam || 6.10 (= 63) ||(p.29, l.7)

uktaṃ ca |

yasmai devāḥ prayacchanti puruṣāya parābhavam | buddhiṃ tasyāpakarṣanti na sa vetty ātmano hitam || 6.10 (= 63) ||

p.29, l.7

tena ca rājan vikramārka buddhimuktena guhyaṃ kīrtitam | yato hīnapuṇyo (p.29, l.8)
buddhyā mucyate | (p.29, l.9)

tena ca rājan vikramārka buddhimuktena guhyaṃ kīrtitam | yato hīnapuṇyo buddhyā mucyate |

p.29, l.9

uktaṃ ca |

rāmo hemamṛgaṃ na vetti nahuṣo yāne yunakti dvijān(p.29, l.10)
viprād eva savatsadhenuharaṇe jātā matiś cārjune |(p.29, l.11)
 dyūte bhrātṛcatuṣṭayaṃ ca mahiṣīṃ dharmātmajo dattavān(p.29, l.12)
prāyaḥ satpuruṣo 'py anarthasamaye buddhyā parityajyate || 6.11 (= 64) ||(p.29, l.13)

uktaṃ ca |

rāmo hemamṛgaṃ na vetti nahuṣo yāne yunakti dvijān viprād eva savatsadhenuharaṇe jātā matiś cārjune | dyūte bhrātṛcatuṣṭayaṃ ca mahiṣīṃ dharmātmajo dattavān prāyaḥ satpuruṣo 'py anarthasamaye buddhyā parityajyate || 6.11 (= 64) ||

p.29, l.13

sā ca patimukhāt śrutvā sakhīpuro jagāda | tayā cātmapatiḥ kuṭhārahastaḥ (p.30, l.1)
preṣito vināyakapārśve | so 'pi padminīpatiś ca prātas tatra (p.30, l.2)
jagāma | vināyako 'pi tau dvāv api mayūrabandhair bandhayām āsa | so 'pi (p.30, l.3)
ca padminīpatir uktaḥ | re tvadīya evāyam anarthaḥ | tatas tvayy eva daṇḍo (p.30, l.4)
yujyate | tataḥ sakhīpatir yayāce | tān pañca maṇḍakān tasmai sa pradadau | (p.30, l.5)
tau dvāv api svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tataḥ patyā padminī jalpitā | (p.30, l.6)
tvayā te pañcāpi maṇḍakā asmākaṃ spheṭitāḥ etasya dāpitāḥ | paścāttāpaṃ (p.30, l.7)
ca kurute | tatas tvam api rājendra māṃ mā pṛccha | tava paścāttāpo (p.30, l.8)
bhaviṣyati | idaṃ ślokaṃ svayam eva vicintaya | iti kathayitvā bālapaṇḍitā (p.30, l.9)
utthāya svagṛhaṃ gatā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.30, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭhī kathā ||

sā ca patimukhāt śrutvā sakhīpuro jagāda | tayā cātmapatiḥ kuṭhārahastaḥ preṣito vināyakapārśve | so 'pi padminīpatiś ca prātas tatra jagāma | vināyako 'pi tau dvāv api mayūrabandhair bandhayām āsa | so 'pi ca padminīpatir uktaḥ | re tvadīya evāyam anarthaḥ | tatas tvayy eva daṇḍo yujyate | tataḥ sakhīpatir yayāce | tān pañca maṇḍakān tasmai sa pradadau | tau dvāv api svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tataḥ patyā padminī jalpitā | tvayā te pañcāpi maṇḍakā asmākaṃ spheṭitāḥ etasya dāpitāḥ | paścāttāpaṃ ca kurute | tatas tvam api rājendra māṃ mā pṛccha | tava paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati | idaṃ ślokaṃ svayam eva vicintaya | iti kathayitvā bālapaṇḍitā utthāya svagṛhaṃ gatā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭhī kathā ||

§ 7

(p.31, l.1)

p.31, l.1

anyasmin dine prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha | kīra punas tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ (p.31, l.2)
rājñā śrutaṃ na vā | śukaḥ prāha | prātaḥ punar bālapaṇḍitām ākārayitvā (p.31, l.3)
rājā prāha | kiṃ tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇam brūhi śīghraṃ bālike | (p.31, l.4)
sā cāha | (p.31, l.5)

anyasmin dine prabhāvatī śukaṃ papraccha | kīra punas tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ rājñā śrutaṃ na vā | śukaḥ prāha | prātaḥ punar bālapaṇḍitām ākārayitvā rājā prāha | kiṃ tanmatsyahāsyakāraṇam brūhi śīghraṃ bālike | sā cāha |

p.31, l.5

devāgraho na kartavyaḥ paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati |(p.31, l.6)
 sthagikāsaktacittasya viprasyābhūt purā yathā || 7.1 (= 65) ||(p.31, l.7)
devāgraho na kartavyaḥ paścāttāpo bhaviṣyati | sthagikāsaktacittasya viprasyābhūt purā yathā || 7.1 (= 65) ||

p.31, l.7

asti dharaṇītale vatsonanāma paṭṭanam | tatra vīrākhyo rājā | tatra (p.31, l.8)
ca keśavo nāma brāhmaṇaḥ | tena kadācid iti cintitam | yad ahaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ (p.31, l.9)
na bhokṣye | (p.32, l.1)

asti dharaṇītale vatsonanāma paṭṭanam | tatra vīrākhyo rājā | tatra ca keśavo nāma brāhmaṇaḥ | tena kadācid iti cintitam | yad ahaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ na bhokṣye |

p.32, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

uttamāḥ svaguṇaiḥ khyātā madhyamāś ca pitur guṇaiḥ |(p.32, l.2)
 adhamā mātulaiḥ khyātā śvaśuraiś cādhamādhamāḥ || 7.2 (= 66) ||(p.32, l.3)

uktaṃ ca |

uttamāḥ svaguṇaiḥ khyātā madhyamāś ca pitur guṇaiḥ | adhamā mātulaiḥ khyātā śvaśuraiś cādhamādhamāḥ || 7.2 (= 66) ||

kiṃ ca |

piara viḍhattaï davvaḍaï caḍḍiri ko ṇa karei |(p.32, l.4)
 saïṁ viḍhavaï saïṁ bhojaaï viralā jaṇaṇi jaṇei || 7.3 (= 67) ||

(•)

kiṃ ca |

piara viḍhattaï davvaḍaï caḍḍiri ko ṇa karei | saïṁ viḍhavaï saïṁ bhojaaï viralā jaṇaṇi jaṇei || 7.3 (= 67) ||

(•)

p.32, l.5

ity avadhārya sa medinyāṃ babhrāma devatīrthaśmaśānanagareṣu dhanārtham | (p.32, l.6)
anyadā sa nirjane pradeśe prasiddhe śivacatvare karālāyāḥ śmaśāne ca (p.32, l.7)
paribhramya pariśrāntaḥ kapilakamaṭham apaśyat | tatra ca paryaṅkāsanasthaṃ tāpasaṃ (p.32, l.8)
dadarśa | sa ca vipras tasyāgre kṛtāñjalipuṭas tasthau | tāpaso dhyānaṃ (p.32, l.9)
śanair muktvā evam uktavān | (p.33, l.1)

ity avadhārya sa medinyāṃ babhrāma devatīrthaśmaśānanagareṣu dhanārtham | anyadā sa nirjane pradeśe prasiddhe śivacatvare karālāyāḥ śmaśāne ca paribhramya pariśrāntaḥ kapilakamaṭham apaśyat | tatra ca paryaṅkāsanasthaṃ tāpasaṃ dadarśa | sa ca vipras tasyāgre kṛtāñjalipuṭas tasthau | tāpaso dhyānaṃ śanair muktvā evam uktavān |

p.33, l.1

kiṃ kasmai dīyate loke trāyate ko bhavārṇavāt |(p.33, l.2)
 asādhyaṃ sādhyate kasya kāle 'sminn atither aho || 7.4 (= 68) ||(p.33, l.3)
kiṃ kasmai dīyate loke trāyate ko bhavārṇavāt | asādhyaṃ sādhyate kasya kāle 'sminn atither aho || 7.4 (= 68) ||

p.33, l.3

tataḥ sa brāhmaṇa ūrdhvabāhur jagāda | tavāham atithir dhanārthī | tāpaso (p.33, l.4)
'pi taṃ vipram alpayācakaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasi duḥkhībabhūva | (p.33, l.5)

tataḥ sa brāhmaṇa ūrdhvabāhur jagāda | tavāham atithir dhanārthī | tāpaso 'pi taṃ vipram alpayācakaṃ dṛṣṭvā manasi duḥkhībabhūva |

p.33, l.5

uktaṃ ca |

stokārthaprārthanān dīnān dṛṣṭvodārān hi yācakān |(p.33, l.6)
 khidyante 'tīva manasi api prāṇapradāyinaḥ || 7.5 (= 69) ||(p.33, l.7)

uktaṃ ca |

stokārthaprārthanān dīnān dṛṣṭvodārān hi yācakān | khidyante 'tīva manasi api prāṇapradāyinaḥ || 7.5 (= 69) ||

kiṃ ca |

ahihūo vi a vivaā karei suaṇo parassa uvaāraṃ |(p.33, l.8)
 oṇei aṇṇadāvaṃ candaṇataruo sakhaṇḍo vi || 7.6 (= 70) ||

(•)

kiṃ ca |

ahihūo vi a vivaā karei suaṇo parassa uvaāraṃ | oṇei aṇṇadāvaṃ candaṇataruo sakhaṇḍo vi || 7.6 (= 70) ||

(•)

p.34, l.1

tato yogīndra yadā tvam etatsparśanaṃ kariṣyasi tadā hemnaḥ pañcaśatāni (p.34, l.2)
nityaṃ dāsyatīty uktvā viprāya paryaṅkīkṛtaṃ sindūram arpayām āsa | uktaś ca | (p.34, l.3)
etat tvayānyasmai na dātavyaṃ na kathanīyaṃ ca | anyathā mama samīpe vyāvṛtya (p.34, l.4)
sameṣyati | tadarpitaṃ yadā sa dvijaḥ prātaḥ spṛśati tadā suvarṇaśatapañcakaṃ (p.34, l.5)
dadāti | sa ca ratnāvatīṃ purīṃ gataḥ | tatra sthagikāṃ nāma (p.34, l.6)
veśyāṃ nityaṃ kāmayate | sā ca taddravyāgamanaṃ na jānāti | kuṭṭinī (p.34, l.7)
pṛcchati | hale eṣa vipraḥ kim api vyavasāyādikaṃ na vidhatte | paraṃ (p.34, l.8)
dravyaṃ kuto 'smākaṃ vitarati kasmād vilasatīti | tato veśyā taṃ pṛcchati | (p.34, l.9)
sa vipraḥ sarvathā na kathayati | tato veśyayā svakalayā bhaktyā (p.35, l.1)
cārādhitaḥ | tataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san kathayām āsa yat sindūrād dravyāgamaḥ | tayā (p.35, l.2)
ca suptasya sindūraṃ gṛhītam | tato dravyābhāve kuṭṭinyā gṛhān niḥkāsitaḥ | (p.35, l.3)

tato yogīndra yadā tvam etatsparśanaṃ kariṣyasi tadā hemnaḥ pañcaśatāni nityaṃ dāsyatīty uktvā viprāya paryaṅkīkṛtaṃ sindūram arpayām āsa | uktaś ca | etat tvayānyasmai na dātavyaṃ na kathanīyaṃ ca | anyathā mama samīpe vyāvṛtya sameṣyati | tadarpitaṃ yadā sa dvijaḥ prātaḥ spṛśati tadā suvarṇaśatapañcakaṃ dadāti | sa ca ratnāvatīṃ purīṃ gataḥ | tatra sthagikāṃ nāma veśyāṃ nityaṃ kāmayate | sā ca taddravyāgamanaṃ na jānāti | kuṭṭinī pṛcchati | hale eṣa vipraḥ kim api vyavasāyādikaṃ na vidhatte | paraṃ dravyaṃ kuto 'smākaṃ vitarati kasmād vilasatīti | tato veśyā taṃ pṛcchati | sa vipraḥ sarvathā na kathayati | tato veśyayā svakalayā bhaktyā cārādhitaḥ | tataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ san kathayām āsa yat sindūrād dravyāgamaḥ | tayā ca suptasya sindūraṃ gṛhītam | tato dravyābhāve kuṭṭinyā gṛhān niḥkāsitaḥ |

p.35, l.4

uktaṃ ca |

viśvāsapratipannānāṃ vañcane kā vidagdhatā |(p.35, l.5)
 aṅkam āruhya suptaṃ hi hantuṃ kiṃ nāma pauruṣam || 7.7 (= 71) ||(p.35, l.6)

uktaṃ ca |

viśvāsapratipannānāṃ vañcane kā vidagdhatā | aṅkam āruhya suptaṃ hi hantuṃ kiṃ nāma pauruṣam || 7.7 (= 71) ||

p.35, l.5

sa vipras tatsindūram apaśyan phūtkurvan rājadvāraṃ yayau muṣito 'ham iti vadan | (p.35, l.6)
tato vivādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | kuṭṭiny āha | (p.35, l.7)

sa vipras tatsindūram apaśyan phūtkurvan rājadvāraṃ yayau muṣito 'ham iti vadan | tato vivādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | kuṭṭiny āha |

p.35, l.7

dhūrto 'sau matsutālubdho dhanahīno bhavaty asau |(p.35, l.8)
 manobhavagrahagrasto asamaṃjasam īdṛśam || 7.8 (= 72) ||(p.35, l.9)
dhūrto 'sau matsutālubdho dhanahīno bhavaty asau | manobhavagrahagrasto asamaṃjasam īdṛśam || 7.8 (= 72) ||
janair guṇair asaṃbhāvyaṃ rājñā kathaṃ saṃbhāvyate |(p.35, l.10)
 paraṃ satyam idaṃ jātaṃ sindūraṃ dhanadaṃ yataḥ || 7.9 (= 73) ||(p.35, l.11)
janair guṇair asaṃbhāvyaṃ rājñā kathaṃ saṃbhāvyate | paraṃ satyam idaṃ jātaṃ sindūraṃ dhanadaṃ yataḥ || 7.9 (= 73) ||

p.35, l.11

sa ca janair vaideśiko 'yam iti jñātvā nirvāsitaḥ | tac ca sindūraṃ (p.36, l.1)
yogīndram eva yayau | tato rājan vikramāditya sthagikāprītinibandhanāt (p.36, l.2)
tenākhyāte ca sindūre sthagikā naiva viprasya babhūva na ca sindūram | (p.36, l.3)
evaṃ tavāpi rājan ratiḥ prītiś ca na bhaviṣyati | evam uktvā bālapaṇḍitā (p.36, l.4)
gṛhaṃ jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.36, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau saptamī kathā || (p.36, l.6)

sa ca janair vaideśiko 'yam iti jñātvā nirvāsitaḥ | tac ca sindūraṃ yogīndram eva yayau | tato rājan vikramāditya sthagikāprītinibandhanāt tenākhyāte ca sindūre sthagikā naiva viprasya babhūva na ca sindūram | evaṃ tavāpi rājan ratiḥ prītiś ca na bhaviṣyati | evam uktvā bālapaṇḍitā gṛhaṃ jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptamī kathā ||

§ 8

p.36, l.6

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka uttaraṃ dadau | devi bālapaṇḍitā (p.36, l.7)
dvitīye 'hni saṃyāte rājānaṃ prāha | deva nāgrahaḥ kartuṃ yujyate | (p.36, l.8)

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka uttaraṃ dadau | devi bālapaṇḍitā dvitīye 'hni saṃyāte rājānaṃ prāha | deva nāgrahaḥ kartuṃ yujyate |

p.36, l.8

yataḥ |

rājñā naivāgrahaḥ kāryaḥ śubhe vāśubhakarmaṇi |(p.36, l.9)
 tadaṅgāni hi bhūtāni rājñāṃ hi mahatī tanuḥ || 8.1 (= 74) ||(p.36, l.10)

yataḥ |

rājñā naivāgrahaḥ kāryaḥ śubhe vāśubhakarmaṇi | tadaṅgāni hi bhūtāni rājñāṃ hi mahatī tanuḥ || 8.1 (= 74) ||
ākhyāte ca tava mayā vaṇikputryā yathābhavat |(p.36, l.11)
 na bahir na gṛhaṃ rājan tathā te 'pi bhaviṣyati || 8.2 (= 75) ||(p.37, l.1)
ākhyāte ca tava mayā vaṇikputryā yathābhavat | na bahir na gṛhaṃ rājan tathā te 'pi bhaviṣyati || 8.2 (= 75) ||

p.37, l.1

rājā pṛcchati | katham etat | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | asti pṛthvītale (p.37, l.2)
tripuraṃ nāma sthānam | tasmin trivikramo nāma rājā | tatra sundarābhidhāno (p.37, l.3)
vaṇik | tadbhāryā subhagā nāma atīva kulaṭā | sā ca (p.37, l.4)
bhartrā gṛhān niryāntī prayatnena niyantritā | tāṃ ca niyantraṇāt pūrvam eko (p.37, l.5)
vaṇig yakṣagṛhe sthitaḥ sakāmām abhajat | yadā ca bahir nirgacchantī patinā (p.37, l.6)
nivāritā tadā sakhīṃ prāha | sakhi adya tvayā sa mānavo yakṣāyatane (p.37, l.7)
ākāraṇīyaḥ yathāhaṃ tatra gatvā taṃ rame | tvayā ca mayi gatāyāṃ (p.37, l.8)
paścād asmadgṛhaṃ jvālanīyaṃ yathā gṛhakāryāsakto jano māṃ gatāṃ na (p.37, l.9)
jānāti | atrāntare 'haṃ taṃ svecchayā bhuktā samupāgacchāmi | tataḥ (p.37, l.10)
sakhīvacanāt sa pumān tatrāyātaḥ | sāpy āgatā | tadā ca gatāyāṃ tasyāṃ (p.38, l.1)
sā sakhī tadgṛhaṃ prajvālitavatī | sa pumān prajvalane kutūhalī yakṣāyatanaṃ (p.38, l.2)
muktvā tatrāvalokanāya gataḥ | sā ca tatra sthitāsamāptātmaprayojanā (p.38, l.3)
yāvatā gṛham āgatā tāvatā gṛhaṃ dagdham | (p.38, l.4)

rājā pṛcchati | katham etat | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | asti pṛthvītale tripuraṃ nāma sthānam | tasmin trivikramo nāma rājā | tatra sundarābhidhāno vaṇik | tadbhāryā subhagā nāma atīva kulaṭā | sā ca bhartrā gṛhān niryāntī prayatnena niyantritā | tāṃ ca niyantraṇāt pūrvam eko vaṇig yakṣagṛhe sthitaḥ sakāmām abhajat | yadā ca bahir nirgacchantī patinā nivāritā tadā sakhīṃ prāha | sakhi adya tvayā sa mānavo yakṣāyatane ākāraṇīyaḥ yathāhaṃ tatra gatvā taṃ rame | tvayā ca mayi gatāyāṃ paścād asmadgṛhaṃ jvālanīyaṃ yathā gṛhakāryāsakto jano māṃ gatāṃ na jānāti | atrāntare 'haṃ taṃ svecchayā bhuktā samupāgacchāmi | tataḥ sakhīvacanāt sa pumān tatrāyātaḥ | sāpy āgatā | tadā ca gatāyāṃ tasyāṃ sā sakhī tadgṛhaṃ prajvālitavatī | sa pumān prajvalane kutūhalī yakṣāyatanaṃ muktvā tatrāvalokanāya gataḥ | sā ca tatra sthitāsamāptātmaprayojanā yāvatā gṛham āgatā tāvatā gṛhaṃ dagdham |

p.38, l.4

na gṛhaṃ na bahir bhūpa vaṇigvadhvā yathābhavat |(p.38, l.5)
 tathā tava mahārāja bhaviṣyati suniścayam || 8.3 (= 76) ||(p.38, l.6)
na gṛhaṃ na bahir bhūpa vaṇigvadhvā yathābhavat | tathā tava mahārāja bhaviṣyati suniścayam || 8.3 (= 76) ||

p.38, l.6

atha cet jñātena ślokārthena prayojanaṃ tadā kalye svayam eva jñāpayiṣyāmi | (p.38, l.7)
ity uktvā sā gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || (p.38, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭamī kathā || (p.38, l.9)

atha cet jñātena ślokārthena prayojanaṃ tadā kalye svayam eva jñāpayiṣyāmi | ity uktvā sā gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau aṣṭamī kathā ||

§ 9

p.38, l.9

athāparedyuḥ savismayā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka kiṃ vijñātaṃ (p.39, l.1)
vikramārkeṇa matsyahasanakāraṇam | śukaḥ prāha | devi na kim api rājñā (p.39, l.2)
svayaṃ jñātam | tato rājā prātar dvijasutām āhūya bālapaṇḍitāṃ prāha | (p.39, l.3)
tvayā ity uktaṃ yat tvaṃ svayam eva jñāsyasi | mayā tu kim api na jñātam | (p.39, l.4)
bālapaṇḍitā prāha | yadi rājann evam api mayā kathyamānaṃ na vetsi (p.39, l.5)
tataḥ śṛṇu | puṣpahāso nāma mantrī sarvamantriṇām agraṇīr nirdoṣo guptaḥ | (p.39, l.6)
kim iti niyantrito 'sti | rājā prāha | anvartho 'yaṃ puṣpahāsaḥ | (p.39, l.7)
yataḥ | yadāsau madīyāyāṃ saṃsadi hasati tadāsyāsyāt puṣpaprakaro (p.39, l.8)
nipatati | iyaṃ ca kathāpararājyamaṇḍaleṣu khyātābhūt | tatas taiḥ preṣitāḥ (p.39, l.9)
svīyapumāṃsaḥ kutūhalānveṣaṇāya | teṣu samāyāteṣu tena na hasitaṃ puṣpaprakaro (p.39, l.10)
'pi nābhūt | iti kāraṇāt guptibandhaḥ | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | (p.40, l.1)
kenāpi kāraṇena mantriṇā na hasitam | rājan tatkāraṇaṃ tvayā jñātaṃ (p.40, l.2)
na vā | rājā prāha | mayā kim api na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā (p.40, l.3)
prāha | tarhi katham idaṃ daṇḍaṃ kurvan pāpabhāk na bhavasi | (p.40, l.4)

athāparedyuḥ savismayā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka kiṃ vijñātaṃ vikramārkeṇa matsyahasanakāraṇam | śukaḥ prāha | devi na kim api rājñā svayaṃ jñātam | tato rājā prātar dvijasutām āhūya bālapaṇḍitāṃ prāha | tvayā ity uktaṃ yat tvaṃ svayam eva jñāsyasi | mayā tu kim api na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | yadi rājann evam api mayā kathyamānaṃ na vetsi tataḥ śṛṇu | puṣpahāso nāma mantrī sarvamantriṇām agraṇīr nirdoṣo guptaḥ | kim iti niyantrito 'sti | rājā prāha | anvartho 'yaṃ puṣpahāsaḥ | yataḥ | yadāsau madīyāyāṃ saṃsadi hasati tadāsyāsyāt puṣpaprakaro nipatati | iyaṃ ca kathāpararājyamaṇḍaleṣu khyātābhūt | tatas taiḥ preṣitāḥ svīyapumāṃsaḥ kutūhalānveṣaṇāya | teṣu samāyāteṣu tena na hasitaṃ puṣpaprakaro 'pi nābhūt | iti kāraṇāt guptibandhaḥ | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | kenāpi kāraṇena mantriṇā na hasitam | rājan tatkāraṇaṃ tvayā jñātaṃ na vā | rājā prāha | mayā kim api na jñātam | bālapaṇḍitā prāha | tarhi katham idaṃ daṇḍaṃ kurvan pāpabhāk na bhavasi |

p.40, l.4

uktaṃ ca |

dharmeṇa rāṣṭraṃ vindeta dharmeṇaivānupālayet |(p.40, l.5)
 dharmāc charaṇyatāṃ yāti rājā sarvabhayāpahaḥ || 9.1 (= 77) ||(p.40, l.6)

uktaṃ ca |

dharmeṇa rāṣṭraṃ vindeta dharmeṇaivānupālayet | dharmāc charaṇyatāṃ yāti rājā sarvabhayāpahaḥ || 9.1 (= 77) ||

p.40, l.6

yathā āgrahān māṃ matsyahāsakāraṇaṃ pṛcchasi tathā tam api pṛccha hāsyakāraṇam | (p.40, l.7)
sa evātmīyahāsyasya matsyahāsyasya ca kāraṇaṃ vaktā | rājāpi (p.40, l.8)
tadvacanāt puṣpahāsaṃ mantriṇaṃ vastradānapūrvaṃ mantripade pratiṣṭhāpya (p.40, l.9)
matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ papraccha | mantry āha | yady api gṛhaduścaritam akathyam | (p.40, l.10)

yathā āgrahān māṃ matsyahāsakāraṇaṃ pṛcchasi tathā tam api pṛccha hāsyakāraṇam | sa evātmīyahāsyasya matsyahāsyasya ca kāraṇaṃ vaktā | rājāpi tadvacanāt puṣpahāsaṃ mantriṇaṃ vastradānapūrvaṃ mantripade pratiṣṭhāpya matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ papraccha | mantry āha | yady api gṛhaduścaritam akathyam |

p.40, l.10

yataḥ |

arthanāśaṃ manastāpaṃ gṛhe duścaritāni ca |(p.40, l.11)
 vañcanaṃ cāpamānaṃ ca matimān na prakāśayet || 9.2 (= 78) ||(p.41, l.1)

yataḥ |

arthanāśaṃ manastāpaṃ gṛhe duścaritāni ca | vañcanaṃ cāpamānaṃ ca matimān na prakāśayet || 9.2 (= 78) ||

p.41, l.1

tathāpi tu rājājñā mahatī | (p.41, l.2)

tathāpi tu rājājñā mahatī |

p.41, l.2

yataḥ |

prabhuḥ prītisnigdhāṃ dṛśam api na pāpeṣu visṛjet(p.41, l.3)
kutaḥ ślāghyām ājñāṃ praṇayarasasāndreṇa manasā |(p.41, l.4)
 atītyādityāgniprabhṛti bhuvi dharmendriyam ayaṃ(p.41, l.5)
nṛpākhyaṃ hi jyotiḥ prasabham idam aindraṃ vijayate || 9.3 (= 79) ||(p.41, l.6)

yataḥ |

prabhuḥ prītisnigdhāṃ dṛśam api na pāpeṣu visṛjet kutaḥ ślāghyām ājñāṃ praṇayarasasāndreṇa manasā | atītyādityāgniprabhṛti bhuvi dharmendriyam ayaṃ nṛpākhyaṃ hi jyotiḥ prasabham idam aindraṃ vijayate || 9.3 (= 79) ||

p.41, l.6

tato rājan me kalatraṃ narāntararataṃ jātaṃ tac ca mayā jñātam | tena ca (p.41, l.7)
duḥkhena na hasitaḥ | rājāpīdam ākarṇya puṣpahastakai rājñīm āhatya saṃmukham (p.41, l.8)
avalokayām āsa | sā ca tena prahāreṇa kapaṭamūrcchāṃ nāṭayati sma | (p.41, l.9)
puṣpahāso 'pi tām avalokya sahāso babhūva puṣpotkaraś ca samajani | (p.41, l.10)
rājāpi tām āśvāsya kṛtakopo dvijātmajāsyaṃ vilokya mantriṇam avādīt | (p.41, l.11)
katham asmadduḥkhe sahāso 'si | mantry api sabhayam añjaliṃ baddhvābhāṣata | (p.42, l.1)
rājan poṭakajanais tvadīyā rājñī rātrau nāḍikābhir āhatāpi na (p.42, l.2)
mūrcchitā adhunā mūrcchiteti hāsyam | rājāpi sakopo mantrinn idaṃ (p.42, l.3)
tvayā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ veti papraccha | mantry āha | svāmin dṛṣṭam evedam | yadi (p.42, l.4)
svāmī na pratyeti tadā kañcukam uttāryāvalokayatu | evaṃ kṛte rājā (p.42, l.5)
sarvam ajñāsīt | mantriṇo dvijasutāyāś ca mukham avalokya kim idam ity avādīt | (p.42, l.6)
mantry āha | svāmin yad idaṃ dvijaputryā gūḍhārthaṃ matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ (p.42, l.7)
niveditaṃ tan mayā prakaṭīkṛtam | ity evam ukto rājā āsthānaṃ vyasarjayat | (p.42, l.8)
atha dvijasutāpuṣpahāsāv api bhītahṛṣṭau svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | (p.42, l.9)
tena ca rājñā tasyā mañjūṣāsthito naro dṛṣṭo vināśitaḥ | sā ca (p.42, l.10)
nijavāsād visarjitā | śukaḥ prabhāvatīm āha | (p.42, l.11)

tato rājan me kalatraṃ narāntararataṃ jātaṃ tac ca mayā jñātam | tena ca duḥkhena na hasitaḥ | rājāpīdam ākarṇya puṣpahastakai rājñīm āhatya saṃmukham avalokayām āsa | sā ca tena prahāreṇa kapaṭamūrcchāṃ nāṭayati sma | puṣpahāso 'pi tām avalokya sahāso babhūva puṣpotkaraś ca samajani | rājāpi tām āśvāsya kṛtakopo dvijātmajāsyaṃ vilokya mantriṇam avādīt | katham asmadduḥkhe sahāso 'si | mantry api sabhayam añjaliṃ baddhvābhāṣata | rājan poṭakajanais tvadīyā rājñī rātrau nāḍikābhir āhatāpi na mūrcchitā adhunā mūrcchiteti hāsyam | rājāpi sakopo mantrinn idaṃ tvayā dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ veti papraccha | mantry āha | svāmin dṛṣṭam evedam | yadi svāmī na pratyeti tadā kañcukam uttāryāvalokayatu | evaṃ kṛte rājā sarvam ajñāsīt | mantriṇo dvijasutāyāś ca mukham avalokya kim idam ity avādīt | mantry āha | svāmin yad idaṃ dvijaputryā gūḍhārthaṃ matsyahāsyakāraṇaṃ niveditaṃ tan mayā prakaṭīkṛtam | ity evam ukto rājā āsthānaṃ vyasarjayat | atha dvijasutāpuṣpahāsāv api bhītahṛṣṭau svaṃ svaṃ gṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tena ca rājñā tasyā mañjūṣāsthito naro dṛṣṭo vināśitaḥ | sā ca nijavāsād visarjitā | śukaḥ prabhāvatīm āha |

p.42, l.11

tathā tvam api kalyāṇi mā kuruṣva vṛthāgraham |(p.43, l.1)
 yad āgrahaparo loke vilakṣo vikramārkavat || 9.4 (= 80) ||(p.43, l.2)
tathā tvam api kalyāṇi mā kuruṣva vṛthāgraham | yad āgrahaparo loke vilakṣo vikramārkavat || 9.4 (= 80) ||

p.43, l.2

iti śukasaptatau navamī kathā || (p.43, l.4)

p.43, l.5

 yadi te 'sti sakhī yāhi śṛṅgārīva sahāyinī || 10.1 (= 81) ||(p.43, l.7)
kiṃ kartavyaṃ mayā kīra tvaṃ vadādya priyaṃvada | yadi te 'sti sakhī yāhi śṛṅgārīva sahāyinī || 10.1 (= 81) ||

p.43, l.7

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti rājapuraṃ nāma sthānam | (p.43, l.8)
tatra devasākhyaḥ kauṭumbikaḥ | tatkalatre śṛṅgāravatī subhagā ca | parasparaparitrāṇakṛtabandhaparāyaṇe | (p.43, l.9)
parapuruṣalampaṭe prasiddhe ratakarmaṇi | (|| 10.2 (= 82) ||) anyadā (p.43, l.10)
yāvat subhagā upapatinā saha gṛhāntar vidyate tāvad bahiḥsthānāt patir (p.43, l.11)
jhiṇṭahasto gṛhadvāri samāyayau | tadā sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | (p.44, l.1)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti rājapuraṃ nāma sthānam | tatra devasākhyaḥ kauṭumbikaḥ | tatkalatre śṛṅgāravatī subhagā ca | parasparaparitrāṇakṛtabandhaparāyaṇe | parapuruṣalampaṭe prasiddhe ratakarmaṇi | (|| 10.2 (= 82) ||) anyadā yāvat subhagā upapatinā saha gṛhāntar vidyate tāvad bahiḥsthānāt patir jhiṇṭahasto gṛhadvāri samāyayau | tadā sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ |

p.44, l.1

uttaram āha śukaḥ | tataḥ śṛṅgāradevyā sā nagnīkṛtya gṛhād bahir niṣkāśitā | (p.44, l.2)
patir api kim idam iti bruvāṇo 'tyādarāt śṛṅgāradevyā uktaḥ | (p.44, l.3)
yat tvayā etāni jhiṇṭāni devyā upavanād ānītāni tata iyaṃ grahilā (p.44, l.4)
saṃjātā | tato yathāsthānaṃ gatvā muñca yathā praguṇā syāt | tataḥ sa (p.44, l.5)
mūḍho yāvad evaṃ kartuṃ bahir jagāma tāvat tayā gṛhād upapatir niṣkāśitaḥ | (p.44, l.6)
iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.44, l.7)
iti śukasaptatau daśamī kathā || (p.44, l.8)

uttaram āha śukaḥ | tataḥ śṛṅgāradevyā sā nagnīkṛtya gṛhād bahir niṣkāśitā | patir api kim idam iti bruvāṇo 'tyādarāt śṛṅgāradevyā uktaḥ | yat tvayā etāni jhiṇṭāni devyā upavanād ānītāni tata iyaṃ grahilā saṃjātā | tato yathāsthānaṃ gatvā muñca yathā praguṇā syāt | tataḥ sa mūḍho yāvad evaṃ kartuṃ bahir jagāma tāvat tayā gṛhād upapatir niṣkāśitaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau daśamī kathā ||

 mano 'bhīṣṭe payo nimne gacchat kaḥ prativārayet || 11.2 (= 84) ||(p.45, l.2)

 yathā rambhikayā pūrvaṃ brāhmaṇārthe 'dbhutaṃ kṛtam || 11.3 (= 85) ||(p.45, l.4)

ādāya vāpīṃ yayau | dṛṣṭvā ca tatra surūpaṃ pathikaṃ bhaṭṭaputraṃ krīḍārthaṃ (p.45, l.8)

 puṇaruttapecchirīe bālaa kiṃ kiṃ ṇa bhaṇio si || 11.5 (= 87) ||

p.46, l.5

tataḥ sa tadantikam āgatya jagāda | bhadre kiṃ vidheyam | sāha | tvayā (p.46, l.6)
mama pṛṣṭhalagnena asmadgṛhaṃ samāgantavyaṃ mama patyuś ca namaskāro vidheyaḥ | (p.46, l.7)
sarvam anyad ahaṃ kariṣye | tvayā tathaiveti vācyam | evam uktvā sā gṛhaṃ (p.46, l.8)
praviṣṭā | so 'pi gṛhaṃ praviṣṭas tatpatyur agre tasthau | patir api vismitaḥ | (p.47, l.1)
tataḥ sā kumbhaṃ muktvā patyuḥ sakāśam āgatyābravīt | nātha upalakṣasvainam | (p.47, l.2)
sa āha | na vedmīti | tataḥ sā prāha | ayaṃ mātṛsvasuḥ suto yo (p.47, l.3)
mayā śiśutve muktaḥ | sa dhavalo nāma mama milanārthaṃ samāgamat | (p.47, l.4)
tato mayā āliṅgya sarvāpi svajanavārttā pṛṣṭā | sa ca brāhmaṇa evam (p.47, l.5)
iti jalpati | tataḥ patinā sānujñātā taṃ mahānasaṃ nītvā bhojanacchādanasaṃskārais (p.47, l.6)
toṣayām āsa | patir api tuṣṭaḥ prāha | bhadre tvayā (p.47, l.7)
nijabāndhavasya mahatī bhaktiḥ kāryety uktvā suptaḥ | tadā ca rambhikā (p.47, l.8)
brāhmaṇakhaṭvām upāviśat | tatas tenoktam | tvayā patyur agre ity uktaṃ yan madīyo (p.47, l.9)
bhrātā samāgataḥ | tat tvaṃ me pratipannā bhaginī pratipannaṃ ca (p.47, l.10)
nirvāhyate | (p.48, l.1)

tataḥ sa tadantikam āgatya jagāda | bhadre kiṃ vidheyam | sāha | tvayā mama pṛṣṭhalagnena asmadgṛhaṃ samāgantavyaṃ mama patyuś ca namaskāro vidheyaḥ | sarvam anyad ahaṃ kariṣye | tvayā tathaiveti vācyam | evam uktvā sā gṛhaṃ praviṣṭā | so 'pi gṛhaṃ praviṣṭas tatpatyur agre tasthau | patir api vismitaḥ | tataḥ sā kumbhaṃ muktvā patyuḥ sakāśam āgatyābravīt | nātha upalakṣasvainam | sa āha | na vedmīti | tataḥ sā prāha | ayaṃ mātṛsvasuḥ suto yo mayā śiśutve muktaḥ | sa dhavalo nāma mama milanārthaṃ samāgamat | tato mayā āliṅgya sarvāpi svajanavārttā pṛṣṭā | sa ca brāhmaṇa evam iti jalpati | tataḥ patinā sānujñātā taṃ mahānasaṃ nītvā bhojanacchādanasaṃskārais toṣayām āsa | patir api tuṣṭaḥ prāha | bhadre tvayā nijabāndhavasya mahatī bhaktiḥ kāryety uktvā suptaḥ | tadā ca rambhikā brāhmaṇakhaṭvām upāviśat | tatas tenoktam | tvayā patyur agre ity uktaṃ yan madīyo bhrātā samāgataḥ | tat tvaṃ me pratipannā bhaginī pratipannaṃ ca nirvāhyate |

p.48, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

śrūyate rukmiṇī pūrvaṃ kṛṣṇena madanāturā |(p.49, l.6)
 gṛhītā bhrātṛjāyāpi kaḥ kāmam atilaṅghayet || 11.13 (= 95) ||(p.49, l.7)
