virañcir api kāmārtaḥ svasutām abhilāṣukaḥ |(p.49, l.8)
 dṛśyate 'dyāpi viyati hāriṇīṃ tanum āśritaḥ || 11.14 (= 96) ||(p.49, l.9)
virañcir api kāmārtaḥ svasutām abhilāṣukaḥ | dṛśyate 'dyāpi viyati hāriṇīṃ tanum āśritaḥ || 11.14 (= 96) ||
vivāhe pārvatīṃ dṛṣṭvā harasya haravallabhām |(p.49, l.10)
 caskanda retas tasyāpi bālakhilyās tadudbhavāḥ || 11.15 (= 97) ||(p.49, l.11)
vivāhe pārvatīṃ dṛṣṭvā harasya haravallabhām | caskanda retas tasyāpi bālakhilyās tadudbhavāḥ || 11.15 (= 97) ||
tayaivaṃ bodhito mūrkhaḥ sa yāvad ramate na tām |(p.49, l.12)
 phūtkṛtaṃ muṣitāsmīti trāyatāṃ trāyatām aho || 11.16 (= 98) ||(p.50, l.1)
tayaivaṃ bodhito mūrkhaḥ sa yāvad ramate na tām | phūtkṛtaṃ muṣitāsmīti trāyatāṃ trāyatām aho || 11.16 (= 98) ||

p.50, l.1

tayā ca phūtkṛte kim idam iti kurvāṇo bāndhavaiḥ saha dhāvito bhartā | (p.50, l.2)
sa ca kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | evaṃ ca sa brāhmaṇaḥ (p.50, l.3)
sabhayaḥ san tatpādayoḥ patito jagāda | svāmini prāṇān rakṣa | tavehitaṃ (p.50, l.4)
kariṣyāmi | evaṃ sthite sā dugdhasahitaṃ bhaktam aḍhaṃḍholayat antike (p.50, l.5)
jvalinam ajvālayat āgataṃ ca patiṃ jagāda | asya viṣūcikā utpannā | (p.50, l.6)
tato mayā phūtkṛtam | evam uktvā dugdhabhaktaṃ pradarśitam | patir api (p.50, l.7)
mūrkho dṛṣṭvā yayau | tataḥ sā patyau supte yadṛcchayā surataṃ cakāra | (p.50, l.8)
so 'pi ca māndyavyājān māsam ekaṃ sthitaḥ paścāj jagāma | iti śrutvā (p.50, l.9)
prabhāvatī suptā | (p.50, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau ekādaśī kathā ||

tayā ca phūtkṛte kim idam iti kurvāṇo bāndhavaiḥ saha dhāvito bhartā | sa ca kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | evaṃ ca sa brāhmaṇaḥ sabhayaḥ san tatpādayoḥ patito jagāda | svāmini prāṇān rakṣa | tavehitaṃ kariṣyāmi | evaṃ sthite sā dugdhasahitaṃ bhaktam aḍhaṃḍholayat antike jvalinam ajvālayat āgataṃ ca patiṃ jagāda | asya viṣūcikā utpannā | tato mayā phūtkṛtam | evam uktvā dugdhabhaktaṃ pradarśitam | patir api mūrkho dṛṣṭvā yayau | tataḥ sā patyau supte yadṛcchayā surataṃ cakāra | so 'pi ca māndyavyājān māsam ekaṃ sthitaḥ paścāj jagāma | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekādaśī kathā ||

§ 12

(p.51, l.1)

p.51, l.1

athānyadā sā calitā | śukaḥ prāha | (p.51, l.2)

athānyadā sā calitā | śukaḥ prāha |

p.51, l.2

viparīte samāyāte yadi vetsi tvam uttaram |(p.51, l.3)
 yathā śobhikayā proktaṃ vavvūle caṭite sati || 12.1 (= 99) ||(p.51, l.4)
viparīte samāyāte yadi vetsi tvam uttaram | yathā śobhikayā proktaṃ vavvūle caṭite sati || 12.1 (= 99) ||

p.51, l.4

asty atra nalaüḍāgrāme kulālo mahādhanaḥ | tasya bhāryā śobhikā (p.51, l.5)
nāma paraṃ kulaṭā naralampaṭā ca | sā patyau bahir gate upapatisahitā (p.51, l.6)
gṛhāntaḥ krīḍati | tasyāś caivaṃ sthitāyā bhartā gṛhaṃ samāgamat | (p.51, l.7)
tadanantaraṃ sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | (p.51, l.8)
śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā sa (p.51, l.9)
āgacchan jñātas tadā upapatir uktaḥ | caṭa tvaṃ vavvūlavṛkṣam | evaṃ ca sa (p.51, l.10)
tayā proktas tathā cakāra | tasya ca vṛkṣe caṭataḥ paridhānavastraṃ vilagnaṃ (p.51, l.11)
nagno 'pi vṛkṣam ārūḍhaḥ | tasmiṃś ca vṛkṣam ārūḍhe patiḥ prāha | kim idam iti | (p.52, l.1)
sā āha | ayaṃ śatrubhir abhibhūto 'dho vastram api tyaktvā vavvūlam adhirūḍhaḥ | (p.52, l.2)
tataḥ samāgatya tasyāḥ patinā vṛkṣān mandaṃ mandam uttārya sa svagṛhaṃ (p.52, l.3)
preṣitaḥ | tayā dhūrtayā ca saha hastatālaṃ hasitam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā (p.52, l.4)
prabhāvatī suptā | (p.52, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau dvādaśī kathā || (p.52, l.6)

asty atra nalaüḍāgrāme kulālo mahādhanaḥ | tasya bhāryā śobhikā nāma paraṃ kulaṭā naralampaṭā ca | sā patyau bahir gate upapatisahitā gṛhāntaḥ krīḍati | tasyāś caivaṃ sthitāyā bhartā gṛhaṃ samāgamat | tadanantaraṃ sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā sa āgacchan jñātas tadā upapatir uktaḥ | caṭa tvaṃ vavvūlavṛkṣam | evaṃ ca sa tayā proktas tathā cakāra | tasya ca vṛkṣe caṭataḥ paridhānavastraṃ vilagnaṃ nagno 'pi vṛkṣam ārūḍhaḥ | tasmiṃś ca vṛkṣam ārūḍhe patiḥ prāha | kim idam iti | sā āha | ayaṃ śatrubhir abhibhūto 'dho vastram api tyaktvā vavvūlam adhirūḍhaḥ | tataḥ samāgatya tasyāḥ patinā vṛkṣān mandaṃ mandam uttārya sa svagṛhaṃ preṣitaḥ | tayā dhūrtayā ca saha hastatālaṃ hasitam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvādaśī kathā ||

§ 13

p.52, l.6

athānyedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka āha | (p.52, l.7)

athānyedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka āha |

p.52, l.7

vraja devi sukhaṃ bhuṅkṣva ardhabhukte patau yathā |(p.52, l.8)
 kṛtaṃ rājikayā citram uttaraṃ dhūlisaṃyutam || 13.1 (= 100) ||(p.52, l.9)
vraja devi sukhaṃ bhuṅkṣva ardhabhukte patau yathā | kṛtaṃ rājikayā citram uttaraṃ dhūlisaṃyutam || 13.1 (= 100) ||

p.52, l.9

asti nāgapuraṃ nāma sthānam | yatraiko vaṇik | tatpatnī rājikānāmnī (p.52, l.10)
surūpā paraṃ duścāriṇī | vaṇiksutaś ca tāṃ narāntarāsaktāṃ na (p.52, l.11)
jānāti | tataś ca ekadā sa bhojanāya yadopaviṣṭas tadā upapatiḥ kṛtasaṃketo (p.52, l.12)
mārge gacchan tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā gṛhe 'dya ghṛtaṃ nāsti ity uktvā (p.53, l.1)
dravyaṃ tatsakāśād ādāya ghṛtānayanadambhena veśmato nirgatya ca sā bahir (p.53, l.2)
jāreṇa saha ciraṃ sthitā | patis tu gṛhe kṣudhārtaḥ kruddhaś ca | tataḥ sā (p.53, l.3)
kathaṃ gṛhaṃ gantum arhati | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | tataḥ sā hastau pādau (p.53, l.4)
mukhaṃ ca dhūlidhūsaraṃ vidhāya sadrammā dhūliṃ gṛhītvā gṛham āgatā | (p.53, l.5)
patiḥ kruddho raktekṣaṇaḥ kim idam ity āha | sā ca saniḥśvāsaṃ rudatī (p.53, l.6)
dhūlipuñjaṃ darśayitvā idam uvāca | yatkṛte tvaṃ kruddhaḥ sa te dravyo 'tra (p.53, l.7)
dhūlyāṃ patitaḥ | enām utkṣipya gṛhāṇa tvam | evam uktaḥ sa vilakṣaḥ (p.53, l.8)
tadaṅgāni vastrāñcalena saṃmārjya sāntvayām āsa vividhalālanaiḥ | iti (p.53, l.9)
kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.53, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau trayodaśī kathā || (p.53, l.11)

asti nāgapuraṃ nāma sthānam | yatraiko vaṇik | tatpatnī rājikānāmnī surūpā paraṃ duścāriṇī | vaṇiksutaś ca tāṃ narāntarāsaktāṃ na jānāti | tataś ca ekadā sa bhojanāya yadopaviṣṭas tadā upapatiḥ kṛtasaṃketo mārge gacchan tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | taṃ ca dṛṣṭvā gṛhe 'dya ghṛtaṃ nāsti ity uktvā dravyaṃ tatsakāśād ādāya ghṛtānayanadambhena veśmato nirgatya ca sā bahir jāreṇa saha ciraṃ sthitā | patis tu gṛhe kṣudhārtaḥ kruddhaś ca | tataḥ sā kathaṃ gṛhaṃ gantum arhati | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | tataḥ sā hastau pādau mukhaṃ ca dhūlidhūsaraṃ vidhāya sadrammā dhūliṃ gṛhītvā gṛham āgatā | patiḥ kruddho raktekṣaṇaḥ kim idam ity āha | sā ca saniḥśvāsaṃ rudatī dhūlipuñjaṃ darśayitvā idam uvāca | yatkṛte tvaṃ kruddhaḥ sa te dravyo 'tra dhūlyāṃ patitaḥ | enām utkṣipya gṛhāṇa tvam | evam uktaḥ sa vilakṣaḥ tadaṅgāni vastrāñcalena saṃmārjya sāntvayām āsa vividhalālanaiḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau trayodaśī kathā ||

§ 14

p.53, l.11

sā nitambinī anyedyuś calitā | śukenoktam | (p.53, l.12)

sā nitambinī anyedyuś calitā | śukenoktam |

p.53, l.12

yuktam eva viśālākṣi paraṃ rantuṃ yadṛcchayā |(p.54, l.1)
 yady āyāte patau vetsi dhanaśrīr iva bhāṣitum || 14.1 (= 101) ||(p.54, l.2)
yuktam eva viśālākṣi paraṃ rantuṃ yadṛcchayā | yady āyāte patau vetsi dhanaśrīr iva bhāṣitum || 14.1 (= 101) ||

p.54, l.2

prabhāvaty āha | kim etat | śukaḥ prāha | asti padmāvatī purī | tatra (p.54, l.3)
dhanapālo nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā prāṇebhyo 'pi priyā dhanaśrīr (p.54, l.4)
nāma | tac ca mithunaṃ parasparaṃ snehanirbharaṃ krīḍati | anyadā tu (p.54, l.5)
vaṇig dravyasāram ādāya tām āpṛcchya deśāntaraṃ jagāma | sā ca tasmin (p.54, l.6)
gate saṃsthiteva gṛhasthitā | (p.54, l.7)

prabhāvaty āha | kim etat | śukaḥ prāha | asti padmāvatī purī | tatra dhanapālo nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā prāṇebhyo 'pi priyā dhanaśrīr nāma | tac ca mithunaṃ parasparaṃ snehanirbharaṃ krīḍati | anyadā tu vaṇig dravyasāram ādāya tām āpṛcchya deśāntaraṃ jagāma | sā ca tasmin gate saṃsthiteva gṛhasthitā |

p.54, l.7

na snāti na ca sā bhuṅkte na jalpati sakhīsamam |(p.54, l.8)
 nirastāśeṣasaṃskārā svadehe 'pi parāṅmukhī || 14.2 (= 102) ||(p.54, l.9)
na snāti na ca sā bhuṅkte na jalpati sakhīsamam | nirastāśeṣasaṃskārā svadehe 'pi parāṅmukhī || 14.2 (= 102) ||
malayānilam ārūḍhaḥ kokilālāpaḍiṇḍimaḥ |(p.54, l.10)
 mallikāmodadūtaś ca madhupāravamaṅgalaḥ || 14.3 (= 103) ||(p.54, l.11)
malayānilam ārūḍhaḥ kokilālāpaḍiṇḍimaḥ | mallikāmodadūtaś ca madhupāravamaṅgalaḥ || 14.3 (= 103) ||
anyadā tu samāyāto vasantaḥ kālarāṭ kṣitau |(p.54, l.12)
 mano 'pi vikriyāṃ yasmin yāti saṃyamināṃ kila || 14.4 (= 104) ||(p.54, l.13)
anyadā tu samāyāto vasantaḥ kālarāṭ kṣitau | mano 'pi vikriyāṃ yasmin yāti saṃyamināṃ kila || 14.4 (= 104) ||

p.54, l.13

tasmin vasantotsave gṛhopari sthitā nagarīramaṇīyakam ālokya yauvanaṃ (p.55, l.1)
rūpaṃ ca nininda | sakhī ca tadiṅgitajñā jagāda | bhāmini rūpaṃ (p.55, l.2)
vayaś ca mā vyarthaṃ vidhehi | (p.55, l.3)

tasmin vasantotsave gṛhopari sthitā nagarīramaṇīyakam ālokya yauvanaṃ rūpaṃ ca nininda | sakhī ca tadiṅgitajñā jagāda | bhāmini rūpaṃ vayaś ca mā vyarthaṃ vidhehi |

p.55, l.3

yataḥ |

vādyate śṛṇu rambhoru kokilārāvaḍiṇḍimaḥ |(p.55, l.4)
 madanasya nṛpasyeva vasantena dharātale || 14.5 (= 105) ||(p.55, l.5)

yataḥ |

vādyate śṛṇu rambhoru kokilārāvaḍiṇḍimaḥ | madanasya nṛpasyeva vasantena dharātale || 14.5 (= 105) ||
muñcantu māninaḥ sarve mānaṃ sevantu vallabhāḥ |(p.55, l.6)
 gatvaraṃ yauvanaṃ loke jīvitaṃ ca tathā calam || 14.6 (= 106) ||(p.55, l.7)
muñcantu māninaḥ sarve mānaṃ sevantu vallabhāḥ | gatvaraṃ yauvanaṃ loke jīvitaṃ ca tathā calam || 14.6 (= 106) ||

p.55, l.7

tatas tvam api kuru vayaḥsāphalyam ity ukte dhanaśrīr jagāda | nāhaṃ vilambituṃ (p.55, l.8)
sahāmi | yat tvayā bhavati tat śīghraṃ vidhehi | tatas tayā sā narāntareṇa (p.55, l.9)
yojitā | yadā ca sā tenātmāsaktā jñātā tadā tadīyaśiroveṇī (p.55, l.10)
chinnā | tatkāle ca patir deśāntarād ājagāma | tadā sā kathaṃ (p.55, l.11)
bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca patir gṛhadvāram āyayau tadā (p.56, l.1)
tayottaraṃ vicintyoktam | nātha tvayā tāvad gṛhadvāri sthīyatāṃ yāvat sarvaṃ (p.56, l.2)
sajjaṃ vidhīyate | tena caivaṃ pratipanne sā madhye gatvā bhaṭṭārikāṃ pūjayitvā (p.56, l.3)
purato veṇīṃ sthāpayām āsa | evaṃ kṛtvā bahir nirgatya caraṇamaṇḍakaiḥ (p.56, l.4)
patiṃ gṛhāntar devīpurato nītvā jagāda | nātha pūjaya gṛhādhidevatām | (p.56, l.5)
tena pūjayatā veṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā uktam | kim idam iti | (p.56, l.6)
tayoktam | mayopayācitam āsīt | yadā me patiḥ sameṣyati tadā (p.56, l.7)
svāminy ahaṃ tavāgre veṇīṃ chetsyāmi | tad adhunā mayā kṛtam | sa ca (p.56, l.8)
mugdho devīṃ namaskṛtya tāṃ bahumānayām āsa | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī (p.56, l.9)
suptā | (p.56, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau caturdaśī kathā || (p.56, l.11)

tatas tvam api kuru vayaḥsāphalyam ity ukte dhanaśrīr jagāda | nāhaṃ vilambituṃ sahāmi | yat tvayā bhavati tat śīghraṃ vidhehi | tatas tayā sā narāntareṇa yojitā | yadā ca sā tenātmāsaktā jñātā tadā tadīyaśiroveṇī chinnā | tatkāle ca patir deśāntarād ājagāma | tadā sā kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca patir gṛhadvāram āyayau tadā tayottaraṃ vicintyoktam | nātha tvayā tāvad gṛhadvāri sthīyatāṃ yāvat sarvaṃ sajjaṃ vidhīyate | tena caivaṃ pratipanne sā madhye gatvā bhaṭṭārikāṃ pūjayitvā purato veṇīṃ sthāpayām āsa | evaṃ kṛtvā bahir nirgatya caraṇamaṇḍakaiḥ patiṃ gṛhāntar devīpurato nītvā jagāda | nātha pūjaya gṛhādhidevatām | tena pūjayatā veṇīṃ dṛṣṭvā uktam | kim idam iti | tayoktam | mayopayācitam āsīt | yadā me patiḥ sameṣyati tadā svāminy ahaṃ tavāgre veṇīṃ chetsyāmi | tad adhunā mayā kṛtam | sa ca mugdho devīṃ namaskṛtya tāṃ bahumānayām āsa | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau caturdaśī kathā ||

p.57, l.1

jayikā | tayoḥ suto guṇākaro nāmābhūt | tadbhāryā śriyādevī | (p.57, l.3)

'pi saṃjāte 'nuraktas tadīyaḥ patir na kim api karṇe karoti | (p.57, l.5)

(•)

p.58, l.1

anyadā sā śvaśureṇa narāntarasahitā suptā dṛṣṭā | tataś caraṇān nūpuraṃ (p.58, l.2)
śvaśureṇa cottāritaṃ tayā ca jñātam | tataḥ sā taṃ jāraṃ prasthāpya (p.58, l.3)
bhartāraṃ tatrānīya tena saha suptā | nidrāntare ca patir utthāpitaḥ kathitaṃ (p.58, l.4)
ca | tvadīyena pitrā nūpuram asmatpadādavatārya gṛhītam | evaṃvidhaṃ (p.58, l.5)
ca pātakaṃ kvāpi na dṛṣṭaṃ yad vadhūpādāt śvaśuro nūpuraṃ gṛhṇāti | tenoktam | (p.58, l.6)
prātaḥ pituḥ sakāśāt svayam arpayiṣyāmi | tena ca guṇākareṇa (p.58, l.7)
pitaraṃ nirbhartsya tatsakāśān nūpuraṃ yācitam | pitrā coktam | yad iyaṃ (p.58, l.8)
parapuruṣeṇa saha suptā dṛṣṭā ato mayā nūpuraṃ gṛhītam | tayoktam | (p.58, l.9)
tvatputreṇa saha suptāham āsam | ityarthe divyaṃ karomi | atraiva grāme (p.58, l.10)
uttarasyāṃ diśi yakṣo 'sti | tasya jaṅghāntarān nirgamiṣyāmi | yaḥ (p.58, l.11)
kaścit satyo bhavati sa jaṅghayor antarān niṣkrāmyatīti prasiddham | evaṃ (p.59, l.1)
śvaśureṇa cāṅgīkṛte sā kulaṭāsati dine jārasya gṛhe gatvā tam uvāca | (p.59, l.2)
bhoḥ kānta prātar ahaṃ divyārthaṃ yakṣasya jaṅghāntarān nirgamiṣyāmi | tvayā (p.59, l.3)
tatra samāgatya vātūlatvam āśritya mama kaṇṭhagraho vidheyaḥ | tena ca (p.59, l.4)
tathokte sā svagṛham ājagāma | atha prātaḥ samastamahājanaṃ melayitvā (p.59, l.5)
puṣpākṣatādikam ādāya yakṣāyatane gatvā samīpasarasi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣapūjārthaṃ (p.59, l.6)
samāgacchantyās tasyāḥ pūrvasaṃketito jāro grahilībhūtas tatkaṇṭhe (p.59, l.7)
nijabāhudvayaṃ yojayām āsa | tata āḥ kim etad ity abhidhāya sā punaḥ (p.59, l.8)
snānārthaṃ yayau | so 'pi grahilo lokaiḥ kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā tasmāt pradeśād (p.59, l.9)
dūrīkṛtaḥ | sāpi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣasamīpam āgatya puṣpagandhādyair abhyarcya (p.59, l.10)
sarvalokānāṃ śṛṇvatām uvāca | bho bhagavan yakṣa nijabhartāram enaṃ ca grahilaṃ (p.59, l.11)
vinā yady anyapuruṣaḥ spṛśati kadācana māṃ tadā tava jaṅghābhyāṃ sakāśān (p.59, l.12)
mama niṣkramaṇaṃ mā bhavatv ity abhidhāya sarvalokasamakṣam eva jaṅghayor madhye (p.59, l.13)
praviśya niṣkrāntā | yakṣo 'pi tadbuddhiṃ manasi ślāghamāna eva sthitaḥ | (p.59, l.14)
sāpi satīti samastalokaiḥ pūjitā svabhavanaṃ jagāma | evaṃ cet śriyādevīvat (p.59, l.15)
kartuṃ jānāsi tadā vraja | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.59, l.16)
iti śukasaptatau pañcadaśī kathā ||

anyadā sā śvaśureṇa narāntarasahitā suptā dṛṣṭā | tataś caraṇān nūpuraṃ śvaśureṇa cottāritaṃ tayā ca jñātam | tataḥ sā taṃ jāraṃ prasthāpya bhartāraṃ tatrānīya tena saha suptā | nidrāntare ca patir utthāpitaḥ kathitaṃ ca | tvadīyena pitrā nūpuram asmatpadādavatārya gṛhītam | evaṃvidhaṃ ca pātakaṃ kvāpi na dṛṣṭaṃ yad vadhūpādāt śvaśuro nūpuraṃ gṛhṇāti | tenoktam | prātaḥ pituḥ sakāśāt svayam arpayiṣyāmi | tena ca guṇākareṇa pitaraṃ nirbhartsya tatsakāśān nūpuraṃ yācitam | pitrā coktam | yad iyaṃ parapuruṣeṇa saha suptā dṛṣṭā ato mayā nūpuraṃ gṛhītam | tayoktam | tvatputreṇa saha suptāham āsam | ityarthe divyaṃ karomi | atraiva grāme uttarasyāṃ diśi yakṣo 'sti | tasya jaṅghāntarān nirgamiṣyāmi | yaḥ kaścit satyo bhavati sa jaṅghayor antarān niṣkrāmyatīti prasiddham | evaṃ śvaśureṇa cāṅgīkṛte sā kulaṭāsati dine jārasya gṛhe gatvā tam uvāca | bhoḥ kānta prātar ahaṃ divyārthaṃ yakṣasya jaṅghāntarān nirgamiṣyāmi | tvayā tatra samāgatya vātūlatvam āśritya mama kaṇṭhagraho vidheyaḥ | tena ca tathokte sā svagṛham ājagāma | atha prātaḥ samastamahājanaṃ melayitvā puṣpākṣatādikam ādāya yakṣāyatane gatvā samīpasarasi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣapūjārthaṃ samāgacchantyās tasyāḥ pūrvasaṃketito jāro grahilībhūtas tatkaṇṭhe nijabāhudvayaṃ yojayām āsa | tata āḥ kim etad ity abhidhāya sā punaḥ snānārthaṃ yayau | so 'pi grahilo lokaiḥ kaṇṭhe gṛhītvā tasmāt pradeśād dūrīkṛtaḥ | sāpi snānaṃ kṛtvā yakṣasamīpam āgatya puṣpagandhādyair abhyarcya sarvalokānāṃ śṛṇvatām uvāca | bho bhagavan yakṣa nijabhartāram enaṃ ca grahilaṃ vinā yady anyapuruṣaḥ spṛśati kadācana māṃ tadā tava jaṅghābhyāṃ sakāśān mama niṣkramaṇaṃ mā bhavatv ity abhidhāya sarvalokasamakṣam eva jaṅghayor madhye praviśya niṣkrāntā | yakṣo 'pi tadbuddhiṃ manasi ślāghamāna eva sthitaḥ | sāpi satīti samastalokaiḥ pūjitā svabhavanaṃ jagāma | evaṃ cet śriyādevīvat kartuṃ jānāsi tadā vraja | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcadaśī kathā ||

(p.60, l.1)

p.60, l.1

śukaḥ prāha | (p.60, l.3)

anyadā sā calitā śukaṃ prāha | śukāhaṃ narāntaraṃ gamiṣyāmi | śukaḥ prāha |

p.60, l.3

satyam eva tvayābhāṇi kartavyaṃ yan mano 'nugam |(p.60, l.4)
 manas tu mugdhikā yadvad aśakyān khedayaty alam || 16.1 (= 110) ||(p.60, l.5)
satyam eva tvayābhāṇi kartavyaṃ yan mano 'nugam | manas tu mugdhikā yadvad aśakyān khedayaty alam || 16.1 (= 110) ||

p.60, l.5

tac chrutvā prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | so 'bravīt | asti vidiśā nāma (p.60, l.6)
purī | tasyāṃ janavallabho nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā mugdhikā nāma (p.60, l.7)
capalā svairiṇī | yadā ca tayātiśayena vidūṣito 'yaṃ tadā bandhūnāṃ (p.60, l.8)
kathayām āsa yad iyaṃ bahiḥ śāyinī | yadā ca tair evam uktā tadā tayāpy (p.60, l.9)
uktam | ayam eva bahiḥśāyī sadaiva | māṃ mudhāpavādayati | tatas (p.60, l.10)
tair militvā nirbandhaḥ kṛtaḥ | yaḥ ko 'pi adyaprabhṛti bahiḥ śāyī so (p.60, l.11)
'parādhī | evaṃ nirbandhe kṛte 'pi sā suptaṃ patiṃ vihāya bahir gatā | (p.61, l.1)
tasyāṃ ca bahir gatāyāṃ sa patir dvāraṃ dattvā suptaḥ | yadā ca bahiḥ krīḍāṃ (p.61, l.2)
kṛtvā samāgatāyāḥ sa patir dvāraṃ nodghāṭayati tadā sā kūpe dṛṣadaṃ kṣiptvā (p.61, l.3)
dvāradeśa eva sthitā | patir api kūpe patitā bhaviṣyatīti jñātvā (p.61, l.4)
dvāram udghāṭya bahir nirgataḥ | tadā sā dvāraṃ pidhāya madhye sthitā | so (p.61, l.5)
'pi ca bahiḥ sthito hā priye evaṃ vadan mahatā śabdena roditum ārabdhaḥ | (p.61, l.6)
sāpi vigopakabhayād bahir nirgatya patiṃ madhye nināya | tatas tan mithunaṃ (p.61, l.7)
parasparaṃ nirbandhaṃ cakāra | yad adyaprabhṛti mayā tvayā ca visaṃvādo na (p.61, l.8)
vidheyaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.61, l.9)
iti śukasaptatau ṣoḍaśī kathā || (p.61, l.10)

tac chrutvā prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | so 'bravīt | asti vidiśā nāma purī | tasyāṃ janavallabho nāma vaṇik | tasya bhāryā mugdhikā nāma capalā svairiṇī | yadā ca tayātiśayena vidūṣito 'yaṃ tadā bandhūnāṃ kathayām āsa yad iyaṃ bahiḥ śāyinī | yadā ca tair evam uktā tadā tayāpy uktam | ayam eva bahiḥśāyī sadaiva | māṃ mudhāpavādayati | tatas tair militvā nirbandhaḥ kṛtaḥ | yaḥ ko 'pi adyaprabhṛti bahiḥ śāyī so 'parādhī | evaṃ nirbandhe kṛte 'pi sā suptaṃ patiṃ vihāya bahir gatā | tasyāṃ ca bahir gatāyāṃ sa patir dvāraṃ dattvā suptaḥ | yadā ca bahiḥ krīḍāṃ kṛtvā samāgatāyāḥ sa patir dvāraṃ nodghāṭayati tadā sā kūpe dṛṣadaṃ kṣiptvā dvāradeśa eva sthitā | patir api kūpe patitā bhaviṣyatīti jñātvā dvāram udghāṭya bahir nirgataḥ | tadā sā dvāraṃ pidhāya madhye sthitā | so 'pi ca bahiḥ sthito hā priye evaṃ vadan mahatā śabdena roditum ārabdhaḥ | sāpi vigopakabhayād bahir nirgatya patiṃ madhye nināya | tatas tan mithunaṃ parasparaṃ nirbandhaṃ cakāra | yad adyaprabhṛti mayā tvayā ca visaṃvādo na vidheyaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣoḍaśī kathā ||

§ 17

p.61, l.10

anyadā sā hasantī narāntaragamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka āha | (p.61, l.11)
yad eva manaso 'bhīṣṭaṃ tad eva kāryam | (p.61, l.12)

anyadā sā hasantī narāntaragamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śuka āha | yad eva manaso 'bhīṣṭaṃ tad eva kāryam |

p.61, l.12

uktaṃ ca |

dṛṣṭipūtaṃ nyaset pādaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet |(p.61, l.13)
 satyapūtaṃ vaded vākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret || 17.1 (= 111) ||(p.62, l.1)

uktaṃ ca |

dṛṣṭipūtaṃ nyaset pādaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet | satyapūtaṃ vaded vākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret || 17.1 (= 111) ||
mano 'nukūlaṃ kurvantu tanvi te duḥkham āgatam |(p.62, l.2)
 soḍhuṃ śaktās tathā vaktuṃ guṇāḍhyo brāhmaṇo yathā || 17.2 (= 112) ||(p.62, l.3)
mano 'nukūlaṃ kurvantu tanvi te duḥkham āgatam | soḍhuṃ śaktās tathā vaktuṃ guṇāḍhyo brāhmaṇo yathā || 17.2 (= 112) ||

p.62, l.3

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā purī | (p.62, l.4)
tatra yāyajūko brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya patnī pāhinī nāma surūpā ativallabhā | (p.62, l.5)
tatputraḥ pitrā sarvām api kramād vidyāṃ grāhitaḥ | anyadā sa (p.62, l.6)
pitarau muktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | guṇāḍhya iti viśruto babhūva | jayantyāṃ (p.62, l.7)
ca nagaryāṃ buddhijīvanaṃ vyacintayat | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaṃ yavakāśādibhiḥ pupoṣa | (p.62, l.8)
so 'pi ṣaṇḍas tam anu paribhramati | anyadā sabandhanaṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ vidhāya (p.62, l.9)
vaṇijārakaveṣadhārī madanāyā veśyāyāḥ kuṭṭinīṃ jagāda | asmadīyā (p.62, l.10)
balīvardāḥ savastukāḥ prātar eṣyanti | adyāhaṃ tṛṇānayanārtham āgataḥ | (p.62, l.11)
tad yatra asmadīyasya balīvardasya sthānaṃ bhavati tatrāhaṃ svapimi | (p.63, l.1)
ity ukte sā kuṭṭinī balīvardadhanaiṣiṇī taṃ sthāpayām āsa | so 'pi taṃ (p.63, l.2)
ṣaṇḍaṃ baddhvā vilāsinīpārśve yayau | tayā ca snāpito bhojitaś ca (p.63, l.3)
guṇāḍhyo rajanyāṃ śṛṅgāritaḥ tatsakāśe sthitaḥ | so 'pi ca prabhātāyāṃ (p.63, l.4)
niśi prathamam evotthāya svarṇaśṛṅkhalaṃ gṛhītvā jagāma | gate ca (p.63, l.5)
tasminn ekā ceṭī utthitā ṣaṇḍam adṛṣṭvā kuṭṭinīṃ pratyāha | āue kim (p.63, l.6)
idam | tatas taṃ vilāsinīpārśvād gataṃ jñātvā maunaṃ vidhāya sthitā | (p.63, l.7)

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti viśālā purī | tatra yāyajūko brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya patnī pāhinī nāma surūpā ativallabhā | tatputraḥ pitrā sarvām api kramād vidyāṃ grāhitaḥ | anyadā sa pitarau muktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | guṇāḍhya iti viśruto babhūva | jayantyāṃ ca nagaryāṃ buddhijīvanaṃ vyacintayat | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaṃ yavakāśādibhiḥ pupoṣa | so 'pi ṣaṇḍas tam anu paribhramati | anyadā sabandhanaṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ vidhāya vaṇijārakaveṣadhārī madanāyā veśyāyāḥ kuṭṭinīṃ jagāda | asmadīyā balīvardāḥ savastukāḥ prātar eṣyanti | adyāhaṃ tṛṇānayanārtham āgataḥ | tad yatra asmadīyasya balīvardasya sthānaṃ bhavati tatrāhaṃ svapimi | ity ukte sā kuṭṭinī balīvardadhanaiṣiṇī taṃ sthāpayām āsa | so 'pi taṃ ṣaṇḍaṃ baddhvā vilāsinīpārśve yayau | tayā ca snāpito bhojitaś ca guṇāḍhyo rajanyāṃ śṛṅgāritaḥ tatsakāśe sthitaḥ | so 'pi ca prabhātāyāṃ niśi prathamam evotthāya svarṇaśṛṅkhalaṃ gṛhītvā jagāma | gate ca tasminn ekā ceṭī utthitā ṣaṇḍam adṛṣṭvā kuṭṭinīṃ pratyāha | āue kim idam | tatas taṃ vilāsinīpārśvād gataṃ jñātvā maunaṃ vidhāya sthitā |

p.63, l.7

uktaṃ ca |

arthanāśaṃ manastāpaṃ gṛhe duścaritāni ca |(p.63, l.8)
 vañcanaṃ cāpamānaṃ ca matimān na prakāśayet || 17.3 (= 113) ||(p.63, l.9)

uktaṃ ca |

arthanāśaṃ manastāpaṃ gṛhe duścaritāni ca | vañcanaṃ cāpamānaṃ ca matimān na prakāśayet || 17.3 (= 113) ||

p.63, l.9

anyadā guṇāḍhyo dyūtanirjitaḥ khaṭikāhasto veśyayā dhṛtaḥ | tenopāyaś (p.63, l.10)
cintitaḥ | śambalī śambalīti jagāda | tatas tayā rājabhayān muktaḥ | (p.63, l.11)
tatas tasyāṃ calitāyāṃ pṛṣṭhalagna eva śambalīti vadan gacchati | tatas (p.63, l.12)
tayā vijane nītvā hastāt prasādya svarṇābharaṇaṃ dattam | (p.64, l.1)

anyadā guṇāḍhyo dyūtanirjitaḥ khaṭikāhasto veśyayā dhṛtaḥ | tenopāyaś cintitaḥ | śambalī śambalīti jagāda | tatas tayā rājabhayān muktaḥ | tatas tasyāṃ calitāyāṃ pṛṣṭhalagna eva śambalīti vadan gacchati | tatas tayā vijane nītvā hastāt prasādya svarṇābharaṇaṃ dattam |

p.64, l.1

soḍhuṃ tyaktuṃ ca yaḥ śakto manasā kṛtam anyathā |(p.64, l.2)
 mano 'nukūlatāṃ kurvan na sa nindyaḥ sadā satām || 17.4 (= 114) ||(p.64, l.3)

p.64, l.8

asti śubhasthānaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra daridro nāma vaṇik | tasya (p.64, l.9)
gṛhe cauraḥ praviṣṭaḥ | so 'pi ca tatrānyat kim apy alabhamānaḥ sarṣapān (p.64, l.10)
gṛhītvā nirgato rājapuruṣaiḥ prāptaḥ | sarṣapān gale baddhvā bhrāmito (p.64, l.11)
rājakulāt sa kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | yo yaḥ pṛcchati tasya tasyāgre (p.64, l.12)
vadati | aho sarṣapāṇāṃ madhye na kiṃcit | tato rājñā sabhāyām (p.64, l.13)
ākārya pṛṣṭaḥ | tava vaco 'bhiprāyaṃ na jāne | sa prāha | (p.65, l.1)

asti śubhasthānaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra daridro nāma vaṇik | tasya gṛhe cauraḥ praviṣṭaḥ | so 'pi ca tatrānyat kim apy alabhamānaḥ sarṣapān gṛhītvā nirgato rājapuruṣaiḥ prāptaḥ | sarṣapān gale baddhvā bhrāmito rājakulāt sa kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | yo yaḥ pṛcchati tasya tasyāgre vadati | aho sarṣapāṇāṃ madhye na kiṃcit | tato rājñā sabhāyām ākārya pṛṣṭaḥ | tava vaco 'bhiprāyaṃ na jāne | sa prāha |

p.65, l.1

 haste badhnāti tan nūnam apramāṇam ataḥ param || 18.2 (= 116) ||(p.65, l.3)
baler varṣadine lokaḥ sarṣapān pañca rakṣakān | haste badhnāti tan nūnam apramāṇam ataḥ param || 18.2 (= 116) ||

kuru yad rocate bhīru yadi kartuṃ tvam īśvarā |(p.65, l.8)
 yathā santikayā bhartā svacchandā ca vimocitāḥ || 19.1 (= 117) ||(p.65, l.9)

p.65, l.9

asti karahaḍābhidhaṃ puram | tatra rājā guṇapriyo nāma yathārthaḥ | (p.65, l.10)
tatra ca soḍhāko nāma śreṣṭhiḥ | tadbhāryā santikā nāma pativratā | (p.65, l.11)
tatraiva cānyo vaṇik | tadbhāryā svacchandā nāma puṃścalī | (p.66, l.1)
sā ca soḍhākaṃ nityam icchati paraṃ so 'bhivāñchāṃ na vidhatte | anyadā (p.66, l.2)
ca manorathābhidhaṃ yakṣaṃ namaskartuṃ jagāma saḥ | tataḥ svacchandā pṛṣṭhalagnā (p.66, l.3)
tatra praviṣṭā | sa ca hāvabhāvādyair anukūlito bhuktaḥ | (p.66, l.4)

asti karahaḍābhidhaṃ puram | tatra rājā guṇapriyo nāma yathārthaḥ | tatra ca soḍhāko nāma śreṣṭhiḥ | tadbhāryā santikā nāma pativratā | tatraiva cānyo vaṇik | tadbhāryā svacchandā nāma puṃścalī | sā ca soḍhākaṃ nityam icchati paraṃ so 'bhivāñchāṃ na vidhatte | anyadā ca manorathābhidhaṃ yakṣaṃ namaskartuṃ jagāma saḥ | tataḥ svacchandā pṛṣṭhalagnā tatra praviṣṭā | sa ca hāvabhāvādyair anukūlito bhuktaḥ |

p.66, l.4

yuktam uktaṃ ca |

sanmārge tāvad āste prabhavati puruṣas tāvad evendriyāṇāṃ(p.66, l.5)
lajjāṃ tāvad vidhatte vinayam api samālambate tāvad eva |(p.66, l.6)
 bhrūcāpākṛṣṭamuktāḥ śravaṇapathajuṣo nīlapakṣmāṇa ete(p.66, l.7)
yāval līlāvatīnāṃ na hṛdi dhṛtimuṣo dṛṣṭibāṇāḥ patanti || 19.2 (= 118) ||(p.66, l.8)

yuktam uktaṃ ca |

sanmārge tāvad āste prabhavati puruṣas tāvad evendriyāṇāṃ lajjāṃ tāvad vidhatte vinayam api samālambate tāvad eva | bhrūcāpākṛṣṭamuktāḥ śravaṇapathajuṣo nīlapakṣmāṇa ete yāval līlāvatīnāṃ na hṛdi dhṛtimuṣo dṛṣṭibāṇāḥ patanti || 19.2 (= 118) ||

p.66, l.8

tac ca mithunaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā rājapuruṣaiḥ tadbandhanāya yakṣagṛhaṃ veṣṭitam | (p.66, l.9)
santikā ca śuddhiṃ jñātvā rātrau mahatā tūryaśabdena yakṣagṛhaṃ gatā | (p.66, l.10)
teṣām ārakṣakāṇāṃ purata uktam | aham adyadinavratā yakṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhojanaṃ (p.66, l.11)
vijane vidhāsye | māṃ ca kiṃcid dhanaṃ gṛhītvā madhye praveśayata | tair api (p.66, l.12)
tathaiva kṛtam | tatas tayā svacchandā svaveṣāṃ kārayitvā bahir niṣkāsitā | (p.67, l.1)
svayaṃ te madhye sthitā | taṃ ca prātar nijakāntāsahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ārakṣakā (p.67, l.2)
vilakṣībabhūvuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.67, l.3)
iti śukasaptatau ekonaviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.67, l.4)

tac ca mithunaṃ tathā dṛṣṭvā rājapuruṣaiḥ tadbandhanāya yakṣagṛhaṃ veṣṭitam | santikā ca śuddhiṃ jñātvā rātrau mahatā tūryaśabdena yakṣagṛhaṃ gatā | teṣām ārakṣakāṇāṃ purata uktam | aham adyadinavratā yakṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhojanaṃ vijane vidhāsye | māṃ ca kiṃcid dhanaṃ gṛhītvā madhye praveśayata | tair api tathaiva kṛtam | tatas tayā svacchandā svaveṣāṃ kārayitvā bahir niṣkāsitā | svayaṃ te madhye sthitā | taṃ ca prātar nijakāntāsahitaṃ dṛṣṭvā ārakṣakā vilakṣībabhūvuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.67, l.7

asti sābhramatyā nadyās taṭe śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma sthānam | tatra ca karṣukaḥ (p.67, l.8)
sūrākhyo dhanī | tasya kelikā bhāryā paraṃ kuṭilā kulaṭā ca | (p.67, l.9)
sānyasmin nadītīre siddheśvarapurasthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāmayate | tadāsaktā ca (p.68, l.1)
rātrau prātiveśikādūtikāsāhāyyān nadīṃ tīrtvā tadantikaṃ prāpnoti | (p.68, l.2)
anyadā bhartrā jñātam | sa ca tatra gatas taccaritragaveṣaṇāya | yāvat sā (p.68, l.3)
nadītīre tatra samāgatā tayā sa tāvad dṛṣṭaḥ | tatas taraṇaghaṭaṃ pānīyabhṛtaṃ (p.68, l.4)
vidhāya prātiveśmikāgṛhamadhye bhaṭṭārikāṃ maṇḍayitvā tena payasā (p.68, l.5)
snāpayitvā pratyuvāca prathamasaṃketitāṃ dūtikām uddiśya | svāmini purā (p.68, l.6)
tvayā uktam | yadi tvaṃ siddheśvarīṃ na snāpayasi tataḥ pañcānāṃ dinānāṃ (p.68, l.7)
madhye tvadbhartṛmaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tato yadi tvadvacanapramāṇaṃ tadā (p.68, l.8)
mama patiś ciraṃ jīvatu | prātiveśmikayoktam | evam astv iti śrutvā (p.68, l.9)
sa patis tuṣṭo bhūtvālakṣita eva jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī (p.68, l.10)
suptā | (p.68, l.11)
iti śukasaptatau viṃśatitamī kathā ||

asti sābhramatyā nadyās taṭe śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma sthānam | tatra ca karṣukaḥ sūrākhyo dhanī | tasya kelikā bhāryā paraṃ kuṭilā kulaṭā ca | sānyasmin nadītīre siddheśvarapurasthaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ kāmayate | tadāsaktā ca rātrau prātiveśikādūtikāsāhāyyān nadīṃ tīrtvā tadantikaṃ prāpnoti | anyadā bhartrā jñātam | sa ca tatra gatas taccaritragaveṣaṇāya | yāvat sā nadītīre tatra samāgatā tayā sa tāvad dṛṣṭaḥ | tatas taraṇaghaṭaṃ pānīyabhṛtaṃ vidhāya prātiveśmikāgṛhamadhye bhaṭṭārikāṃ maṇḍayitvā tena payasā snāpayitvā pratyuvāca prathamasaṃketitāṃ dūtikām uddiśya | svāmini purā tvayā uktam | yadi tvaṃ siddheśvarīṃ na snāpayasi tataḥ pañcānāṃ dinānāṃ madhye tvadbhartṛmaraṇaṃ bhaviṣyati | tato yadi tvadvacanapramāṇaṃ tadā mama patiś ciraṃ jīvatu | prātiveśmikayoktam | evam astv iti śrutvā sa patis tuṣṭo bhūtvālakṣita eva jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau viṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.69, l.2

 buddhir asti yadā yeṣāṃ mandodaryāḥ sahāyinī || 21.1 (= 118bis) ||(p.69, l.4)

p.69, l.4

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti pratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma nagaram | (p.69, l.5)
tatra hemaprabho nāma rājā | śrutaśīlo mantrī | śreṣṭhī yaśodharaḥ | (p.69, l.6)
mohinī bhāryā | tayos tanayā mandodarī | sa śrīvatsāya vaṇije (p.69, l.7)
kāntipurīsamāgatāya dattā | tanmithunam atīva snehalampaṭam | sā ca (p.69, l.8)
prātiveśmikayā pitṛbhāryayā kuṭṭinyā daṃṣṭrākarālayā yojitam anyaṃ rājaputram (p.69, l.9)
upabhuṅkte | sā cāpannasattvā bhūtā garbhasaṃbhavāt saṃjāte dohade rājavallabhaṃ (p.69, l.10)
mayūraṃ mārayitvā bhakṣitavatī | rājā tu tasmin mayūre samāgate (p.70, l.1)
bhuṅkte iti sthitiḥ | tasmin divase tu bhojanavelāyāṃ na labdhaḥ | ḍiṇḍimaghoṣaṇe (p.70, l.2)
kṛte kuṭṭinyā paṭahaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tayā ca jñātaṃ yat kayācid (p.70, l.3)
āpannasattvayā mayūro dohadādbhakṣitaḥ | tataḥ sā garbhavatī pṛṣṭā | (p.70, l.4)
tayā kuṭṭinī gṛham āgatā saṃmānitā | (p.70, l.5)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti pratiṣṭhānaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra hemaprabho nāma rājā | śrutaśīlo mantrī | śreṣṭhī yaśodharaḥ | mohinī bhāryā | tayos tanayā mandodarī | sa śrīvatsāya vaṇije kāntipurīsamāgatāya dattā | tanmithunam atīva snehalampaṭam | sā ca prātiveśmikayā pitṛbhāryayā kuṭṭinyā daṃṣṭrākarālayā yojitam anyaṃ rājaputram upabhuṅkte | sā cāpannasattvā bhūtā garbhasaṃbhavāt saṃjāte dohade rājavallabhaṃ mayūraṃ mārayitvā bhakṣitavatī | rājā tu tasmin mayūre samāgate bhuṅkte iti sthitiḥ | tasmin divase tu bhojanavelāyāṃ na labdhaḥ | ḍiṇḍimaghoṣaṇe kṛte kuṭṭinyā paṭahaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tayā ca jñātaṃ yat kayācid āpannasattvayā mayūro dohadādbhakṣitaḥ | tataḥ sā garbhavatī pṛṣṭā | tayā kuṭṭinī gṛham āgatā saṃmānitā |

 marmajñeṣv anuvartanaṃ bahuvidhā mānaṃ jane garvite(p.70, l.8)

p.71, l.11

tad vaṇijo nagarapradhānasya vadhvā naitan niṣpadyate | yāvad ātmanā na dṛṣṭaṃ (p.71, l.12)

ca mantriṇaṃ peṭāyāṃ nikṣipya tadgṛhe nyāsavyājena mumoca | (p.72, l.2)

ślāghyā | (p.72, l.4)

p.72, l.6

punar api samagro vṛttāntaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ | kathyamānaś ca peṭāhananakṛtasaṃjñena mantriṇā (p.72, l.7)
śrutaḥ | tat kathaṃ sā śreṣṭhivadhūs tatpitā śvaśuraś ca mucyantām | (p.72, l.8)

punar api samagro vṛttāntaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ | kathyamānaś ca peṭāhananakṛtasaṃjñena mantriṇā śrutaḥ | tat kathaṃ sā śreṣṭhivadhūs tatpitā śvaśuraś ca mucyantām |

p.72, l.8

uktaṃ ca |

na nīcajanasaṃsargān naro bhadrāṇi paśyati |(p.72, l.9)
 darśayaty eva vikṛtiṃ supriye 'pi khalo yataḥ || 21.9 (= 126) ||(p.72, l.10)

uktaṃ ca |

na nīcajanasaṃsargān naro bhadrāṇi paśyati | darśayaty eva vikṛtiṃ supriye 'pi khalo yataḥ || 21.9 (= 126) ||
nāśayitum eva nīcaḥ parakāryaṃ vetti na prasādhayitum |(p.72, l.11)
 pāṭayitum eva śaktir nākhor uddhartum annapiṭam || 21.10 (= 127) ||(p.73, l.1)
nāśayitum eva nīcaḥ parakāryaṃ vetti na prasādhayitum | pāṭayitum eva śaktir nākhor uddhartum annapiṭam || 21.10 (= 127) ||
dujjaṇajaṇasaṃsagge kāaccāo vi hoi vibuhāṇaṃ |(p.73, l.2)
 pecchaha tilehi pattaṃ khalasaṅge pīḍaṇaṃ jatto || 21.11 (= 128) ||

(•)

dujjaṇajaṇasaṃsagge kāaccāo vi hoi vibuhāṇaṃ | pecchaha tilehi pattaṃ khalasaṅge pīḍaṇaṃ jatto || 21.11 (= 128) ||

(•)

p.73, l.3

yāvat sā kuṭṭinī peṭāṃ hastena hanti tāvat sā vaṇikputrī savitarkam avādīt | (p.73, l.4)

yāvat sā kuṭṭinī peṭāṃ hastena hanti tāvat sā vaṇikputrī savitarkam avādīt |

p.73, l.5

vibhātā rajanī tāvad yāvad evaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā |(p.73, l.6)
 prabuddhaṃ ca tadā mātar nāgre kiṃcid vidṛśyate || 21.12 (= 129) ||(p.73, l.7)
vibhātā rajanī tāvad yāvad evaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā | prabuddhaṃ ca tadā mātar nāgre kiṃcid vidṛśyate || 21.12 (= 129) ||

p.73, l.6

mātar mayā evaṃvidhaḥ svapno dṛṣṭaḥ | yaḥ kaścid arthapramāṇo me bhavati sa (p.73, l.7)
kathyatām | evaṃ śrutvā mantrī dvāram āhatya bahir nirgataḥ | tataḥ sanmānitā (p.73, l.8)
vaṇigvadhūḥ | sā tu kuṭṭinīti nirvāsitā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā (p.73, l.9)
prabhāvatī suptā || (p.73, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau ekaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

mātar mayā evaṃvidhaḥ svapno dṛṣṭaḥ | yaḥ kaścid arthapramāṇo me bhavati sa kathyatām | evaṃ śrutvā mantrī dvāram āhatya bahir nirgataḥ | tataḥ sanmānitā vaṇigvadhūḥ | sā tu kuṭṭinīti nirvāsitā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā || iti śukasaptatau ekaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

§ 22

(p.74, l.1)

p.74, l.1

punaḥ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | (p.74, l.2)

punaḥ prabhāvatyā pṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha |

p.74, l.2

yāhi devi punar yāhi madīyaṃ matam īdṛśam |(p.74, l.3)
 yadi vetsy uttaraṃ kiṃcid yathā māḍhukayā kṛtam || 22.1 (= 130) ||(p.74, l.4)
yāhi devi punar yāhi madīyaṃ matam īdṛśam | yadi vetsy uttaraṃ kiṃcid yathā māḍhukayā kṛtam || 22.1 (= 130) ||

p.74, l.4

tac chrutvā prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | dāmbhilāgrāme soḍhāko (p.74, l.5)
karṣukaḥ | tadbhāryā māḍhukā nāma | tāṃ ca bhaktahāriṇīṃ pathi (p.74, l.6)
gacchantīm eko bahiḥ sūrapālākhyo naro bhuṅkte | sā kadācin mārge bhaktaṃ (p.74, l.7)
muktvā tena saha sthitā | tato mūladevena dhūrtena tasmin bhakte uṣṭrikā (p.74, l.8)
kṛtā | tayā ca evaṃjātaṃ bhaktam anutpāṭayitvā nītam | yāvac ca bhartrā (p.74, l.9)
uṣṭrikā dṛṣṭā tāvat kim idam iti sā pṛṣṭā | tatas tayā tatkālottaraṃ (p.75, l.1)
kṛtvoktam | nāthādya rātrau svapne uṣṭrikayā bhakṣito dṛṣṭas tvam | tato (p.75, l.2)
mayā vighnāpahārāya viparītam idaṃ kṛtam | viśrabdhaṃ bhakṣaya yathā vighno (p.75, l.3)
naśyati | iti śrutvā ratātmanā tenoṣṭrikāpi bhakṣitā | iti kathāṃ (p.75, l.4)
śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.75, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau dvāviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.75, l.6)

tac chrutvā prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | dāmbhilāgrāme soḍhāko karṣukaḥ | tadbhāryā māḍhukā nāma | tāṃ ca bhaktahāriṇīṃ pathi gacchantīm eko bahiḥ sūrapālākhyo naro bhuṅkte | sā kadācin mārge bhaktaṃ muktvā tena saha sthitā | tato mūladevena dhūrtena tasmin bhakte uṣṭrikā kṛtā | tayā ca evaṃjātaṃ bhaktam anutpāṭayitvā nītam | yāvac ca bhartrā uṣṭrikā dṛṣṭā tāvat kim idam iti sā pṛṣṭā | tatas tayā tatkālottaraṃ kṛtvoktam | nāthādya rātrau svapne uṣṭrikayā bhakṣito dṛṣṭas tvam | tato mayā vighnāpahārāya viparītam idaṃ kṛtam | viśrabdhaṃ bhakṣaya yathā vighno naśyati | iti śrutvā ratātmanā tenoṣṭrikāpi bhakṣitā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvāviṃśatitamī kathā ||

 bhātīva vidrumaghaṭaḥ srastaḥ saṃdhyāvadhūkarāt || 23.14 (= 144) ||(p.78, l.13)

 udayādriśiraḥ sthātum udyato 'ṃśubhaṭair vṛtaḥ || 23.15 (= 145) ||(p.79, l.1)

p.79, l.5

p.80, l.2

ity uktvā dhūrtamāyāṃ kuṭṭinīm ākāryedam abravīt | tava kanakasahasraṃ dāsye | (p.80, l.3)
mama putraṃ strīmāyāvañcanadakṣaṃ kuru | tatheti tayā pratijñāte putraṃ (p.80, l.4)
sasākṣikaṃ tasyai dattvā yady asmatputraḥ kvāpi veśyāyāḥ kapaṭena jito (p.80, l.5)
bhavati tadāhaṃ dviguṇaṃ kanakaṃ grahīṣye | tayoktam evam astv iti | lekhayitvā (p.80, l.6)
putraṃ tadgṛhe preṣayām āsa | sa ca tatrastho veśyājanodbhavān vikārān (p.80, l.7)
gṛhṇāti | (p.80, l.8)

ity uktvā dhūrtamāyāṃ kuṭṭinīm ākāryedam abravīt | tava kanakasahasraṃ dāsye | mama putraṃ strīmāyāvañcanadakṣaṃ kuru | tatheti tayā pratijñāte putraṃ sasākṣikaṃ tasyai dattvā yady asmatputraḥ kvāpi veśyāyāḥ kapaṭena jito bhavati tadāhaṃ dviguṇaṃ kanakaṃ grahīṣye | tayoktam evam astv iti | lekhayitvā putraṃ tadgṛhe preṣayām āsa | sa ca tatrastho veśyājanodbhavān vikārān gṛhṇāti |

p.80, l.8

tad yathā |

 kauṭilyaṃ kṛtrimaṃ bhāvaṃ kṛtrimaṃ ruditaṃ tathā || 23.20 (= 150) ||(p.80, l.10)

tad yathā |

vaiśikīṃ kṛtrimāṃ vāṇīṃ vyalīkān śapathāṃs tathā | kauṭilyaṃ kṛtrimaṃ bhāvaṃ kṛtrimaṃ ruditaṃ tathā || 23.20 (= 150) ||
hāsyaṃ ca kṛtrimaṃ duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ caivam apārthakam |(p.81, l.1)
 yācanaṃ vinayopetaṃ snehabhāvo nirīhatā || 23.21 (= 151) ||(p.81, l.2)

samatvaṃ sukhaduḥkheṣu dharmādharmasamakriyā |(p.81, l.3)
 bhujaṃgapurataś caiva kauṭilyakramadarśanam || 23.22 (= 152) ||(p.81, l.4)
samatvaṃ sukhaduḥkheṣu dharmādharmasamakriyā | bhujaṃgapurataś caiva kauṭilyakramadarśanam || 23.22 (= 152) ||

 itthiajaṇasāmaṇṇaṃ hiaaṃ jaṃ jassa taṃ tassa || 23.23 (= 153) ||

(•)

p.81, l.6

ity evamādi samagraṃ veśyānugaṃ caritaṃ śikṣitam | tataḥ sa putraḥ pratijñāpūrvaṃ (p.81, l.7)
vaṇije samarpitaḥ | pitur vākyena ca suvarṇadvīpe vāṇijyāya (p.81, l.8)
preṣitaḥ | tatra ca kalāvatī veśyā | tayā saha varṣam ekaṃ sthitaḥ | tāṃ (p.81, l.9)
vaiśikāni kurvantīṃ sa prāha | viśeṣaṃ vada | eva mamānujāpi vadati | (p.81, l.10)
tato bahubhir api vaiśikair na tatsarvasvaṃ gṛhītuṃ śaknoti | tatas tayā (p.82, l.1)
sarvam api mātur niveditam | mātāpi prāha | niścitam eṣa veśyāsutaḥ | nedṛśair (p.82, l.2)
gṛhyate | prapañcenaiva grāhyaḥ | tato yadāyaṃ svadeśaṃ gantukāmas tvām utkalāpayati (p.82, l.3)
tadā tvayā vācyam | aham api tatra yāsyāmi | yadi na (p.82, l.4)
nayasi tadā mariṣyāmīty uktvā kūpe jhampā deyā | tato 'sau prītas tvāṃ (p.82, l.5)
prati sarvaṃ dāsyati | tayoktam | mātar māṃ vinā taddravyeṇa kim | (p.82, l.6)

ity evamādi samagraṃ veśyānugaṃ caritaṃ śikṣitam | tataḥ sa putraḥ pratijñāpūrvaṃ vaṇije samarpitaḥ | pitur vākyena ca suvarṇadvīpe vāṇijyāya preṣitaḥ | tatra ca kalāvatī veśyā | tayā saha varṣam ekaṃ sthitaḥ | tāṃ vaiśikāni kurvantīṃ sa prāha | viśeṣaṃ vada | eva mamānujāpi vadati | tato bahubhir api vaiśikair na tatsarvasvaṃ gṛhītuṃ śaknoti | tatas tayā sarvam api mātur niveditam | mātāpi prāha | niścitam eṣa veśyāsutaḥ | nedṛśair gṛhyate | prapañcenaiva grāhyaḥ | tato yadāyaṃ svadeśaṃ gantukāmas tvām utkalāpayati tadā tvayā vācyam | aham api tatra yāsyāmi | yadi na nayasi tadā mariṣyāmīty uktvā kūpe jhampā deyā | tato 'sau prītas tvāṃ prati sarvaṃ dāsyati | tayoktam | mātar māṃ vinā taddravyeṇa kim |

p.87, l.3

tataḥ śreṣṭhī taṃ putraṃ preṣayāmāsāśu tayā samaṃ suvarṇadvīpe | tatas tasmin sarvo (p.87, l.4)
'pi paurajanaḥ prīto babhūva | sā ca kalāvatī sānukūlā taṃ vinayenājuhāva | (p.87, l.5)
tathā ca sa tayāvarjito yathāsau ātmāyattaḥ kṛtaḥ | (p.87, l.6)
dravyaṃ ca sarvaṃ gṛhītam | tataḥ sā dhūrtamāyā kuṭṭinī kiṃ karotu | (p.87, l.7)
iti praśnaḥ | sā prāha | śuka na jāne | tvaṃ vada | śukaḥ | yady adya na (p.87, l.8)
yāsi tadā kathayāmi | sā āha | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | yadā (p.87, l.9)
tasya sarvasvaṃ gṛhītaṃ tasmin samaye kaiścid dinaiś cāgre 'pi cāṇḍālarūpadhāriṇī (p.87, l.10)
dhūrtamāyā nityaṃ nityaṃ gaveṣamāṇaiva kiṃcit | anyadā sa kalāvatyā (p.87, l.11)
sahitaḥ khaṭvāyām upaviṣṭas tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | tāṃ dvāri dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya nāśayitum (p.87, l.12)
udyataḥ pūrvam eva saṃketitam | tam uttiṣṭhantam anu kalāvaty api utthitā | (p.88, l.1)
uktaś ca | kim idam iti | rāmas tām uvāca | bhadre iyaṃ mama jananī | (p.88, l.2)
ahaṃ ca hṛtārthako bahudinebhyo na tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | dhūrtamāyāpi taṃ saṃketasthaṃ (p.88, l.3)
dvārasthaiva saśaṅkā hastasaṃjñayā ājuhāva | (p.88, l.4)

tataḥ śreṣṭhī taṃ putraṃ preṣayāmāsāśu tayā samaṃ suvarṇadvīpe | tatas tasmin sarvo 'pi paurajanaḥ prīto babhūva | sā ca kalāvatī sānukūlā taṃ vinayenājuhāva | tathā ca sa tayāvarjito yathāsau ātmāyattaḥ kṛtaḥ | dravyaṃ ca sarvaṃ gṛhītam | tataḥ sā dhūrtamāyā kuṭṭinī kiṃ karotu | iti praśnaḥ | sā prāha | śuka na jāne | tvaṃ vada | śukaḥ | yady adya na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | sā āha | na yāsyāmi | śukaḥ | yadā tasya sarvasvaṃ gṛhītaṃ tasmin samaye kaiścid dinaiś cāgre 'pi cāṇḍālarūpadhāriṇī dhūrtamāyā nityaṃ nityaṃ gaveṣamāṇaiva kiṃcit | anyadā sa kalāvatyā sahitaḥ khaṭvāyām upaviṣṭas tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | tāṃ dvāri dṛṣṭvā sahasotthāya nāśayitum udyataḥ pūrvam eva saṃketitam | tam uttiṣṭhantam anu kalāvaty api utthitā | uktaś ca | kim idam iti | rāmas tām uvāca | bhadre iyaṃ mama jananī | ahaṃ ca hṛtārthako bahudinebhyo na tayā dṛṣṭaḥ | dhūrtamāyāpi taṃ saṃketasthaṃ dvārasthaiva saśaṅkā hastasaṃjñayā ājuhāva |

p.88, l.4

jagādeti cirāl labdho veśyāgṛhagato bhavān |(p.88, l.5)
 mlecchī bhūtā iyaṃ veśyā sarvasvaṃ me tvayā hṛtam || 23.37 (= 167) ||(p.88, l.6)
jagādeti cirāl labdho veśyāgṛhagato bhavān | mlecchī bhūtā iyaṃ veśyā sarvasvaṃ me tvayā hṛtam || 23.37 (= 167) ||

p.88, l.6

yāvad evaṃ gṛhāṅgaṇagatā śapati tāvat sa vaṇik cāṇḍālarūpīṃ samāgatya (p.88, l.7)
tatpādayoḥ patitaḥ | etac ca dṛṣṭvā kalāvatī kuṭṭinīsahitā tām gṛhamadhye (p.88, l.8)
nītvā pṛcchati sma | amba ko 'yam | kiṃjātīyaḥ | tvaṃ kā | tayoktam | (p.88, l.9)
padmāvatīpurīnāthasya rājñaḥ sudarśanasya mātaṅgī gāyinī aham | (p.88, l.10)
ayaṃ ca madīyaṃ dravyaṃ hṛtvā ihāgataḥ | tac ca tvayāptam | tan mayā jñātam | (p.88, l.11)
param adhunā sa samāgacchatu | tataḥ kuṭṭinī kalāvatīsahitā (p.88, l.12)
tatpādayor lagnā uvāca | gṛhāṇedaṃ dravyam | dhūrtamāyā prāha | nāhaṃ (p.89, l.1)
gṛhakoṇe grahīṣye | rājaviditaṃ grahīṣyāmi | tato veśyāmātāpi atiśayena (p.89, l.2)
bhītā mātaṅgīṃ pratijagāda | imāṃ matsutāṃ rakṣa rakṣa | (p.89, l.3)
pāramparyāgataṃ dravyaṃ gṛhāṇa sarvasvam | paraṃ māṃ maivaṃ viḍambaya | dhūrtamāyā (p.89, l.4)
āha | grahīṣye | tataḥ sā veśyayā kuṭṭinyā saha hastapādau (p.89, l.5)
gṛhītvā sammānitā | dhūrtamāyāpi nijaṃ tadīyaṃ ca dravyaṃ sarvasvaṃ gṛhītvā (p.89, l.6)
rāmeṇa saha potam āruhya svagṛham āgatya mahotsavam akārayat | (p.89, l.7)
iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.89, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau trayoviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.89, l.9)

yāvad evaṃ gṛhāṅgaṇagatā śapati tāvat sa vaṇik cāṇḍālarūpīṃ samāgatya tatpādayoḥ patitaḥ | etac ca dṛṣṭvā kalāvatī kuṭṭinīsahitā tām gṛhamadhye nītvā pṛcchati sma | amba ko 'yam | kiṃjātīyaḥ | tvaṃ kā | tayoktam | padmāvatīpurīnāthasya rājñaḥ sudarśanasya mātaṅgī gāyinī aham | ayaṃ ca madīyaṃ dravyaṃ hṛtvā ihāgataḥ | tac ca tvayāptam | tan mayā jñātam | param adhunā sa samāgacchatu | tataḥ kuṭṭinī kalāvatīsahitā tatpādayor lagnā uvāca | gṛhāṇedaṃ dravyam | dhūrtamāyā prāha | nāhaṃ gṛhakoṇe grahīṣye | rājaviditaṃ grahīṣyāmi | tato veśyāmātāpi atiśayena bhītā mātaṅgīṃ pratijagāda | imāṃ matsutāṃ rakṣa rakṣa | pāramparyāgataṃ dravyaṃ gṛhāṇa sarvasvam | paraṃ māṃ maivaṃ viḍambaya | dhūrtamāyā āha | grahīṣye | tataḥ sā veśyayā kuṭṭinyā saha hastapādau gṛhītvā sammānitā | dhūrtamāyāpi nijaṃ tadīyaṃ ca dravyaṃ sarvasvaṃ gṛhītvā rāmeṇa saha potam āruhya svagṛham āgatya mahotsavam akārayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau trayoviṃśatitamī kathā ||

 sajjanīva purā vaktuṃ bhartur agre kacagrahe || 24.1 (= 168) ||(p.90, l.2)

p.90, l.2

prabhāvaty āha | kim etat | kīro 'bravīt | asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | (p.90, l.3)
tatrābhūd vardhakiḥ sūrapālākhyaḥ śrīmān | tasya sajjanī nāma (p.90, l.4)
bhāryā atyantaṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tāṃ ca tadgṛhasthāṃ devako nāma ramate | (p.90, l.5)
iti lokād etad ākarṇya vardhakiḥ kapaṭena gṛhān nirgatya prātaḥ saṃdhyāyām ācchannaḥ (p.90, l.6)
samāgatya talpasyādhobhāge sthitaḥ | sā ca jāreṇa saha tatrārūḍhā (p.90, l.7)
patyā keśeṣu gṛhītā kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | sā patyā dhṛtā (p.90, l.8)
satī dvitīyapatimukham ālokya prāha | mayā tava kathitaṃ yad rathakāro (p.90, l.9)
mama patir gṛhe na vidyate | sa cāgatas tava tad eva aucityaṃ vidhāsyati | (p.91, l.1)
yady api pūrvaṃ patyā tvadīyaṃ dravyam apahṛtaṃ tathāpi kṣantavyam | rathakṛti (p.91, l.2)
samāgate tava gṛhaṃ gamiṣyāmi yuvayoḥ saṃgatiṃ vā kariṣye | nātra (p.91, l.3)
saṃśayaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.91, l.4)
iti śukasaptatau caturviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.91, l.5)

prabhāvaty āha | kim etat | kīro 'bravīt | asti candrapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatrābhūd vardhakiḥ sūrapālākhyaḥ śrīmān | tasya sajjanī nāma bhāryā atyantaṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tāṃ ca tadgṛhasthāṃ devako nāma ramate | iti lokād etad ākarṇya vardhakiḥ kapaṭena gṛhān nirgatya prātaḥ saṃdhyāyām ācchannaḥ samāgatya talpasyādhobhāge sthitaḥ | sā ca jāreṇa saha tatrārūḍhā patyā keśeṣu gṛhītā kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | sā patyā dhṛtā satī dvitīyapatimukham ālokya prāha | mayā tava kathitaṃ yad rathakāro mama patir gṛhe na vidyate | sa cāgatas tava tad eva aucityaṃ vidhāsyati | yady api pūrvaṃ patyā tvadīyaṃ dravyam apahṛtaṃ tathāpi kṣantavyam | rathakṛti samāgate tava gṛhaṃ gamiṣyāmi yuvayoḥ saṃgatiṃ vā kariṣye | nātra saṃśayaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau caturviṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.91, l.5

anyadā prabhāvatī śukaṃ gamanāya pṛcchati | śukaḥ prāha | (p.91, l.6)

p.91, l.6

kuru yad rocate kartuṃ yadi vetsi pratīṅgitam |(p.91, l.7)
 śvetāmbareṇa ruddhena yathā pūrvaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā || 25.1 (= 169) ||(p.91, l.8)
kuru yad rocate kartuṃ yadi vetsi pratīṅgitam | śvetāmbareṇa ruddhena yathā pūrvaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā || 25.1 (= 169) ||

p.91, l.8

asti candrapurī nāma nagarī | tatra siddhaseno nāma kṣapaṇako janapūjitaḥ | (p.91, l.9)
tasminn eva nagare 'nyaḥ sitapaṭo guṇināṃ mukhyaḥ samāgataḥ | (p.91, l.10)
tena ca guṇinā sarvo 'pi jana āvarjitaḥ śrāvakā apy ātmāyattāḥ (p.92, l.1)
kṛtāḥ | sa kṣapaṇako 'pi tasya pūjāṃ kriyamāṇām asahamānaḥ svayaṃ tadīyopāśraye (p.92, l.2)
veśyāṃ preṣayitvā asau veśyālubdho na suśīla iti śvetāmbarasya (p.92, l.3)
lokapravādam akarot | taddarśanāya janam ākārayām āsa | brūte ca | (p.92, l.4)
kṣapaṇakā eva brahmacāriṇaḥ śvetāmbarās tu viplutāḥ | so 'pi śvetāmbaro (p.92, l.5)
dīpāgninā upādhiṃ prajvālya prabhātaprāptāyāṃ rajanyāṃ nagnībhūya veśyāyā (p.92, l.6)
dattahasto nirgataḥ | tato lokāpavādaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | yad asau kṣapaṇako na (p.92, l.7)
sitavastraḥ | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.92, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau pañcaviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.92, l.9)

asti candrapurī nāma nagarī | tatra siddhaseno nāma kṣapaṇako janapūjitaḥ | tasminn eva nagare 'nyaḥ sitapaṭo guṇināṃ mukhyaḥ samāgataḥ | tena ca guṇinā sarvo 'pi jana āvarjitaḥ śrāvakā apy ātmāyattāḥ kṛtāḥ | sa kṣapaṇako 'pi tasya pūjāṃ kriyamāṇām asahamānaḥ svayaṃ tadīyopāśraye veśyāṃ preṣayitvā asau veśyālubdho na suśīla iti śvetāmbarasya lokapravādam akarot | taddarśanāya janam ākārayām āsa | brūte ca | kṣapaṇakā eva brahmacāriṇaḥ śvetāmbarās tu viplutāḥ | so 'pi śvetāmbaro dīpāgninā upādhiṃ prajvālya prabhātaprāptāyāṃ rajanyāṃ nagnībhūya veśyāyā dattahasto nirgataḥ | tato lokāpavādaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | yad asau kṣapaṇako na sitavastraḥ | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.94, l.8

asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra āryo vaṇig abhūt | tasya mohinī (p.94, l.9)
nāma bhāryā | tāṃ ca bahir gatāṃ kumukho nāma dhūrto ramate | tatpatinā (p.94, l.10)
cābhijñāyi | tatpatiś cātiśayena bhīruḥ | tato 'sau tāṃ bahir yāntīṃ (p.95, l.1)
nivārya pārśvasthita eva tiṣṭhati | tathāpi tayā dhūrtasya kathāpitam | (p.95, l.2)
māṃ rātrau bhartṛkhaṭvāsthitām arvāk suptāṃ bhaja tvam | tena tathā kṛtam | (p.95, l.3)
tac ca kurvan bhartrāsau puṃścihne dhṛtaḥ kathaṃ gacchatu | uttaram | dhṛtvā ca (p.95, l.4)
patiḥ prāha | pradīpam ānaya mayā cauro dhṛto 'sti | tayoktam | (p.95, l.5)
bahir yāntī bibhemy aham | enaṃ grahīṣye tvaṃ dīpam ānaya | tena ca tathā (p.95, l.6)
kṛtam | sā ca jāraṃ muktvā gṛhāntar baddhasya paṭṭakasya (?) jihvāṃ gṛhītvā (p.95, l.7)
tathaiva suptā yāvat patir lakuṭahasto dīpaṃ gṛhītvā samāyātaḥ pṛcchati | (p.95, l.8)
kim iyaṃ paṭṭakasya (?) jihvā | katham atra | tayoktam | kṣudhārto 'yam | (p.95, l.9)
anena muktā lālā kṛśā sthitā | uktipratyuktivādena nirjitaḥ | (p.95, l.10)
uktaś ca | hataka anena pauruṣeṇa kṣayaṃ vrajasi | iti nirbhartsito lajjitaś (p.95, l.11)
ca suptaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.95, l.12)
iti śukasaptatau saptaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra āryo vaṇig abhūt | tasya mohinī nāma bhāryā | tāṃ ca bahir gatāṃ kumukho nāma dhūrto ramate | tatpatinā cābhijñāyi | tatpatiś cātiśayena bhīruḥ | tato 'sau tāṃ bahir yāntīṃ nivārya pārśvasthita eva tiṣṭhati | tathāpi tayā dhūrtasya kathāpitam | māṃ rātrau bhartṛkhaṭvāsthitām arvāk suptāṃ bhaja tvam | tena tathā kṛtam | tac ca kurvan bhartrāsau puṃścihne dhṛtaḥ kathaṃ gacchatu | uttaram | dhṛtvā ca patiḥ prāha | pradīpam ānaya mayā cauro dhṛto 'sti | tayoktam | bahir yāntī bibhemy aham | enaṃ grahīṣye tvaṃ dīpam ānaya | tena ca tathā kṛtam | sā ca jāraṃ muktvā gṛhāntar baddhasya paṭṭakasya (?) jihvāṃ gṛhītvā tathaiva suptā yāvat patir lakuṭahasto dīpaṃ gṛhītvā samāyātaḥ pṛcchati | kim iyaṃ paṭṭakasya (?) jihvā | katham atra | tayoktam | kṣudhārto 'yam | anena muktā lālā kṛśā sthitā | uktipratyuktivādena nirjitaḥ | uktaś ca | hataka anena pauruṣeṇa kṣayaṃ vrajasi | iti nirbhartsito lajjitaś ca suptaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptaviṃśatitamī kathā ||

p.96, l.4

asti kuhāḍākhyo mahāgrāmaḥ | tatra jarasākhyo kuṭumbiko mahāmūrkhaḥ | (p.96, l.5)
tadbhāryā devikā puṃścalī | tāṃ ca prabhākaro brāhmaṇaḥ kṣetramadhye vibhītakavṛkṣasamīpe (p.96, l.6)
guptasthāne mudā ramate | īdṛśaṃ vyatikaraṃ janāc chrutvā (p.96, l.7)
tatpatis tatrāvalokanāya svayaṃ gataḥ | tena ca vṛkṣārūḍhena tat tathaiva dṛṣṭam | (p.96, l.8)
dṛṣṭvā tatrasthenāpi jalpitam | dhūrtike bahudinebhyo 'dya saṃprāptā | (p.96, l.9)
ity uktā katham iyaṃ bhartāraṃ pratyāyayatu | (p.96, l.10)
tayoktam | nāhaṃ jāne tvam eva (p.96, l.11)
kathaya | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayā tatheti pratipanne (p.96, l.12)
śukaḥ prāha | sā ca tad vacaḥ śrutvā taṃ jāraṃ preṣayām āsa patyā cāvatīrya (p.96, l.13)
samāgatena upālabdhā | sāha | he prabho | īdṛśa eva vṛkṣaḥ (p.97, l.1)
atrārūḍhair mithunaṃ dṛśyate | tena patinā uktam | tvam āruhya avalokaya | (p.97, l.2)
tayā tathā kṛtam | vṛkṣārūḍhayā ca tayā proktaṃ kapaṭena | bahudivasebhyo (p.97, l.3)
'nyāṃ narīm abhigaman dṛṣṭo 'si | tena mūrkheṇa jñātam | satyam (p.97, l.4)
idam | sa ca tāṃ śāntayitvā gṛhaṃ nināya | iti kathāṃ śrutvā (p.97, l.5)
prabhāvatī suptā | (p.97, l.6)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭāviṃśatitamī kathā || (p.97, l.7)

asti kuhāḍākhyo mahāgrāmaḥ | tatra jarasākhyo kuṭumbiko mahāmūrkhaḥ | tadbhāryā devikā puṃścalī | tāṃ ca prabhākaro brāhmaṇaḥ kṣetramadhye vibhītakavṛkṣasamīpe guptasthāne mudā ramate | īdṛśaṃ vyatikaraṃ janāc chrutvā tatpatis tatrāvalokanāya svayaṃ gataḥ | tena ca vṛkṣārūḍhena tat tathaiva dṛṣṭam | dṛṣṭvā tatrasthenāpi jalpitam | dhūrtike bahudinebhyo 'dya saṃprāptā | ity uktā katham iyaṃ bhartāraṃ pratyāyayatu | tayoktam | nāhaṃ jāne tvam eva kathaya | yadi na yāsi tadā kathayāmi | tayā tatheti pratipanne śukaḥ prāha | sā ca tad vacaḥ śrutvā taṃ jāraṃ preṣayām āsa patyā cāvatīrya samāgatena upālabdhā | sāha | he prabho | īdṛśa eva vṛkṣaḥ atrārūḍhair mithunaṃ dṛśyate | tena patinā uktam | tvam āruhya avalokaya | tayā tathā kṛtam | vṛkṣārūḍhayā ca tayā proktaṃ kapaṭena | bahudivasebhyo 'nyāṃ narīm abhigaman dṛṣṭo 'si | tena mūrkheṇa jñātam | satyam idam | sa ca tāṃ śāntayitvā gṛhaṃ nināya | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭāviṃśatitamī kathā ||

iti śukasaptatau ekonatriṃśattamī kathā || (p.98, l.9)

astīha pṛthivyāṃ bhūtavāsaṃ nāma śmaśānam | tatra dvau piśācau karālottālanāmānau | bhārye ca dhūmaprabhāmeghaprabhākhye tayoś ca | bhāryārāmaṇīyakatve vivādaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | anyadā ca tābhyāṃ bhāryāsahitābhyāṃ mūladevo dṛṣṭo bāhubhyāṃ vidhṛtya pṛṣṭaḥ | kā anayor madhyād ramaṇīyā | anṛtaṃ vadantaṃ vyāpādayiṣyāmaḥ | tatkalatre virūpe bhīṣaṇe vṛddhe piśācinyau | sa ca yathārthavādī bhakṣitaḥ kim uttaraṃ kuryād iti | uttaram |

p.99, l.7

tenoktam |

yā yasya vallabhā loke ramyā sā tasya nāparā |(p.99, l.9)
 gadite dhūrtarājena tābhyāṃ muktaś ca tatkṣaṇāt || 30.2 (= 176) ||(p.99, l.10)

tenoktam |

yā yasya vallabhā loke ramyā sā tasya nāparā | gadite dhūrtarājena tābhyāṃ muktaś ca tatkṣaṇāt || 30.2 (= 176) ||

§ 31

(p.100, l.1)

p.100, l.1

p.100, l.2

yatheṣṭaṃ vraja kalyāṇi keliṃ kartuṃ kṛśodari |(p.100, l.3)
 śaśakasyeva te buddhir asti cet susahāyinī || 31.1 (= 177) ||(p.100, l.4)
yatheṣṭaṃ vraja kalyāṇi keliṃ kartuṃ kṛśodari | śaśakasyeva te buddhir asti cet susahāyinī || 31.1 (= 177) ||

p.100, l.4

madhurākhye vane piṅgalanāmā siṃhaḥ | sa sattvāni bahūni hanan sarvaiḥ (p.100, l.5)
paśubhir vicārya pratidinam ekaikasattvaparikalpanavyavasthayā nivāritaḥ | (p.100, l.6)
anyadā śaśakasyaikasya vārakaḥ saṃjātaḥ | sa ca na yāti śvāpadair (p.100, l.7)
bhaṇito 'pi | gaccha tvam anyathā pūrvavat sarvāṇi bhūtāni sa bhakṣayiṣyati | (p.100, l.8)
sa cādyaprabhṛti tadantike sattvāni na yāsyanti | ity uktvā bahukālakṣepaṃ (p.100, l.9)
cakāra | madhyāhnasamaye eva ca mandaṃ mandaṃ siṃhasyāgre gantuṃ (p.101, l.1)
vyavasitaḥ | tenāpi sahasākrāntaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | śaśakaḥ (p.101, l.2)
siṃhaṃ prāha | svāminn ahaṃ śaśakacatuṣṭayena saha āgacchan mārge tava śatruṇā (p.101, l.3)
dhṛto 'to velātikramo babhūva | tenoktam | sa śatruḥ kvāste | tataḥ (p.101, l.4)
sa śaśakena dhūrtena vāṭīṃ nītvā tasyaiva pratibimbaḥ kūpe darśitaḥ | (p.101, l.5)
siṃho 'pi mūrkhas taṃ jale dṛṣṭvā kupito jhampām adān mṛtaś ca | (p.101, l.6)

madhurākhye vane piṅgalanāmā siṃhaḥ | sa sattvāni bahūni hanan sarvaiḥ paśubhir vicārya pratidinam ekaikasattvaparikalpanavyavasthayā nivāritaḥ | anyadā śaśakasyaikasya vārakaḥ saṃjātaḥ | sa ca na yāti śvāpadair bhaṇito 'pi | gaccha tvam anyathā pūrvavat sarvāṇi bhūtāni sa bhakṣayiṣyati | sa cādyaprabhṛti tadantike sattvāni na yāsyanti | ity uktvā bahukālakṣepaṃ cakāra | madhyāhnasamaye eva ca mandaṃ mandaṃ siṃhasyāgre gantuṃ vyavasitaḥ | tenāpi sahasākrāntaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | uttaram | śaśakaḥ siṃhaṃ prāha | svāminn ahaṃ śaśakacatuṣṭayena saha āgacchan mārge tava śatruṇā dhṛto 'to velātikramo babhūva | tenoktam | sa śatruḥ kvāste | tataḥ sa śaśakena dhūrtena vāṭīṃ nītvā tasyaiva pratibimbaḥ kūpe darśitaḥ | siṃho 'pi mūrkhas taṃ jale dṛṣṭvā kupito jhampām adān mṛtaś ca |

p.101, l.6

buddhir balavatī bhīrusattvānāṃ na parākramaḥ |(p.101, l.7)
 śaśakenālpasattvena hataḥ siṃhaḥ parākramī || 31.2 (= 178) ||(p.101, l.8)
buddhir balavatī bhīrusattvānāṃ na parākramaḥ | śaśakenālpasattvena hataḥ siṃhaḥ parākramī || 31.2 (= 178) ||

uktaṃ ca |

ekaṃ hanyān na vā hanyād iṣur mukto dhanuṣmatā |(p.101, l.9)
 sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantriniścayaḥ || 31.3 (= 179) ||(p.101, l.10)

uktaṃ ca |

ekaṃ hanyān na vā hanyād iṣur mukto dhanuṣmatā | sarāṣṭraṃ saprajaṃ hanti rājānaṃ mantriniścayaḥ || 31.3 (= 179) ||

p.101, l.10

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.101, l.11)

 rājinīva vijānāsi vaktuṃ dhūliviparyaye || 32.1 (= 180) ||(p.102, l.4)
yāhi devi mano yatra gantuṃ te kamalānane | rājinīva vijānāsi vaktuṃ dhūliviparyaye || 32.1 (= 180) ||

p.102, l.4

asti śāntipuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra mādhavaḥ śreṣṭhī | tasya mohinī (p.102, l.5)
bhāryā | tayos tanayaḥ sohaḍābhidhaḥ | tasya bhāryā rājinīnāmnī (p.102, l.6)
rūpasaṃpannā caturā puṃścalī | sānyadā drammam arpayitvā śvaśrvājñaptā godhūmān (p.102, l.7)
haṭṭe gṛhītvāgaccha | sā ca haṭṭe gatā | krīṇatyā copapatir dṛṣṭaḥ (p.102, l.8)
saṃjñitaś ca samīpam āyayau | godhūmān moṭāyāṃ baddhvā haṭṭe muktvā tena (p.103, l.1)
sārdhaṃ sā yayau | vaṇijāpi godhūmān utsārya moṭāyāṃ dhūlir baddhā | (p.103, l.2)
sāpi tena saha ciraṃ sthitvā āgatyākulā moṭām anutpāṭayitvā gṛhaṃ (p.103, l.3)
yayau | tāṃ choṭayitvā yāvat śvaśrūḥ paśyati kīdṛśā godhūmā iti (p.103, l.4)
tāvad dhūliṃ paśyati | atra kim uttaram | śukaḥ | kim idam iti yadā (p.103, l.5)
śvaśrvā pṛṣṭā tadā tayoktam | mātar mama hastād drammo haṭṭāgre bhūmau patitaḥ | (p.103, l.6)
tato mayā dhūlir āhṛtā | tataḥ sā śvaśrūr drammam anavalokamānā (p.103, l.7)
vikalībhūtā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.103, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau dvātriṃśattamī kathā || (p.103, l.9)

asti śāntipuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra mādhavaḥ śreṣṭhī | tasya mohinī bhāryā | tayos tanayaḥ sohaḍābhidhaḥ | tasya bhāryā rājinīnāmnī rūpasaṃpannā caturā puṃścalī | sānyadā drammam arpayitvā śvaśrvājñaptā godhūmān haṭṭe gṛhītvāgaccha | sā ca haṭṭe gatā | krīṇatyā copapatir dṛṣṭaḥ saṃjñitaś ca samīpam āyayau | godhūmān moṭāyāṃ baddhvā haṭṭe muktvā tena sārdhaṃ sā yayau | vaṇijāpi godhūmān utsārya moṭāyāṃ dhūlir baddhā | sāpi tena saha ciraṃ sthitvā āgatyākulā moṭām anutpāṭayitvā gṛhaṃ yayau | tāṃ choṭayitvā yāvat śvaśrūḥ paśyati kīdṛśā godhūmā iti tāvad dhūliṃ paśyati | atra kim uttaram | śukaḥ | kim idam iti yadā śvaśrvā pṛṣṭā tadā tayoktam | mātar mama hastād drammo haṭṭāgre bhūmau patitaḥ | tato mayā dhūlir āhṛtā | tataḥ sā śvaśrūr drammam anavalokamānā vikalībhūtā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvātriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.103, l.10

ko doṣo gamyatāṃ devi yadi kartuṃ tvam īśvarā |(p.104, l.1)
 viṣame mālinī yadvad rambhikā patisaṃnidhau || 33.1 (= 181) ||(p.104, l.2)
ko doṣo gamyatāṃ devi yadi kartuṃ tvam īśvarā | viṣame mālinī yadvad rambhikā patisaṃnidhau || 33.1 (= 181) ||

p.104, l.2

katham etat | śuko 'bravīt | asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra (p.104, l.3)
śaṅkaro nāma mālikaḥ samṛddhimān | tasya rambhikā nāma bhāryā (p.104, l.4)
bahuratipriyā subhagā surūpā bahubhartṛkā ca | anyadā śaṅkaragṛhe pitṛkāryam (p.104, l.5)
āgatam | tasmin dine tayopapatayaś catvāro nimantritāḥ | puṣpāṇāṃ (p.104, l.6)
vikrīṇāya gatayā catuṣpathe grāmaṇīr vaṇiksūnus talāraś ca balādhipaś (p.104, l.7)
ca pratyekaṃ te te pṛthak pṛthak ākāritāḥ parasparam ajānantaḥ | (p.104, l.8)
madīyaṃ bhavanaṃ prati prāg eva samāgantavyam iti | dvitīye 'hni (p.105, l.1)
mālike vāṭikāṃ gate vaṇiksūnuḥ snātvā bhuktvā ca tayā saha rantuṃ (p.105, l.2)
samāyayau | vaṇiji ardhasnāte grāmakūṭo gṛhadvāraṃ samāpatan dṛṣṭaḥ | (p.105, l.3)
tataḥ snānaṃ kurvan vaṇik tathābhūto vaṃśamaye koṣṭhe khaliyukte kṣipto bhayayuktaś (p.105, l.4)
ca | grāmakūṭe 'py ardhasnāte bahis talāraḥ samāyātaḥ | taṃ dṛṣṭvā so (p.105, l.5)
'pi tasminn eva koṣṭhe kṣipta uktaś ca yad adhaḥ sarpiṇī prasūtāsti | tato (p.105, l.6)
'py antarāla eva sthātavyam iti talāro 'py ardhasnāto balādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.105, l.7)
bhāṇḍasamūhe kṣiptaḥ | balādhipo 'py ardhasnāto mālikaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva (p.105, l.8)
kṣiptaḥ | tato māliko lokaś ca tasmin pitṛkārye yadṛcchayā bhojitāḥ | (p.105, l.9)
evaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ caturṇām api parasparam alakṣitānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak bhojanaṃ (p.105, l.10)
paramānnāmṛtaṃ samarpitam | vaṇijā tu bhuñjānena bahu phūtkṛtam | tadoparisthitena (p.106, l.1)
ca sarpiṇīṃ śaṅkamānena mūtritam | vaṇijā tu ghṛtām iti (p.106, l.2)
jñātvā bhājanam utkṣiptam | uparisthitasya mukhe lagnam | tataḥ sa śaṅkitaḥ | (p.106, l.3)
so 'pi ca lagnaṃ lagnam iti vadan dattajhampo niryayau | anye (p.106, l.4)
'pi lagnākṣarabhayākulā yāvan nirgatāḥ śaṅkareṇa janaiś ca dṛṣṭāḥ savismayaṃ (p.106, l.5)
khalikharaḍitāḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaram | yadā sā patyā (p.106, l.6)
pṛṣṭā kim idam iti tadā tayoktam | (p.106, l.7)

katham etat | śuko 'bravīt | asti śaṅkhapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra śaṅkaro nāma mālikaḥ samṛddhimān | tasya rambhikā nāma bhāryā bahuratipriyā subhagā surūpā bahubhartṛkā ca | anyadā śaṅkaragṛhe pitṛkāryam āgatam | tasmin dine tayopapatayaś catvāro nimantritāḥ | puṣpāṇāṃ vikrīṇāya gatayā catuṣpathe grāmaṇīr vaṇiksūnus talāraś ca balādhipaś ca pratyekaṃ te te pṛthak pṛthak ākāritāḥ parasparam ajānantaḥ | madīyaṃ bhavanaṃ prati prāg eva samāgantavyam iti | dvitīye 'hni mālike vāṭikāṃ gate vaṇiksūnuḥ snātvā bhuktvā ca tayā saha rantuṃ samāyayau | vaṇiji ardhasnāte grāmakūṭo gṛhadvāraṃ samāpatan dṛṣṭaḥ | tataḥ snānaṃ kurvan vaṇik tathābhūto vaṃśamaye koṣṭhe khaliyukte kṣipto bhayayuktaś ca | grāmakūṭe 'py ardhasnāte bahis talāraḥ samāyātaḥ | taṃ dṛṣṭvā so 'pi tasminn eva koṣṭhe kṣipta uktaś ca yad adhaḥ sarpiṇī prasūtāsti | tato 'py antarāla eva sthātavyam iti talāro 'py ardhasnāto balādhipaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāṇḍasamūhe kṣiptaḥ | balādhipo 'py ardhasnāto mālikaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatraiva kṣiptaḥ | tato māliko lokaś ca tasmin pitṛkārye yadṛcchayā bhojitāḥ | evaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ caturṇām api parasparam alakṣitānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak bhojanaṃ paramānnāmṛtaṃ samarpitam | vaṇijā tu bhuñjānena bahu phūtkṛtam | tadoparisthitena ca sarpiṇīṃ śaṅkamānena mūtritam | vaṇijā tu ghṛtām iti jñātvā bhājanam utkṣiptam | uparisthitasya mukhe lagnam | tataḥ sa śaṅkitaḥ | so 'pi ca lagnaṃ lagnam iti vadan dattajhampo niryayau | anye 'pi lagnākṣarabhayākulā yāvan nirgatāḥ śaṅkareṇa janaiś ca dṛṣṭāḥ savismayaṃ khalikharaḍitāḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaram | yadā sā patyā pṛṣṭā kim idam iti tadā tayoktam |

p.106, l.7

śraddhāhīnaṃ kṛtaṃ śrāddham idaṃ nūnaṃ tvayā priya |(p.106, l.8)
 ato 'bhuktvā kṣudhākrāntāḥ pitaras te vinirgatāḥ || 33.2 (= 182) ||(p.106, l.9)
śraddhāhīnaṃ kṛtaṃ śrāddham idaṃ nūnaṃ tvayā priya | ato 'bhuktvā kṣudhākrāntāḥ pitaras te vinirgatāḥ || 33.2 (= 182) ||

p.106, l.9

tataḥ sa punaḥ śrāddhaṃ cakāra rambhikāvacanāt te na nirgatāḥ | iti kathāṃ (p.106, l.10)
śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.106, l.11)
iti śukasaptatau trayastriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.107, l.4

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | purā kasmiṃścin nagare śambhunāmā (p.107, l.5)
vipro 'bhūt | dyūtakṛn nānādeśaparibhramaṇaśīlo mārge gacchan kṣetrarakṣikāṃ (p.107, l.6)
surūpāṃ bālikāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāmbūlaṃ dattvā sāntvayann idam uvāca | (p.107, l.7)
yan matsambhogakaraṇe imāṃ madīyāṃ pāraḍīṃ (?) gṛhāṇa mayā saha rataṃ kuru | (p.107, l.8)
sukhāśrayaṃ tayā tathā vihitam | sa ca siddhe kārye tāṃ yācate | (p.107, l.9)
kathaṃ labhate | uttaram | yāvat tena yācitā tāvat sā calitā gṛhaṃ (p.107, l.10)
prati | so 'pi ca pañca kaṇiśāni gṛhītvā pṛṣṭhe lagnaḥ | tena ca (p.108, l.1)
grāmagatena phūtkṛtam | aho grāmamukhyāḥ paśyata | grāme 'smin mahad adbhutam | (p.108, l.2)

tayā ca na kiṃcid uktaṃ lajjayā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.108, l.4)
iti śukasaptatau catustriṃśattamī kathā || (p.108, l.5)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | purā kasmiṃścin nagare śambhunāmā vipro 'bhūt | dyūtakṛn nānādeśaparibhramaṇaśīlo mārge gacchan kṣetrarakṣikāṃ surūpāṃ bālikāṃ dṛṣṭvā tāmbūlaṃ dattvā sāntvayann idam uvāca | yan matsambhogakaraṇe imāṃ madīyāṃ pāraḍīṃ (?) gṛhāṇa mayā saha rataṃ kuru | sukhāśrayaṃ tayā tathā vihitam | sa ca siddhe kārye tāṃ yācate | kathaṃ labhate | uttaram | yāvat tena yācitā tāvat sā calitā gṛhaṃ prati | so 'pi ca pañca kaṇiśāni gṛhītvā pṛṣṭhe lagnaḥ | tena ca grāmagatena phūtkṛtam | aho grāmamukhyāḥ paśyata | grāme 'smin mahad adbhutam | pañcakaṇiśakāraṇenānayā madīyaṃ vastram apahṛtam | grāmyais tatsamarpitam | tayā ca na kiṃcid uktaṃ lajjayā | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catustriṃśattamī kathā ||

 svārthaṃ kartuṃ vijānāsi tilakrayakaro yathā || 35.1 (= 184) ||(p.108, l.8)
gaccha devi na te doṣo yadi tatra gatā satī | svārthaṃ kartuṃ vijānāsi tilakrayakaro yathā || 35.1 (= 184) ||

p.108, l.8

katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | purā kasmiṃścid grāme śambakanāmā vaṇik (p.108, l.9)
tilagrāhakaḥ | sa ca saragrāmaṃ yayau | tatrasthasya bhāṇḍaśālikasya (p.108, l.10)
gṛhe gataḥ | sa gṛhe nāsti | tasya bhāryāsti paraṃ kulaṭā | (p.109, l.1)
netrasaṃjñayā parasparaṃ prītir utpannā | tatraiva sā bhuktā aṅgulīyakaṃ dattvā | (p.109, l.2)
sambandhād anantaraṃ sa tadaṅgulīyakaṃ jighṛkṣati | anena vidhinā dattam (p.109, l.3)
aṅgulīyakaṃ sa kathaṃ gṛhṇātv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | tilagrāhakas tadalabhamāno (p.109, l.4)
vipaṇisthaṃ bhāṇḍaśālikam āha | (p.109, l.5)

katham etat | śukaḥ prāha | purā kasmiṃścid grāme śambakanāmā vaṇik tilagrāhakaḥ | sa ca saragrāmaṃ yayau | tatrasthasya bhāṇḍaśālikasya gṛhe gataḥ | sa gṛhe nāsti | tasya bhāryāsti paraṃ kulaṭā | netrasaṃjñayā parasparaṃ prītir utpannā | tatraiva sā bhuktā aṅgulīyakaṃ dattvā | sambandhād anantaraṃ sa tadaṅgulīyakaṃ jighṛkṣati | anena vidhinā dattam aṅgulīyakaṃ sa kathaṃ gṛhṇātv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | tilagrāhakas tadalabhamāno vipaṇisthaṃ bhāṇḍaśālikam āha |

dehi me tilaprasthaśataṃ yatsatyaṃ kāritaṃ mayā | (!)(p.109, l.6)

ke tilāḥ kaś ca vaktā tvaṃ satyaṃkāraś ca kīdṛśaḥ |(p.110, l.1)
ke tilāḥ kaś ca vaktā tvaṃ satyaṃkāraś ca kīdṛśaḥ |

p.110, l.1

tenoktam | prasthaṃ prati dvikapravṛddhyā tvadbhāryayā satyaṃkāre 'ṅgulīyakaṃ (p.110, l.2)
gṛhītam | tato ruṣṭena vaṇijā bhāryāpārśve nijaṃ sutaṃ preṣayitvā iti (p.110, l.3)
kathayām āsa | tvadīyenedṛśena vyavahāreṇāsmadgṛhaṃ vṛddhim āpsyati | putro (p.110, l.4)
'py aṅgulīyakam ādāya tilagrāhakasyārpayām āsa | so 'pi yathāgataṃ tathā (p.110, l.5)
yayau | tato yadi prabhāvati tavāpy evaṃ buddhir asti tadā gamyatāṃ nānyatheti (p.110, l.6)
kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.110, l.7)
iti śukasaptatau pañcatriṃśattamī kathā || (p.110, l.8)

tenoktam | prasthaṃ prati dvikapravṛddhyā tvadbhāryayā satyaṃkāre 'ṅgulīyakaṃ gṛhītam | tato ruṣṭena vaṇijā bhāryāpārśve nijaṃ sutaṃ preṣayitvā iti kathayām āsa | tvadīyenedṛśena vyavahāreṇāsmadgṛhaṃ vṛddhim āpsyati | putro 'py aṅgulīyakam ādāya tilagrāhakasyārpayām āsa | so 'pi yathāgataṃ tathā yayau | tato yadi prabhāvati tavāpy evaṃ buddhir asti tadā gamyatāṃ nānyatheti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcatriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.111, l.1

kā kīra nāyinī kutra tayā kiṃ kṛtam uttaram |(p.111, l.2)
 kathāṃ kathaya kalyāṇīṃ kautukaṃ me kathākrame || 36.2 (= 186) ||(p.111, l.3)
kā kīra nāyinī kutra tayā kiṃ kṛtam uttaram | kathāṃ kathaya kalyāṇīṃ kautukaṃ me kathākrame || 36.2 (= 186) ||

p.111, l.3

śuka āha | asti saraḍākhye grāme grāmaṇīḥ śūrapālaḥ | tasya bhāryā (p.111, l.4)
nāyinī | sā ātmapatiṃ nityaṃ paṭṭasūtrakañcukaṃ yācate | sa āha | (p.111, l.5)
vayaṃ karṣukāḥ kārpāsacīvarāḥ | asmadgṛhe paṭṭasūtravārttām api ko 'pi (p.111, l.6)
na jānāti | anyadā sā taṃ grāmasaṃsadisthaṃ jagāda | gṛham ehi gṛhādhipa | (p.111, l.7)
rāvaḍīṃ bhuṅkṣva | sa ca tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhāryām āha gṛhāgataḥ | (p.111, l.8)
bhadre tvayā ninditaṃ vaco lajjākārakaṃ mamāpriyaṃ saṃsadi kim ittham (p.111, l.9)
uktam | tayoktam | tvayā mama priyaṃ kathaṃ na kṛtam | grāmaṇīr āha | (p.111, l.10)
dāsyāmi kañcukaṃ te 'dya | nijaṃ vākyaṃ vṛthā kuru | tayoktam | (p.112, l.1)
kañcuke datte uttārayiṣye | dattaḥ kañcukas tena | tad vacaḥ kathaṃ vṛthā bhavatv (p.112, l.2)
iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | anyadā nāyinī jagāda | yadādya tvāṃ (p.112, l.3)
saṃsadisthaṃ pūrvavad ākārayāmi tadā tvayā saṃsadā saha gṛham āgantavyam | (p.112, l.4)
tena ca evam eva kṛtam | tayā ca gṛhāgatāyāḥ saṃsado bhavyarītyā (p.112, l.5)
bhojanaṃ dattam | tato grāmajano vadati | śūrapālaḥ samṛddhaḥ | paraṃ (p.112, l.6)
tadbhāryā auddhatyaparihāreṇa evaṃ vadati | iti vacanam uttāritam | (p.112, l.7)
iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.112, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭtriṃśattamī kathā || 36 || (p.112, l.9)

śuka āha | asti saraḍākhye grāme grāmaṇīḥ śūrapālaḥ | tasya bhāryā nāyinī | sā ātmapatiṃ nityaṃ paṭṭasūtrakañcukaṃ yācate | sa āha | vayaṃ karṣukāḥ kārpāsacīvarāḥ | asmadgṛhe paṭṭasūtravārttām api ko 'pi na jānāti | anyadā sā taṃ grāmasaṃsadisthaṃ jagāda | gṛham ehi gṛhādhipa | rāvaḍīṃ bhuṅkṣva | sa ca tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhāryām āha gṛhāgataḥ | bhadre tvayā ninditaṃ vaco lajjākārakaṃ mamāpriyaṃ saṃsadi kim ittham uktam | tayoktam | tvayā mama priyaṃ kathaṃ na kṛtam | grāmaṇīr āha | dāsyāmi kañcukaṃ te 'dya | nijaṃ vākyaṃ vṛthā kuru | tayoktam | kañcuke datte uttārayiṣye | dattaḥ kañcukas tena | tad vacaḥ kathaṃ vṛthā bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | anyadā nāyinī jagāda | yadādya tvāṃ saṃsadisthaṃ pūrvavad ākārayāmi tadā tvayā saṃsadā saha gṛham āgantavyam | tena ca evam eva kṛtam | tayā ca gṛhāgatāyāḥ saṃsado bhavyarītyā bhojanaṃ dattam | tato grāmajano vadati | śūrapālaḥ samṛddhaḥ | paraṃ tadbhāryā auddhatyaparihāreṇa evaṃ vadati | iti vacanam uttāritam | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭtriṃśattamī kathā || 36 ||

p.113, l.1

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuko 'py āha | saṃgamākhye grāme śūraḥ kauṭumbikaḥ | (p.113, l.2)
tasyāsti pūrṇapālas tu hālikaḥ | sarvatra ca tasya śūrapater (p.113, l.3)
veśmani kṣetre khale pramāṇam | tasya ca hālikasya kṣetrasthasya śūrapatisutā (p.113, l.4)
subhagā nāma nityaṃ bhuktiṃ nayati | sa tāṃ kāmayate kṣetragahvare (p.113, l.5)
śūrapālān niḥśaṅkitaḥ | taṃ ca vṛttāntam asamañjasam iti kṛtvā prativeśmahālikās (p.113, l.6)
tasya kathayām āsuḥ | anyadāsau śūras tayor hālikasutayoḥ saṃbandhaṃ (p.113, l.7)
pratyakṣīkartuṃ kṣetraṃ gatvā gahvarasyādūrasamante 'lakṣitas tasthau | tan mithunaṃ (p.113, l.8)
ratasthaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaraṃ ca kim iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yāvat sa (p.113, l.9)
hālikas tāṃ bhuktvotthitaḥ tāvat śūrapatiṃ dadarśa | tadā sa niḥśvasann āha | (p.114, l.1)
dhiṅ me karmārjanāṃ ca yan mayā halakheṭanaṃ vidheyaṃ iyaṃ ca granthirogiṇī | (p.114, l.2)
ato dvayor api jīvitaṃ rasātalaṃ yātu | mayā tu nityaṃ halakheṭanaṃ (p.114, l.3)
granther ākarṣaṇaṃ ca dvayam api vidheyam | tad ahaṃ kimartham asya śūrapālasya (p.114, l.4)
hāliko bhavāmi | ittham evāhaṃ kṣayaṃ yāsyāmi | iti hālikavacanaṃ (p.114, l.5)
śrutvā nirdoṣo 'yam iti lokasya vacanaṃ vitathīkṛtya śūrapatir lajjito (p.114, l.6)
gṛhaṃ yayau | sā ca prabhāvatī śukoktāṃ kathāṃ śrutvā suptā | (p.114, l.7)
iti śukasaptatau saptatriṃśattamī kathā || (p.114, l.8)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuko 'py āha | saṃgamākhye grāme śūraḥ kauṭumbikaḥ | tasyāsti pūrṇapālas tu hālikaḥ | sarvatra ca tasya śūrapater veśmani kṣetre khale pramāṇam | tasya ca hālikasya kṣetrasthasya śūrapatisutā subhagā nāma nityaṃ bhuktiṃ nayati | sa tāṃ kāmayate kṣetragahvare śūrapālān niḥśaṅkitaḥ | taṃ ca vṛttāntam asamañjasam iti kṛtvā prativeśmahālikās tasya kathayām āsuḥ | anyadāsau śūras tayor hālikasutayoḥ saṃbandhaṃ pratyakṣīkartuṃ kṣetraṃ gatvā gahvarasyādūrasamante 'lakṣitas tasthau | tan mithunaṃ ratasthaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kathaṃ bhavatu | uttaraṃ ca kim iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yāvat sa hālikas tāṃ bhuktvotthitaḥ tāvat śūrapatiṃ dadarśa | tadā sa niḥśvasann āha | dhiṅ me karmārjanāṃ ca yan mayā halakheṭanaṃ vidheyaṃ iyaṃ ca granthirogiṇī | ato dvayor api jīvitaṃ rasātalaṃ yātu | mayā tu nityaṃ halakheṭanaṃ granther ākarṣaṇaṃ ca dvayam api vidheyam | tad ahaṃ kimartham asya śūrapālasya hāliko bhavāmi | ittham evāhaṃ kṣayaṃ yāsyāmi | iti hālikavacanaṃ śrutvā nirdoṣo 'yam iti lokasya vacanaṃ vitathīkṛtya śūrapatir lajjito gṛhaṃ yayau | sā ca prabhāvatī śukoktāṃ kathāṃ śrutvā suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptatriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.114, l.9

 yadi kartuṃ vijānāsi yathā vipraḥ priyaṃvadaḥ || 38.1 (= 188) ||(p.115, l.1)
vāñchitaṃ kartukāmānāṃ nāntarāyaṃ kṛśodari | yadi kartuṃ vijānāsi yathā vipraḥ priyaṃvadaḥ || 38.1 (= 188) ||

p.115, l.1

prabhāvatī papraccha | katham etat | śukaḥ | purābhūd devi priyaṃvado nāma (p.115, l.2)
vipraḥ pathikaḥ | ekadā mārge gacchan sudarśanagrāme kasyacid vaṇijo gṛhaṃ (p.115, l.3)
yayau | tatpatnī ca puṃścalī | sa ca brāhmaṇas tāṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ susthānakṛtavāsakaṃ (p.115, l.4)
mene | sa ca rātrau sakāmas tāṃ prārthayām āsa | aṅgulīyakadānena (p.115, l.5)
ca haṭṭamārgaṃ vaṇiksute gate reme tayā samam | prātaḥ so (p.115, l.6)
'ṅgulīyakaṃ yācate | sā nārpayati | anena vidhinā dattam aṅgulīyakaṃ (p.115, l.7)
sa kathaṃ gṛhṇātu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | yadā tu yācitā na dadāti (p.115, l.8)
tadā sa brāhmaṇaḥ khaṭvācaraṇaṃ gṛhītvā vaṇijaḥ saṃnidhiṃ yayau | khaṭvācaraṇaṃ (p.115, l.9)
darśayitvā phūtkṛtam | vaṇik prāha | bho dvija kim etat | sa (p.115, l.10)
āha | bhagne 'smin tvadīyabhāryayā madīyam aṅgulīyakaṃ jagṛhe | sa ca (p.115, l.11)
vaṇik tadvacanaṃ śrutvā kupito bhāryām āha | anena pramādena asmadgṛhe (p.116, l.1)
ko 'pi pathiko na sameṣyati | ity uktvā niṣṭhuraṃ vacas tatkuṇḍād uttīrya (p.116, l.2)
aṅgulīyakaṃ pathikāya samarpitam | sa ca yathāgataṃ yayau | iti (p.116, l.3)
kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.116, l.4)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭātriṃśattamī kathā || (p.116, l.5)

prabhāvatī papraccha | katham etat | śukaḥ | purābhūd devi priyaṃvado nāma vipraḥ pathikaḥ | ekadā mārge gacchan sudarśanagrāme kasyacid vaṇijo gṛhaṃ yayau | tatpatnī ca puṃścalī | sa ca brāhmaṇas tāṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ susthānakṛtavāsakaṃ mene | sa ca rātrau sakāmas tāṃ prārthayām āsa | aṅgulīyakadānena ca haṭṭamārgaṃ vaṇiksute gate reme tayā samam | prātaḥ so 'ṅgulīyakaṃ yācate | sā nārpayati | anena vidhinā dattam aṅgulīyakaṃ sa kathaṃ gṛhṇātu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | yadā tu yācitā na dadāti tadā sa brāhmaṇaḥ khaṭvācaraṇaṃ gṛhītvā vaṇijaḥ saṃnidhiṃ yayau | khaṭvācaraṇaṃ darśayitvā phūtkṛtam | vaṇik prāha | bho dvija kim etat | sa āha | bhagne 'smin tvadīyabhāryayā madīyam aṅgulīyakaṃ jagṛhe | sa ca vaṇik tadvacanaṃ śrutvā kupito bhāryām āha | anena pramādena asmadgṛhe ko 'pi pathiko na sameṣyati | ity uktvā niṣṭhuraṃ vacas tatkuṇḍād uttīrya aṅgulīyakaṃ pathikāya samarpitam | sa ca yathāgataṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭātriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.116, l.5

p.116, l.7

 vaktuṃ ced viṣame vetsi tulāgrāhīva bhāmini || 39.1 (= 189) ||(p.116, l.9)

p.116, l.10

kas tulāgrāhakaḥ kīra gṛhītā ca tulā kutaḥ |(p.116, l.11)
 viṣamaṃ ca kim āyātaṃ kathāṃ kathaya śobhanām || 39.2 (= 190) ||(p.117, l.1)

p.117, l.1

p.117, l.3

uktaṃ ca |

vidvān dhanī dhanī dātā dhanī sādhur guṇāgraṇīḥ |(p.117, l.4)
 sarvabandhur dhanī pūjyo dhanahīno gataprabhaḥ || 39.3 (= 191) ||(p.117, l.5)

uktaṃ ca |

vidvān dhanī dhanī dātā dhanī sādhur guṇāgraṇīḥ | sarvabandhur dhanī pūjyo dhanahīno gataprabhaḥ || 39.3 (= 191) ||

p.117, l.5

yadā tu sa tulāmātradhano 'bhavat tadānyavaṇiggṛhe tulāṃ muktvā deśāntaraṃ (p.117, l.6)
gataḥ | tatra dhanam arjayitvā nijanagaram āgatya taṃ vaṇijaṃ tulāṃ yayāce | (p.117, l.7)
vaṇikpārśvāt tulā na labdhā | tulāyāṃ tu lubdho vaṇik mūrkha uttaraṃ cakre (p.117, l.8)
yat tvadīyā tulā mūṣikair bhakṣiteti śrutvā bhūdharas tūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ | sa ca ekadā (p.117, l.9)
tasya veśmani bhojanāya gataḥ krīḍantaṃ bālakaṃ dṛṣṭvā pracchannaṃ gṛhītvā (p.118, l.1)
nijagṛhaṃ yayau | bālakapitā ca duḥkhapūritāṅgo ruroda sakuṭumbaḥ | (p.118, l.2)
taṃ ca rudantaṃ dṛṣṭvā prativeśmiko jagāda | re tvadīyaḥ suto bhūdhareṇa (p.118, l.3)
gṛhītaḥ | tato 'sau tadgṛhaṃ gatvā bhūdharāt sutaṃ yācitavān | bhūdhareṇoktam | (p.118, l.4)
mitra tvatputro matsaṃge snānārthe nadītīre gatas tatra śyenenāpahṛtaḥ | (p.118, l.5)
iti śrutvā tena vaṇijā rājakule gatvā putraharaṇavṛttānto (p.118, l.6)
niveditaḥ | bhūdharo 'pi rājakulaṃ yayau | tat kathaya | sa bālahartā (p.118, l.7)
kathaṃ mucyatām iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadā bhūdharo rājasamakṣaṃ mantriṇā (p.118, l.8)
pṛṣṭas tadā evaṃ jagāda | (p.119, l.1)

yadā tu sa tulāmātradhano 'bhavat tadānyavaṇiggṛhe tulāṃ muktvā deśāntaraṃ gataḥ | tatra dhanam arjayitvā nijanagaram āgatya taṃ vaṇijaṃ tulāṃ yayāce | vaṇikpārśvāt tulā na labdhā | tulāyāṃ tu lubdho vaṇik mūrkha uttaraṃ cakre yat tvadīyā tulā mūṣikair bhakṣiteti śrutvā bhūdharas tūṣṇīṃ sthitaḥ | sa ca ekadā tasya veśmani bhojanāya gataḥ krīḍantaṃ bālakaṃ dṛṣṭvā pracchannaṃ gṛhītvā nijagṛhaṃ yayau | bālakapitā ca duḥkhapūritāṅgo ruroda sakuṭumbaḥ | taṃ ca rudantaṃ dṛṣṭvā prativeśmiko jagāda | re tvadīyaḥ suto bhūdhareṇa gṛhītaḥ | tato 'sau tadgṛhaṃ gatvā bhūdharāt sutaṃ yācitavān | bhūdhareṇoktam | mitra tvatputro matsaṃge snānārthe nadītīre gatas tatra śyenenāpahṛtaḥ | iti śrutvā tena vaṇijā rājakule gatvā putraharaṇavṛttānto niveditaḥ | bhūdharo 'pi rājakulaṃ yayau | tat kathaya | sa bālahartā kathaṃ mucyatām iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadā bhūdharo rājasamakṣaṃ mantriṇā pṛṣṭas tadā evaṃ jagāda |

p.119, l.1

tulāṃ lohamayīṃ yatra khādante deva mūṣakāḥ |(p.119, l.2)
 gajaṃ tatra haret śyeno dārake ko 'tra vismayaḥ || 39.4 (= 192) ||(p.119, l.3)
tulāṃ lohamayīṃ yatra khādante deva mūṣakāḥ | gajaṃ tatra haret śyeno dārake ko 'tra vismayaḥ || 39.4 (= 192) ||

p.119, l.3

śrutvaitad vacanaṃ mantriṇoktam | yadāyaṃ dhūrtas tava tulāṃ samarpayati tadā (p.119, l.4)
dārako 'pi dātavyo nānyathā | tena dārakaḥ samarpitaḥ | tulāgrāhī (p.119, l.5)
daṇḍitaḥ san tulāṃ samarpayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.119, l.6)
iti śukasaptatau ekonacatvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.119, l.7)

śrutvaitad vacanaṃ mantriṇoktam | yadāyaṃ dhūrtas tava tulāṃ samarpayati tadā dārako 'pi dātavyo nānyathā | tena dārakaḥ samarpitaḥ | tulāgrāhī daṇḍitaḥ san tulāṃ samarpayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonacatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.119, l.10

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | nagarābhidhe pattane subuddhiḥ kubuddhiś ceti (p.120, l.1)
mitradvayaṃ jane prasiddham | anyadā subuddhir deśāntaraṃ yayau | kubuddhis tu (p.120, l.2)
mitrastriyaṃ ramate | subuddhiś ca dhanam arjayitvā deśāntarāt samāgataḥ | tataḥ (p.120, l.3)
kubuddhiḥ subuddheḥ kapaṭasnehaṃ darśayati | subuddhināpi saṃmānitaḥ kubuddhis taṃ (p.120, l.4)
pratyāha | bhavatā kvāpi kiṃcit kautukaṃ dṛṣṭam | tenoktam | sarasvatīnadītīre (p.120, l.5)
kūpamadhye taramāṇam akālajam āmraphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ manoramanāmni grāme | (p.120, l.6)
kubuddhir āha | mithyedam | subuddhir āha | satyam etat | tenoktam | yadi (p.120, l.7)
satyaṃ bhavati tadā yad asmadgṛhe dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahītuṃ śakyate tat tvayā (p.120, l.8)
grāhyam | alīke tvadīyagṛhād ahaṃ gṛhṇāmi | iti paṇabandhaṃ kṛtvā (p.120, l.9)
kubuddhī rātrau kūpāt tatphalaṃ jagrāha | phalābhāve tu subuddhinā hāritam | (p.120, l.10)
atha sa tadbhāryāṃ grahītukāmaḥ paṇabandhaṃ yācate | tad atra subuddhir (p.120, l.11)
nijabhāryārakṣaṇe kam upāyaṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ śuka āha | (p.120, l.12)
subuddhis taṃ duṣṭāśayaṃ jñātvā nijagṛhavastujātaṃ nijakalatraṃ ca prāsādopari (p.120, l.13)
kṣiptvā ārohaṇikāṃ pātayām āsa | kubuddhiḥ samāyātaḥ | subuddhir (p.120, l.14)
āha | evaṃ yad rocate tad asmadgṛhād gṛhyatām | sa ca kalatrāharaṇāya (p.121, l.1)
niḥśreṇikāṃ dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ jagrāha | tadā subuddhinoktam | mayaivaṃ (p.121, l.2)
pūrvaṃ gaditaṃ ca | yad dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahīṣyase tava tad eva nānyat | (p.121, l.3)
tataḥ kubuddhir vilakṣo bhūtvā bahir yayau janaiś ca ninditaḥ | iti kathāṃ (p.121, l.4)
śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.121, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau catvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.121, l.6)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | nagarābhidhe pattane subuddhiḥ kubuddhiś ceti mitradvayaṃ jane prasiddham | anyadā subuddhir deśāntaraṃ yayau | kubuddhis tu mitrastriyaṃ ramate | subuddhiś ca dhanam arjayitvā deśāntarāt samāgataḥ | tataḥ kubuddhiḥ subuddheḥ kapaṭasnehaṃ darśayati | subuddhināpi saṃmānitaḥ kubuddhis taṃ pratyāha | bhavatā kvāpi kiṃcit kautukaṃ dṛṣṭam | tenoktam | sarasvatīnadītīre kūpamadhye taramāṇam akālajam āmraphalaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ manoramanāmni grāme | kubuddhir āha | mithyedam | subuddhir āha | satyam etat | tenoktam | yadi satyaṃ bhavati tadā yad asmadgṛhe dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahītuṃ śakyate tat tvayā grāhyam | alīke tvadīyagṛhād ahaṃ gṛhṇāmi | iti paṇabandhaṃ kṛtvā kubuddhī rātrau kūpāt tatphalaṃ jagrāha | phalābhāve tu subuddhinā hāritam | atha sa tadbhāryāṃ grahītukāmaḥ paṇabandhaṃ yācate | tad atra subuddhir nijabhāryārakṣaṇe kam upāyaṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ śuka āha | subuddhis taṃ duṣṭāśayaṃ jñātvā nijagṛhavastujātaṃ nijakalatraṃ ca prāsādopari kṣiptvā ārohaṇikāṃ pātayām āsa | kubuddhiḥ samāyātaḥ | subuddhir āha | evaṃ yad rocate tad asmadgṛhād gṛhyatām | sa ca kalatrāharaṇāya niḥśreṇikāṃ dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ jagrāha | tadā subuddhinoktam | mayaivaṃ pūrvaṃ gaditaṃ ca | yad dvābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ grahīṣyase tava tad eva nānyat | tataḥ kubuddhir vilakṣo bhūtvā bahir yayau janaiś ca ninditaḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.121, l.10

prabhāvatī prāha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | (p.121, l.11)
tatra śatrumardano nāma rājā | tatsutāyā madanarekhāyā gale granthir babhūva | (p.121, l.12)
vaidyair asādhyety uktvā parityaktā | tato rājñā ḍiṇḍimāghoṣaṇaṃ (p.122, l.1)
kāritaṃ yathā yaḥ ko 'pi matsutāṃ gatarogāṃ karoti tam ahaṃ dāridryarahitaṃ (p.122, l.2)
karomīti śrutvāparagrāmād āgatayā kayācid dvijabhāryayā ḍiṇḍimaḥ (p.122, l.3)
spṛṣṭaḥ | tasmin spṛṣṭe tayoktam | yan mama patir māntrikaḥ | sa rājasutāṃ (p.122, l.4)
praguṇāṃ vidhāsyati | tato rājapuruṣaiḥ samānītaḥ | tasya ca (p.122, l.5)
nīyamānasya bhāryā jagāda | nātha gaccha nagaram | rājasutāyāṃ praguṇīkṛtāyāṃ (p.122, l.6)
tava bahu phalaṃ bhāvi | sa ca maṇḍalopaviṣṭo mantrādikam (p.122, l.7)
ajānan kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa māntrika (p.122, l.8)
ācāryavistāraṃ kṛtvā mantram ity uccārayām āsa | (p.122, l.9)

prabhāvatī prāha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti pañcapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra śatrumardano nāma rājā | tatsutāyā madanarekhāyā gale granthir babhūva | vaidyair asādhyety uktvā parityaktā | tato rājñā ḍiṇḍimāghoṣaṇaṃ kāritaṃ yathā yaḥ ko 'pi matsutāṃ gatarogāṃ karoti tam ahaṃ dāridryarahitaṃ karomīti śrutvāparagrāmād āgatayā kayācid dvijabhāryayā ḍiṇḍimaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tasmin spṛṣṭe tayoktam | yan mama patir māntrikaḥ | sa rājasutāṃ praguṇāṃ vidhāsyati | tato rājapuruṣaiḥ samānītaḥ | tasya ca nīyamānasya bhāryā jagāda | nātha gaccha nagaram | rājasutāyāṃ praguṇīkṛtāyāṃ tava bahu phalaṃ bhāvi | sa ca maṇḍalopaviṣṭo mantrādikam ajānan kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa māntrika ācāryavistāraṃ kṛtvā mantram ity uccārayām āsa |
