p.126, l.1

tac chrutvā prabhāvaty āha | sukhopabhogaḥ saṃsāre | kīra kathāṃ kathaya | (p.126, l.2)
śukaḥ kathāṃ prāha | asti deulākhyo grāmaḥ | tatra rājasiṃho nāma (p.126, l.3)
rājaputraḥ | tadbhāryā kalahapriyeti viśrutā | sānyadā bhartrā sārdhaṃ (p.126, l.4)
kalahaṃ vidhāya putradvayopetā pitur gṛhaṃ prati calitā | sā ca kopavaśāt (p.126, l.5)
pattanāni bahūni vanāni ca bahūny atikramya gatā malayapārśvasthaṃ (p.126, l.6)
mahākānanam | tac ca kathaṃ bhūtam | (p.126, l.7)

p.127, l.1

evaṃvidhe gahane gatā sā kalahapriyā vyāghraṃ dadarśa | sa ca vyāghras tāṃ (p.127, l.2)
saputrāṃ dṛṣṭvā pucchena bhūmim āhatya dhāvitaḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | (p.127, l.3)
iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ | śukaḥ prāha | sā vyāghram āgacchamānaṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.127, l.4)
dhārṣṭyāt putrau capeṭayā hatvā iti jagāda | katham ekaikaśo vyāghrabhakṣaṇāya (p.127, l.5)
kalahaṃ kuruthaḥ | ayam ekas tāvad vibhajya bhujyatām | paścād anyo dvitīyaḥ (p.127, l.6)
kaścil lakṣyate | iti śrutvā vyāghramārī kācid iyam iti matvā vyāghro (p.127, l.7)
bhayākulacitto naṣṭaḥ | (p.127, l.8)

evaṃvidhe gahane gatā sā kalahapriyā vyāghraṃ dadarśa | sa ca vyāghras tāṃ saputrāṃ dṛṣṭvā pucchena bhūmim āhatya dhāvitaḥ | tataḥ sā kathaṃ bhavatu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ | śukaḥ prāha | sā vyāghram āgacchamānaṃ dṛṣṭvā dhārṣṭyāt putrau capeṭayā hatvā iti jagāda | katham ekaikaśo vyāghrabhakṣaṇāya kalahaṃ kuruthaḥ | ayam ekas tāvad vibhajya bhujyatām | paścād anyo dvitīyaḥ kaścil lakṣyate | iti śrutvā vyāghramārī kācid iyam iti matvā vyāghro bhayākulacitto naṣṭaḥ |

p.127, l.8

nijabuddhyā vimuktā sā bhayād vyāghrasya bhāmini |(p.128, l.1)
 anyo 'pi buddhimāṁl loke mucyate mahato bhayāt || 42.3 (= 211) ||(p.128, l.2)
nijabuddhyā vimuktā sā bhayād vyāghrasya bhāmini | anyo 'pi buddhimāṁl loke mucyate mahato bhayāt || 42.3 (= 211) ||

p.128, l.2

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.128, l.3)
iti śukasaptatau dvicatvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.128, l.4)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau dvicatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.128, l.4

p.128, l.5

vraja devi na te 'yuktaṃ vrajanaṃ gajagāmini |(p.128, l.6)
 vyāghramārīva buddhis te dvitīyāpi yadi sthirā || 43.1 (= 212) ||(p.128, l.7)
vraja devi na te 'yuktaṃ vrajanaṃ gajagāmini | vyāghramārīva buddhis te dvitīyāpi yadi sthirā || 43.1 (= 212) ||

p.128, l.7

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | (p.128, l.8)

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat |

p.128, l.8

vyāghramārīkṛtāṃ buddhiṃ dvitīyāṃ vivadādhunā |(p.128, l.9)
 mahat kautukam atrārthe vidyate me priyaṃvada || 43.2 (= 213) ||(p.128, l.10)
vyāghramārīkṛtāṃ buddhiṃ dvitīyāṃ vivadādhunā | mahat kautukam atrārthe vidyate me priyaṃvada || 43.2 (= 213) ||

p.128, l.10

śukaḥ |

taṃ dṛṣṭvā kānane vyāghraṃ naṣṭaṃ jātaṃ bhayākulam |(p.128, l.12)
 mṛgadhūrto hasann āha vyāghro naṣṭaḥ kuto bhayāt || 43.3 (= 214) ||(p.129, l.1)

śukaḥ |

taṃ dṛṣṭvā kānane vyāghraṃ naṣṭaṃ jātaṃ bhayākulam | mṛgadhūrto hasann āha vyāghro naṣṭaḥ kuto bhayāt || 43.3 (= 214) ||

p.129, l.1

vyāghraḥ | gaccha gaccha jambuka tvam api kiṃcid gūḍhapradeśam | yato vyāghramārīti (p.129, l.2)
yā śāstre śrūyate tayāhaṃ hantum ārabdhaḥ paraṃ gṛhītakarajīvito (p.129, l.3)
naṣṭaḥ śīghraṃ tadagrataḥ | mṛgadhūrtaḥ | vyāghra tvayā mahat kautukam āveditaṃ (p.129, l.4)
yan māṃsapiṇḍān mānuṣād api bibheṣi | vyāghraḥ | pratyakṣam eva mayā sātmaputrāv (p.129, l.5)
ekaikaśo mām antuṃ kalahāyamānau capeṭayā ghnantī dṛṣṭā | jambukaḥ | (p.129, l.6)
svāmin yatrāste sā dhūrtā tatra gamyatām | yadi vyāghra tava tatra gatasya (p.129, l.7)
sā saṃmukham apīkṣate tadā mama tvadīyā velā smaraṇīyā | vyāghraḥ | (p.129, l.8)
śṛgāla yadi tvaṃ māṃ muktvā yāsi tadā velāpy avelā syāt | jambukaḥ | (p.129, l.9)
yady evaṃ tarhi māṃ nijagale baddhvā cala śīghram | sa vyāghras tathā kṛtvā (p.129, l.10)
kānanaṃ yayau | vyāghramāry api prāptā putrasahitā tena jambukakṛtotsāhād (p.129, l.11)
vyāghrāt sā kathaṃ mucyatām | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tayā vyāghramāryā (p.129, l.12)
tadā cintitaṃ yad ayaṃ mṛgadhūrtenānītas tasmād amum eva jambukam ākṣipanty (p.129, l.13)
aṅgulyā tarjayanty uvāca | (p.129, l.14)

vyāghraḥ | gaccha gaccha jambuka tvam api kiṃcid gūḍhapradeśam | yato vyāghramārīti yā śāstre śrūyate tayāhaṃ hantum ārabdhaḥ paraṃ gṛhītakarajīvito naṣṭaḥ śīghraṃ tadagrataḥ | mṛgadhūrtaḥ | vyāghra tvayā mahat kautukam āveditaṃ yan māṃsapiṇḍān mānuṣād api bibheṣi | vyāghraḥ | pratyakṣam eva mayā sātmaputrāv ekaikaśo mām antuṃ kalahāyamānau capeṭayā ghnantī dṛṣṭā | jambukaḥ | svāmin yatrāste sā dhūrtā tatra gamyatām | yadi vyāghra tava tatra gatasya sā saṃmukham apīkṣate tadā mama tvadīyā velā smaraṇīyā | vyāghraḥ | śṛgāla yadi tvaṃ māṃ muktvā yāsi tadā velāpy avelā syāt | jambukaḥ | yady evaṃ tarhi māṃ nijagale baddhvā cala śīghram | sa vyāghras tathā kṛtvā kānanaṃ yayau | vyāghramāry api prāptā putrasahitā tena jambukakṛtotsāhād vyāghrāt sā kathaṃ mucyatām | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tayā vyāghramāryā tadā cintitaṃ yad ayaṃ mṛgadhūrtenānītas tasmād amum eva jambukam ākṣipanty aṅgulyā tarjayanty uvāca |

p.129, l.14

re re dhūrta tvayā dattaṃ mahyaṃ vyāghratrayaṃ purā |(p.129, l.15)
 viśvasyādyaikam ānīya kathaṃ yāsi vadādhunā || 43.4 (= 215) ||(p.130, l.1)
re re dhūrta tvayā dattaṃ mahyaṃ vyāghratrayaṃ purā | viśvasyādyaikam ānīya kathaṃ yāsi vadādhunā || 43.4 (= 215) ||
ity uktvā dhāvitā tūrṇaṃ vyāghramārī bhayaṃkarā |(p.130, l.2)
 vyāghro 'pi sahasā naṣṭo galabaddhaśṛgālakaḥ || 43.5 (= 216) ||(p.130, l.3)
ity uktvā dhāvitā tūrṇaṃ vyāghramārī bhayaṃkarā | vyāghro 'pi sahasā naṣṭo galabaddhaśṛgālakaḥ || 43.5 (= 216) ||
nijabuddhyā punar muktā vyāghrajād devi sā bhayāt |(p.130, l.4)
 buddhir balavatī tanvi sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā || 43.6 (= 217) ||(p.130, l.5)
nijabuddhyā punar muktā vyāghrajād devi sā bhayāt | buddhir balavatī tanvi sarvakāryeṣu sarvadā || 43.6 (= 217) ||

p.130, l.5

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.130, l.6)
iti śukasaptatau tricatvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.130, l.7)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau tricatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

§ 44

p.130, l.7

athānyedyur dināvasāne prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.130, l.8)

athānyedyur dināvasāne prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.130, l.8

ātmānaṃ saṃkaṭād devi yāhi ced vetsi rakṣitum |(p.130, l.9)
 yathātmā saṃkaṭāt tena jambukenāpi rakṣitaḥ || 44.1 (= 218) ||(p.130, l.10)
ātmānaṃ saṃkaṭād devi yāhi ced vetsi rakṣitum | yathātmā saṃkaṭāt tena jambukenāpi rakṣitaḥ || 44.1 (= 218) ||

p.130, l.10

sa ca jambuko galabaddho nighṛṣṭapṛṣṭhacaraṇo galadrudhirapravāho mumūrṣur iva (p.130, l.11)
deśāntaraṃ gantum icchatā vyāghramārībhayād vyāghreṇa nīyate | tato mahato (p.130, l.12)
'pāyāt śṛgālaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ prāha śukaḥ | (p.130, l.13)
tatas taṃ vyāghraṃ bahunadīkānanaviṣamasamapradeśaparvatān ullaṅghayantaṃ satvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.131, l.1)
ātmānaṃ mocayitukāmaḥ śṛgālo bhṛśaṃ jahāsa pīḍito 'pi san | (p.131, l.2)
vyāghreṇoktam | kathaṃ hasitam | sa āha | deva sā mayā vyāghramārīti (p.131, l.3)
dhūrtikā jñātā | tvatprasādāc ca dūradeśam āgato 'haṃ jīvitaḥ | (p.131, l.4)
paraṃ yadi sāsmadraktasrāvasaṃlagnā pāpinī pṛṣṭhataḥ sameti tadā kathaṃ (p.131, l.5)
jīvitavyam | ato 'haṃ hasitaḥ | vyāghrasvāmin sthirībhūya vicāraya | (p.131, l.6)
atha tuṣṭo vyāghras tena vākyena tathety uktvā jambukaṃ muktvā sahasā naṣṭaḥ | (p.131, l.7)
śṛgālo 'pi sukhaṃ tasthau | (p.131, l.8)

sa ca jambuko galabaddho nighṛṣṭapṛṣṭhacaraṇo galadrudhirapravāho mumūrṣur iva deśāntaraṃ gantum icchatā vyāghramārībhayād vyāghreṇa nīyate | tato mahato 'pāyāt śṛgālaḥ kathaṃ mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ prāha śukaḥ | tatas taṃ vyāghraṃ bahunadīkānanaviṣamasamapradeśaparvatān ullaṅghayantaṃ satvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā ātmānaṃ mocayitukāmaḥ śṛgālo bhṛśaṃ jahāsa pīḍito 'pi san | vyāghreṇoktam | kathaṃ hasitam | sa āha | deva sā mayā vyāghramārīti dhūrtikā jñātā | tvatprasādāc ca dūradeśam āgato 'haṃ jīvitaḥ | paraṃ yadi sāsmadraktasrāvasaṃlagnā pāpinī pṛṣṭhataḥ sameti tadā kathaṃ jīvitavyam | ato 'haṃ hasitaḥ | vyāghrasvāmin sthirībhūya vicāraya | atha tuṣṭo vyāghras tena vākyena tathety uktvā jambukaṃ muktvā sahasā naṣṭaḥ | śṛgālo 'pi sukhaṃ tasthau |

p.131, l.8

buddhir varaṃ varārohe dhanamānasukhaiṣiṇām |(p.131, l.9)
 buddhihīnāḥ paraṃ kleśaṃ prāpnuvanti kṛśodari || 44.2 (= 219) ||(p.131, l.10)
buddhir varaṃ varārohe dhanamānasukhaiṣiṇām | buddhihīnāḥ paraṃ kleśaṃ prāpnuvanti kṛśodari || 44.2 (= 219) ||
balaṃ prajñāvihīnasya parakāryāya kevalam |(p.131, l.11)
 girikūṭopamāṅgasya kuñjarasyeva dṛśyate || 44.3 (= 220) ||(p.131, l.12)
balaṃ prajñāvihīnasya parakāryāya kevalam | girikūṭopamāṅgasya kuñjarasyeva dṛśyate || 44.3 (= 220) ||

p.131, l.12

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī śukavākyavismitā suptā | (p.131, l.13)

§ 45

p.131, l.14

anyedyuḥ sā kāminī saṃdhyāyāṃ śukaṃ papraccha | gamiṣyāmīti | śukaḥ (p.131, l.15)
prāha | (p.132, l.1)

anyedyuḥ sā kāminī saṃdhyāyāṃ śukaṃ papraccha | gamiṣyāmīti | śukaḥ prāha |

p.132, l.1

samayo 'yaṃ priyaṃ bhoktuṃ tava bhāmini saṃprati |(p.132, l.2)
 vañcitā vetsi cet kartuṃ kiṃcid viṣṇuḥ purā yathā || 45.1 (= 219bis) ||(p.132, l.3)
samayo 'yaṃ priyaṃ bhoktuṃ tava bhāmini saṃprati | vañcitā vetsi cet kartuṃ kiṃcid viṣṇuḥ purā yathā || 45.1 (= 219bis) ||

p.132, l.3

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti vilāsapuraṃ nāma nagaram | (p.132, l.4)
tatra ariṃdamo nāma rājā | tatra ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo (p.132, l.5)
ratilolupaḥ kuṭumbavarjito ratikarmaṇi sarvanārīduḥsaha iti nagare (p.132, l.6)
prasiddho babhūva | veśyābhir api na śakyate jetuṃ kiṃ punaḥ kulāṅganābhiḥ | (p.132, l.7)
tatra ratipriyā nāma gaṇikā | (yato gaṇikādīnāṃ bahavo bhedāḥ (p.132, l.8)
paraṃ pañca prasiddhāḥ | teṣu saṃlīnāḥ sarve 'pi bhavanti | te ceme pañca (p.132, l.9)
gaṇikā vilāsinī rūpājīvā arthavṛttikā dārikā ceti | eteṣāṃ (p.132, l.10)
bhedānāṃ sā sarvottamā gaṇikā |) atha sā ṣoḍaśa drammān gṛhītvā (p.132, l.11)
tam ājuhāva | tam āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā cāṭūktibhiḥ paricaryāṃ cakāra | so (p.132, l.12)
'pi cānyakāryanivṛttas tasminn eva ratikarmaṇi dattamanās tāṃ rantuṃ jetum ārebhe | (p.133, l.1)
tayā ca sa ratilolupaḥ dravyārthaṃ vā parājayārthaṃ vā praharadvayaṃ yāvat (p.133, l.2)
soḍhaḥ | niśīthe cādhobhūmikām āgatya kuṭṭinyagrato niveditaṃ yad duḥsaho (p.133, l.3)
'yaṃ dvijaḥ | paṇabandhaṃ samarpayitvā tam utkālaya | mayi jīvantyāṃ (p.133, l.4)
prāg eva bāhulyaṃ bhaviṣyati | kuṭṭiny āha | asmadgṛhe na ko 'pi kāmuko (p.133, l.5)
gaṇikāṃ jitvā paṇabandhaṃ jagrāha | tato 'ham enaṃ yāvat prapañcena niḥsārayāmi (p.133, l.6)
tāvat soḍhavya iti | yadā cāhaṃ pippalam āruhya sūrpadvayena pakṣaśabdaṃ (p.133, l.7)
kurvāṇā kukkuṭadhvaniṃ vidadhāmi tadā vibhātam iti kṛtvā niḥsāraṇīyaḥ | (p.133, l.8)
ity uktvā preṣitoparibhūmau gaṇikā | yathoktaṃ ca kuṭṭinyā (p.133, l.9)
tāvat kṛtam | tasmin kṛte vibhātam iti kṛtvā niḥsārito dvijaḥ | yāvad (p.133, l.10)
gṛhadvārastho vyomam ālokayate tadopari niśītho vartate | tadā sa (p.133, l.11)
vipraḥ kuṭṭinīparājito janamadhye parājayaṃ kathaṃ vahatu | iti praśnaḥ | (p.133, l.12)
śukaḥ | yadi vipraḥ kukkuṭadhvanisthānam avalokayati tāvat sūrpadvayayutāṃ (p.133, l.13)
kuṭṭinīṃ dadarśa | tena ca sā loṣṭenāhatya bhūmau pātitā pramadājanaiś ca (p.134, l.1)
dhikkṛtā | sa ca brāhmaṇo grahaṇakaṃ dviguṇaṃ gṛhītvā puramadhye gaṇikāṃ (p.134, l.2)
viḍambya svagṛhaṃ yayau | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.134, l.3)
iti śukasaptatau pañcacatvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.134, l.4)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuka āha | asti vilāsapuraṃ nāma nagaram | tatra ariṃdamo nāma rājā | tatra ca viṣṇunāmā brāhmaṇo ratilolupaḥ kuṭumbavarjito ratikarmaṇi sarvanārīduḥsaha iti nagare prasiddho babhūva | veśyābhir api na śakyate jetuṃ kiṃ punaḥ kulāṅganābhiḥ | tatra ratipriyā nāma gaṇikā | (yato gaṇikādīnāṃ bahavo bhedāḥ paraṃ pañca prasiddhāḥ | teṣu saṃlīnāḥ sarve 'pi bhavanti | te ceme pañca gaṇikā vilāsinī rūpājīvā arthavṛttikā dārikā ceti | eteṣāṃ bhedānāṃ sā sarvottamā gaṇikā |) atha sā ṣoḍaśa drammān gṛhītvā tam ājuhāva | tam āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā sā cāṭūktibhiḥ paricaryāṃ cakāra | so 'pi cānyakāryanivṛttas tasminn eva ratikarmaṇi dattamanās tāṃ rantuṃ jetum ārebhe | tayā ca sa ratilolupaḥ dravyārthaṃ vā parājayārthaṃ vā praharadvayaṃ yāvat soḍhaḥ | niśīthe cādhobhūmikām āgatya kuṭṭinyagrato niveditaṃ yad duḥsaho 'yaṃ dvijaḥ | paṇabandhaṃ samarpayitvā tam utkālaya | mayi jīvantyāṃ prāg eva bāhulyaṃ bhaviṣyati | kuṭṭiny āha | asmadgṛhe na ko 'pi kāmuko gaṇikāṃ jitvā paṇabandhaṃ jagrāha | tato 'ham enaṃ yāvat prapañcena niḥsārayāmi tāvat soḍhavya iti | yadā cāhaṃ pippalam āruhya sūrpadvayena pakṣaśabdaṃ kurvāṇā kukkuṭadhvaniṃ vidadhāmi tadā vibhātam iti kṛtvā niḥsāraṇīyaḥ | ity uktvā preṣitoparibhūmau gaṇikā | yathoktaṃ ca kuṭṭinyā tāvat kṛtam | tasmin kṛte vibhātam iti kṛtvā niḥsārito dvijaḥ | yāvad gṛhadvārastho vyomam ālokayate tadopari niśītho vartate | tadā sa vipraḥ kuṭṭinīparājito janamadhye parājayaṃ kathaṃ vahatu | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | yadi vipraḥ kukkuṭadhvanisthānam avalokayati tāvat sūrpadvayayutāṃ kuṭṭinīṃ dadarśa | tena ca sā loṣṭenāhatya bhūmau pātitā pramadājanaiś ca dhikkṛtā | sa ca brāhmaṇo grahaṇakaṃ dviguṇaṃ gṛhītvā puramadhye gaṇikāṃ viḍambya svagṛhaṃ yayau | iti śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcacatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

§ 46

p.134, l.4

athānyedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.134, l.5)

athānyedyuḥ prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.134, l.5

yāhi devi gṛhaṃ muktvā yadi vetsi tvam uttaram |(p.134, l.6)
 yathā karagarānāthaḥ kṛtavān bhūtanigrahe || 46.1 (= 220bis) ||(p.134, l.7)
yāhi devi gṛhaṃ muktvā yadi vetsi tvam uttaram | yathā karagarānāthaḥ kṛtavān bhūtanigrahe || 46.1 (= 220bis) ||

p.134, l.7

asti devi vatsomaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vidvān daridro brāhmaṇaḥ | (p.134, l.8)
tasya priyā ca karagarābhidhānā yathārthanāmnī sarvajantūdvegakāriṇī yat taddvāradeśavṛkṣasthito (p.134, l.9)
bhūtas tasyāḥ karagarāyā bhayāt palāyyāṭavyāṃ gataḥ | (p.134, l.10)
brāhmaṇo 'pi tasyā udvegād deśāntarābhimukho 'bhūt | so 'pi ca tena (p.135, l.1)
bhūtena dṛṣṭo jalpitaś ca | mārgaśrāntas tvam | tena tvayādya mamātithinā (p.135, l.2)
bhāvyam | vipreṇa bhīruṇoktam | yad ātithyaṃ karoṣi tad vidhehi śīghram | (p.135, l.3)
bhūtenoktam | na tvayā bhetavyam | tvaṃ mama svāmī yato 'haṃ tvadgṛhadvāravṛkṣastho (p.135, l.4)
bhūtaḥ karagarābhayenehāgataḥ | tatas tava nijasvāmino guṇavad (p.135, l.5)
upakartavyam eva | tasmāt tvaṃ dvija mṛgāvatīṃ rājadhānīṃ madanabhūpatisanāthāṃ (p.135, l.6)
gaccha | tatra cāhaṃ tatputrīṃ mṛgalocanāṃ grahīṣye | sā cānyair mantrikair nīrujā (p.135, l.7)
na bhaviṣyati | tat tvayi samāgate tava darśanād evāhaṃ tyakṣyāmi | (p.135, l.8)
tataḥ paraṃ tu mantravādo na vidheyaḥ | iti bhaṇitvā so 'pi bhūto (p.135, l.9)
gatvā tāṃ rājaputrīṃ jagrāha | vipro 'pi tatra yayau | tena ca ḍiṇḍimaḥ (p.135, l.10)
spṛṣṭaḥ | tato rājakulaṃ gato vipra ācāryavistaraṃ vidadhe | bhūta (p.135, l.11)
ācāryavistare yāvan na muñcati tāvat kiṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | (p.135, l.12)
bhūtagrahe 'nivartite vipreṇoktam | (p.136, l.1)

asti devi vatsomaṃ nāma nagaram | tatra vidvān daridro brāhmaṇaḥ | tasya priyā ca karagarābhidhānā yathārthanāmnī sarvajantūdvegakāriṇī yat taddvāradeśavṛkṣasthito bhūtas tasyāḥ karagarāyā bhayāt palāyyāṭavyāṃ gataḥ | brāhmaṇo 'pi tasyā udvegād deśāntarābhimukho 'bhūt | so 'pi ca tena bhūtena dṛṣṭo jalpitaś ca | mārgaśrāntas tvam | tena tvayādya mamātithinā bhāvyam | vipreṇa bhīruṇoktam | yad ātithyaṃ karoṣi tad vidhehi śīghram | bhūtenoktam | na tvayā bhetavyam | tvaṃ mama svāmī yato 'haṃ tvadgṛhadvāravṛkṣastho bhūtaḥ karagarābhayenehāgataḥ | tatas tava nijasvāmino guṇavad upakartavyam eva | tasmāt tvaṃ dvija mṛgāvatīṃ rājadhānīṃ madanabhūpatisanāthāṃ gaccha | tatra cāhaṃ tatputrīṃ mṛgalocanāṃ grahīṣye | sā cānyair mantrikair nīrujā na bhaviṣyati | tat tvayi samāgate tava darśanād evāhaṃ tyakṣyāmi | tataḥ paraṃ tu mantravādo na vidheyaḥ | iti bhaṇitvā so 'pi bhūto gatvā tāṃ rājaputrīṃ jagrāha | vipro 'pi tatra yayau | tena ca ḍiṇḍimaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ | tato rājakulaṃ gato vipra ācāryavistaraṃ vidadhe | bhūta ācāryavistare yāvan na muñcati tāvat kiṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | bhūtagrahe 'nivartite vipreṇoktam |

p.136, l.1

karagaraṇāhaü āiaü bhūa eu vīsasiu ṭhiu dhutta |(p.136, l.2)
 āpaṇi boliu saṃbhari re kūḍaüṃ kiṃ maïṁ deva jutta || 46.2 (= 221) ||

(•)

karagaraṇāhaü āiaü bhūa eu vīsasiu ṭhiu dhutta | āpaṇi boliu saṃbhari re kūḍaüṃ kiṃ maïṁ deva jutta || 46.2 (= 221) ||

(•)

uktaṃ ca |

manuṣyāḥ sukulotpannā api ca brahmacāriṇaḥ |(p.136, l.4)
 na bhavanti mṛṣāvācaḥ kiṃ punar devayonayaḥ || 46.3 (= 222) ||(p.136, l.5)

uktaṃ ca |

manuṣyāḥ sukulotpannā api ca brahmacāriṇaḥ | na bhavanti mṛṣāvācaḥ kiṃ punar devayonayaḥ || 46.3 (= 222) ||

p.136, l.5

tato bhūtaḥ tyaktvā jagāma | iyaṃ muktety uktvā brāhmaṇāya rājñā sutā (p.136, l.6)
rājyārdhaṃ ca pradattam | vipro 'pi pūrṇamanoratho jagāma | iti kathāṃ (p.136, l.7)
śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.136, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

tato bhūtaḥ tyaktvā jagāma | iyaṃ muktety uktvā brāhmaṇāya rājñā sutā rājyārdhaṃ ca pradattam | vipro 'pi pūrṇamanoratho jagāma | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭcatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

(p.137, l.1)

p.137, l.1

dinam ativāhya prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.137, l.2)

p.137, l.2

gaccha devi gatā vetsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram |(p.137, l.3)
 yathā karagarānāthaḥ kṛtavān bhūtasaṃkaṭe || 47.1 (= 223) ||(p.137, l.4)
gaccha devi gatā vetsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram | yathā karagarānāthaḥ kṛtavān bhūtasaṃkaṭe || 47.1 (= 223) ||

p.137, l.4

sa karagarāpatiḥ rājakanyayā saha rājalakṣmīṃ bhuṅkte | atrāntare sa (p.137, l.5)
bhūtaḥ karṇāvatīṃ gatvā rājño bhāryāṃ sulocanāṃ jagrāha | sā madanasya (p.137, l.6)
pitṛṣvasā | sā cātyarthaṃ pīḍitā jīvitaśeṣābhūt | sāpi śatrughnanarapater (p.137, l.7)
bhāryā mātṛrājye keśavamāntrikam ākārayām āsa | sa ca nijadūtān (p.137, l.8)
preṣayitvā keśavo 'pi rājñā priyavākyaiḥ prahito 'py agantukāmukaḥ | (p.137, l.9)
tadā sa karagarāpatir bhāryānurodhato jagāma | tatra gataḥ sanmānito (p.137, l.10)
mahībhujā śatrughnena gataḥ sulocanāveśmani | sa ca bhūtas tam āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.137, l.11)
paruṣair vākyais tarjayann ity āha | mayā pratipannam ekadeśe kṛtam | adhunā tu (p.137, l.12)
vipra tvayā ātmā rakṣaṇīyaḥ | sa ca dvijo na mantraṃ na tantraṃ vijānāti | (p.137, l.13)
kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tadā taṃ bhūtaṃ jñātvā kālavedī (p.137, l.14)
kṛtāñjalir bhūtvā tatkarṇam āśrityeti jagāda dvijaḥ | (p.137, l.15)

sa karagarāpatiḥ rājakanyayā saha rājalakṣmīṃ bhuṅkte | atrāntare sa bhūtaḥ karṇāvatīṃ gatvā rājño bhāryāṃ sulocanāṃ jagrāha | sā madanasya pitṛṣvasā | sā cātyarthaṃ pīḍitā jīvitaśeṣābhūt | sāpi śatrughnanarapater bhāryā mātṛrājye keśavamāntrikam ākārayām āsa | sa ca nijadūtān preṣayitvā keśavo 'pi rājñā priyavākyaiḥ prahito 'py agantukāmukaḥ | tadā sa karagarāpatir bhāryānurodhato jagāma | tatra gataḥ sanmānito mahībhujā śatrughnena gataḥ sulocanāveśmani | sa ca bhūtas tam āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā paruṣair vākyais tarjayann ity āha | mayā pratipannam ekadeśe kṛtam | adhunā tu vipra tvayā ātmā rakṣaṇīyaḥ | sa ca dvijo na mantraṃ na tantraṃ vijānāti | kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tadā taṃ bhūtaṃ jñātvā kālavedī kṛtāñjalir bhūtvā tatkarṇam āśrityeti jagāda dvijaḥ |

p.137, l.15

prāptā karagarā bhūta pṛṣṭhalagnātra me 'dhunā |(p.137, l.16)
 yad bhartā cātra saṃprāptas tad vyākhyātum ihāgataḥ || 47.2 (= 224) ||(p.137, l.17)
prāptā karagarā bhūta pṛṣṭhalagnātra me 'dhunā | yad bhartā cātra saṃprāptas tad vyākhyātum ihāgataḥ || 47.2 (= 224) ||
śrutvaitad vacanaṃ bhīto bhūto vismitamānasaḥ |(p.137, l.18)
 yāmīti brāhmaṇaṃ proktvā (!) pātraṃ tyaktvā jagāma tat || 47.3 (= 225) ||(p.138, l.1)
śrutvaitad vacanaṃ bhīto bhūto vismitamānasaḥ | yāmīti brāhmaṇaṃ proktvā (!) pātraṃ tyaktvā jagāma tat || 47.3 (= 225) ||

p.139, l.1

sa ca rājā dharmanāśakaṃ kurvan nirdravyāṃ ca medinīṃ vidadhāno niṣiddho (p.139, l.2)
mantriṇā | tatas tenāpi mūrkheṇa rājñā sacivo 'vaṭe nikṣiptaḥ | sa (p.139, l.3)
ca saputras tatra ciraṃ tasthau | tataḥ śakaṭāle mahāmātye tatrasthe sarvatra (p.139, l.4)
mṛto mṛta iti vārttābhūt | tato vaṅgālanāthena tatparīkṣārthaṃ ātmīyapuruṣā (p.139, l.5)
ghoṭikādvayaṃ samarpya nandapārśve preṣitāḥ | yad etayor madhyāt kā (p.139, l.6)
mātā kā ca putrī iti jñātvā samāgantavyam | sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇe sadṛśe (p.139, l.7)
ghoṭike tāni ca lakṣaṇāni śālihotrajñātavyāni | yadā ca ko (p.139, l.8)
'pi nandarājye ghoṭikānirṇayaṃ kartuṃ na kṣamas tadā nandarājā vyacintayat | (p.139, l.9)
śakaṭālaṃ vināhaṃ paribhavāspadaṃ jātaḥ | (p.139, l.10)

sa ca rājā dharmanāśakaṃ kurvan nirdravyāṃ ca medinīṃ vidadhāno niṣiddho mantriṇā | tatas tenāpi mūrkheṇa rājñā sacivo 'vaṭe nikṣiptaḥ | sa ca saputras tatra ciraṃ tasthau | tataḥ śakaṭāle mahāmātye tatrasthe sarvatra mṛto mṛta iti vārttābhūt | tato vaṅgālanāthena tatparīkṣārthaṃ ātmīyapuruṣā ghoṭikādvayaṃ samarpya nandapārśve preṣitāḥ | yad etayor madhyāt kā mātā kā ca putrī iti jñātvā samāgantavyam | sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇe sadṛśe ghoṭike tāni ca lakṣaṇāni śālihotrajñātavyāni | yadā ca ko 'pi nandarājye ghoṭikānirṇayaṃ kartuṃ na kṣamas tadā nandarājā vyacintayat | śakaṭālaṃ vināhaṃ paribhavāspadaṃ jātaḥ |

p.139, l.12

p.140, l.9

mantriṇoktam | svāmin kiṃ vidheyaṃ tadādiśa | rājñoktam | asya (p.140, l.10)
vaḍabāyugalasya madhye kā mātā kā ca putrī | iti saṃdeham amīṣāṃ (p.140, l.11)
chalātmanāṃ dūtānāṃ śīghraṃ chindhi | sa kathaṃ chinat tu tatsaṃdeham iti praśnaḥ | (p.140, l.12)
śukaḥ | tato mantriṇā tad vaḍabāyugaṃ saparyāṇaṃ kārayitvā vāhyālyām ativāhya (p.140, l.13)
paryāṇarahitaṃ vidhāya śrāntaṃ saṃmocitam | tad anu tad yugalaṃ ca (p.140, l.14)
mātṛsutāviceṣṭitaṃ cakāra | mātā jihvayā sutāṃ lileha sutā ca tāṃ (p.141, l.1)
prati ativatsalābhūt | tataḥ sumantriṇā mātṛsutāviśeṣo rājño 'gre (p.141, l.2)
niveditaḥ | tataś ca śakaṭālaḥ parāṃ lakṣmīṃ prasiddhiṃ ca lebhe | iti (p.141, l.3)
kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.141, l.4)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭacatvāriṃśattamī kathā || (p.141, l.5)

mantriṇoktam | svāmin kiṃ vidheyaṃ tadādiśa | rājñoktam | asya vaḍabāyugalasya madhye kā mātā kā ca putrī | iti saṃdeham amīṣāṃ chalātmanāṃ dūtānāṃ śīghraṃ chindhi | sa kathaṃ chinat tu tatsaṃdeham iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tato mantriṇā tad vaḍabāyugaṃ saparyāṇaṃ kārayitvā vāhyālyām ativāhya paryāṇarahitaṃ vidhāya śrāntaṃ saṃmocitam | tad anu tad yugalaṃ ca mātṛsutāviceṣṭitaṃ cakāra | mātā jihvayā sutāṃ lileha sutā ca tāṃ prati ativatsalābhūt | tataḥ sumantriṇā mātṛsutāviśeṣo rājño 'gre niveditaḥ | tataś ca śakaṭālaḥ parāṃ lakṣmīṃ prasiddhiṃ ca lebhe | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭacatvāriṃśattamī kathā ||

p.141, l.8

yathā pūrvaṃ tathaiva vaṅgālanātho yaṣṭikāṃ suvṛttāṃ dhvajācchidriṇīmayīṃ (p.141, l.9)
jīvatśakaṭālaparīkṣāyaitair eva puṃbhiḥ preṣayām āsa | yathā yuṣmābhir nandarājye (p.141, l.10)
gatvā asyā yaṣṭikāyā ratnasuvarṇavajrair acitāyā ādim antaṃ (p.141, l.11)
jñātvā samāgantavyam ity ādeśātte pumāṃso nandapārśvam āgatya yaṣṭikāṃ tatpurato (p.141, l.12)
muktvā ādim antaṃ ca papracchuḥ | tac chrutvā pradhānaiḥ kalābhijñair vaṇigvarais (p.142, l.1)
tolitā ānyaiś ca kovidair avalokitā | paraṃ kenāpi ādyantavibhāgo (p.142, l.2)
na jñātaḥ | tato rājā śakaṭālam ādiśat | yat tvāṃ vinā (p.142, l.3)
ādyantavibhāgaṃ na ko 'pi jānāti | tatas tvayā nirṇayo vidheya eva | (p.142, l.4)
tato mantrī vadati | svāmin yuṣmat kṛtā saṃbhāvanāpi na niṣphalā | (p.142, l.5)

yathā pūrvaṃ tathaiva vaṅgālanātho yaṣṭikāṃ suvṛttāṃ dhvajācchidriṇīmayīṃ jīvatśakaṭālaparīkṣāyaitair eva puṃbhiḥ preṣayām āsa | yathā yuṣmābhir nandarājye gatvā asyā yaṣṭikāyā ratnasuvarṇavajrair acitāyā ādim antaṃ jñātvā samāgantavyam ity ādeśātte pumāṃso nandapārśvam āgatya yaṣṭikāṃ tatpurato muktvā ādim antaṃ ca papracchuḥ | tac chrutvā pradhānaiḥ kalābhijñair vaṇigvarais tolitā ānyaiś ca kovidair avalokitā | paraṃ kenāpi ādyantavibhāgo na jñātaḥ | tato rājā śakaṭālam ādiśat | yat tvāṃ vinā ādyantavibhāgaṃ na ko 'pi jānāti | tatas tvayā nirṇayo vidheya eva | tato mantrī vadati | svāmin yuṣmat kṛtā saṃbhāvanāpi na niṣphalā |

p.142, l.5

uktaṃ ca |

suvaṃśasyāvadātasya śaśāṅkasyeva lāñchanam |(p.142, l.6)
 kṛcchreṣu vyarthayā yatra bhūpater bhartur ājñayā || 49.2 (= 235) ||

(?)

uktaṃ ca |

suvaṃśasyāvadātasya śaśāṅkasyeva lāñchanam | kṛcchreṣu vyarthayā yatra bhūpater bhartur ājñayā || 49.2 (= 235) ||

(?)

p.142, l.7

tataś ca sa mantrī saṃbhāvito 'pi kathaṃ jñāsyatīti praśnaḥ | uttaram | (p.142, l.8)
śukaḥ prāha | tato 'sau buddhimān mantrī yaṣṭikāṃ jale cikṣepa | jñātaṃ (p.142, l.9)
ca | yato yan mūlaṃ tad īṣaj jale magnam | tac ca nṛpater niveditam | tena (p.142, l.10)
ca teṣāṃ dūtānām api kathitam | tatas te śrutvā svarājñe nyavedayan | (p.142, l.11)
tataś ca te rājāno nandādhirājasya pūrvajalpitaṃ karaṃ daduḥ | iti kathāṃ (p.142, l.12)
śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.142, l.13)
iti śukasaptatau ekonapañcāśattamī kathā ||

tataś ca sa mantrī saṃbhāvito 'pi kathaṃ jñāsyatīti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | tato 'sau buddhimān mantrī yaṣṭikāṃ jale cikṣepa | jñātaṃ ca | yato yan mūlaṃ tad īṣaj jale magnam | tac ca nṛpater niveditam | tena ca teṣāṃ dūtānām api kathitam | tatas te śrutvā svarājñe nyavedayan | tataś ca te rājāno nandādhirājasya pūrvajalpitaṃ karaṃ daduḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonapañcāśattamī kathā ||

p.143, l.4

katham etat | śukaḥ | asti devi dharāpṛṣṭhe jāṅgalābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra (p.143, l.5)
mitradvayaṃ vartate dharmabuddhir duṣṭabuddhiś ceti | anyadā tau dvāv api dhanāśayā (p.143, l.6)
deśāntaraṃ gatau | kiyadbhir dinaiḥ pracuraṃ dhanam arjayitvā svagrāmāgatau (p.143, l.7)
parasparaṃ mantraṃ cakrāte | yat pippalādho dhanaṃ kiṃcit kṣiptvānyad gṛhe nīyate | (p.143, l.8)
paścāt krameṇa vibhajyate lagnam | iti kṛtvā tau nijagṛhaṃ jagmatur (p.143, l.9)

tan niśamyatām | na ca yujyate vaktum | (p.143, l.11)

katham etat | śukaḥ | asti devi dharāpṛṣṭhe jāṅgalābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra mitradvayaṃ vartate dharmabuddhir duṣṭabuddhiś ceti | anyadā tau dvāv api dhanāśayā deśāntaraṃ gatau | kiyadbhir dinaiḥ pracuraṃ dhanam arjayitvā svagrāmāgatau parasparaṃ mantraṃ cakrāte | yat pippalādho dhanaṃ kiṃcit kṣiptvānyad gṛhe nīyate | paścāt krameṇa vibhajyate lagnam | iti kṛtvā tau nijagṛhaṃ jagmatur hṛṣṭatuṣṭau sukhāsvādatatparau sthitau | atrāntare yat kṛtaṃ duṣṭabuddhinā tan niśamyatām | na ca yujyate vaktum |

p.143, l.13

tena ca duṣṭabuddhinā tad dravyam utpāṭya gṛhītvā nijagṛham ānītam | kālakrameṇa (p.144, l.1)
ca saṃmīlitau pippalādhaḥsthitaṃ dravyaṃ grahītuṃ gatau yāvad ālokayataḥ (p.144, l.2)
tāvad dravyaṃ nāsti | dharmabuddhis tato gatvā mantriṇo 'gre ācakhyau (p.144, l.3)
dhanavṛttāntaṃ hṛtaṃ cāpi kubuddhinā | kubuddhināhṛtena uttaraṃ kṛtam | (p.144, l.4)
sahasrasya paṇo muktaḥ | etadarthe śapathaṃ dāpayiṣyāmi | mantriṇoktam evam (p.144, l.5)
evāstu | dvitīyenāpi pratipannaṃ yadā tadā mantriṇā pratibhuvau gṛhītvā (p.144, l.6)
muktau gatau gehaṃ pṛthakpṛthak | tato duṣṭabuddhir nijaṃ pitaraṃ viditārthaṃ (p.144, l.7)
kṛtvā vṛkṣakoṭare cikṣepa | prabhāte sacivas tau ca vādinau kautukī (p.144, l.8)
lokaś ca taṃ pippalaṃ yayuḥ | duṣṭabuddhiḥ snātaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ satyaṃ (p.144, l.9)
kṛtvā jagāda | idaṃ satyaṃ brūhi nagottama | yadi mayā dravyam apahṛtaṃ (p.144, l.10)
tadānena hṛtam iti vācyam | yadi na hṛtaṃ tadānena na hṛtam iti (p.144, l.11)
vācyam | iti śrutvā tatpitrā nahīti jalpitaṃ sarvalokapratyakṣam | (p.145, l.1)
tato dharmabuddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavatu | iti praśnaḥ | tatsaṃdiṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | (p.145, l.2)
dharmabuddhis taṃ śabdaṃ tatpitur jñātvā koṭare vahniṃ jajvāla | taṃ pitaraṃ koṭarāt (p.145, l.3)
pūtkurvantam ardhajvalitaṃ ca patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā duṣṭabuddher nigrahaṃ vidhāya mantrī (p.145, l.4)
dharmabuddhim ānandayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.145, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau pañcāśattamī kathā || (p.145, l.6)

tena ca duṣṭabuddhinā tad dravyam utpāṭya gṛhītvā nijagṛham ānītam | kālakrameṇa ca saṃmīlitau pippalādhaḥsthitaṃ dravyaṃ grahītuṃ gatau yāvad ālokayataḥ tāvad dravyaṃ nāsti | dharmabuddhis tato gatvā mantriṇo 'gre ācakhyau dhanavṛttāntaṃ hṛtaṃ cāpi kubuddhinā | kubuddhināhṛtena uttaraṃ kṛtam | sahasrasya paṇo muktaḥ | etadarthe śapathaṃ dāpayiṣyāmi | mantriṇoktam evam evāstu | dvitīyenāpi pratipannaṃ yadā tadā mantriṇā pratibhuvau gṛhītvā muktau gatau gehaṃ pṛthakpṛthak | tato duṣṭabuddhir nijaṃ pitaraṃ viditārthaṃ kṛtvā vṛkṣakoṭare cikṣepa | prabhāte sacivas tau ca vādinau kautukī lokaś ca taṃ pippalaṃ yayuḥ | duṣṭabuddhiḥ snātaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ satyaṃ kṛtvā jagāda | idaṃ satyaṃ brūhi nagottama | yadi mayā dravyam apahṛtaṃ tadānena hṛtam iti vācyam | yadi na hṛtaṃ tadānena na hṛtam iti vācyam | iti śrutvā tatpitrā nahīti jalpitaṃ sarvalokapratyakṣam | tato dharmabuddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavatu | iti praśnaḥ | tatsaṃdiṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | dharmabuddhis taṃ śabdaṃ tatpitur jñātvā koṭare vahniṃ jajvāla | taṃ pitaraṃ koṭarāt pūtkurvantam ardhajvalitaṃ ca patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā duṣṭabuddher nigrahaṃ vidhāya mantrī dharmabuddhim ānandayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcāśattamī kathā ||

prabhāvatī brūte | nāhaṃ vedmi | tat kathaya | śukaḥ | asti camatkārapuraṃ (p.145, l.10)
nāma nagaram | tacca caturvedacaturvarṇacaturāśramasamākulam | tataḥ kadācit (p.145, l.11)

dhṛtaḥ | tataḥ sa kathaṃ bhavatviti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sarveṣu dvijeṣu (p.146, l.4)
naṣṭeṣu sa śakaṭasthaḥ udbhrāntaṃ bhrātaraṃ sāhasika iva jagāda | bhrātaḥ (p.146, l.5)

taskarāḥ sarve 'pi naṣṭāḥ | (p.146, l.8)

p.147, l.1

katham etat | śukaḥ | śṛṇu devi | asti dharāpṛṣṭhe pratiṣṭānaṃ nāma pattanam | (p.147, l.2)
tatra sattvaśīlo rājā | tatputro durdamano nāma | tena iti (p.147, l.3)
cintitaṃ yan mayā svabhujopārjitam eva bhoktavyaṃ na tu paitṛkam iti saṃcintya (p.147, l.4)

deśāntaropari | tataś ca tair militaiś cintitaṃ yad asmākaṃ ratnabhūmir mahodadhiḥ (p.147, l.6)
sevituṃ yujyate | (p.147, l.7)

katham etat | śukaḥ | śṛṇu devi | asti dharāpṛṣṭhe pratiṣṭānaṃ nāma pattanam | tatra sattvaśīlo rājā | tatputro durdamano nāma | tena iti cintitaṃ yan mayā svabhujopārjitam eva bhoktavyaṃ na tu paitṛkam iti saṃcintya nijanagaraṃ tyaktvā samaśīlair mitraiḥ brāhmaṇakāṣṭhataḍvaṇikputraiḥ samaṃ niryayau deśāntaropari | tataś ca tair militaiś cintitaṃ yad asmākaṃ ratnabhūmir mahodadhiḥ sevituṃ yujyate |

uktaṃ yataḥ |

vidyāvatāṃ kulīnānāṃ śauryasaṃpattiśālinām |(p.147, l.8)
 sthānaṃ nareśabhavanam athavā yat tato 'dhikam || 52.2 (= 241) ||(p.147, l.9)

 gajānāṃ paṅkamagnānāṃ gajā eva dhuraṃdharāḥ || 52.3 (= 242) ||(p.147, l.11)

p.147, l.11

vicāryaivaṃ sevitaḥ payasāṃ patiḥ triḥsaptakṛtva upoṣitais taiḥ | tatas tuṣṭo (p.147, l.12)
'mbhonidhiḥ tebhyaś caturbhyaś catvāri cintāmaṇiguṇāni ratnāni dadau | (p.148, l.1)

vicāryaivaṃ sevitaḥ payasāṃ patiḥ triḥsaptakṛtva upoṣitais taiḥ | tatas tuṣṭo 'mbhonidhiḥ tebhyaś caturbhyaś catvāri cintāmaṇiguṇāni ratnāni dadau |

p.148, l.1

nivṛttāḥ kṛtakṛtyās te labdhvā ratnacatuṣṭayam |(p.148, l.2)
 viśvastā vaṇijaḥ pārśve sarva eva samārpayan || 52.4 (= 243) ||(p.148, l.3)
nivṛttāḥ kṛtakṛtyās te labdhvā ratnacatuṣṭayam | viśvastā vaṇijaḥ pārśve sarva eva samārpayan || 52.4 (= 243) ||

p.148, l.3

tato duṣṭena tena lobhābhibhūtena tadratnacatuṣṭayaṃ jaṅghāntare kṣiptvā sīvitam | (p.148, l.4)
ekadā anyadā ca mārge phūtkṛtaṃ paścād dūrasthitena vaṇijā (p.148, l.5)
muṣito 'smīti vadanaiḥ | tair uktam | kena hetunā | sā āha | mama (p.148, l.6)
mūtrotsargārthaṃ paścāt sthitasya caureṇa mātrāpahṛtā viśvāpi | evaṃ ca (p.148, l.7)
nivedite tair jñātaṃ paśya dhūrto 'yam | nūnam anena vaṇijā kim api kūṭaṃ (p.148, l.8)
kṛtaṃ bhaviṣyatīti manyamānā vivadantaḥ airāvatīṃ purīṃ yayuḥ | tatra ca (p.148, l.9)
nītisāra ityākhyāto bhūpatiḥ | tasya ca mantrī buddhisāro nāma (p.148, l.10)
jagadvikhyātaḥ | tasyaivaṃ prasiddhir deśe deśāntare ca yad vivādināṃ vacanam uktamātraṃ (p.148, l.11)
jānāti | tatas te rājaputrādyās tasmai mantriṇe ācakhyuḥ nijaṃ ratnagamanavṛttāntaṃ (p.149, l.1)
yathā jātam | tathaiva nirīkṣyāsmākaṃ madhye ratnajātaṃ vadhabandhaṃ (p.149, l.2)
vinā pṛthak pṛthak ekaikaṃ samarpaya | yadi ca nārpayasi tāni (p.149, l.3)
jñātvā tadā prasiddhir bhuvi te vyarthatāṃ yāti | buddhisāra iti śrutvā (p.149, l.4)
cintāvaṣṭabdhaḥ sthitaḥ | sa ca rājā nītisāraḥ kathaṃ syād iti praśnaḥ | (p.149, l.5)
śukaḥ prāha | yadā sa mantrī ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ tanmadhye sthitaṃ na janāti (p.149, l.6)
tadā viṣaṇṇo gṛham āyayau | atrāntare mantriputrī prāptanavayauvanā pārvatīṃ (p.149, l.7)
natvā pitur namaskāraṇāya gatā jayaśrīnāmadheyā | pitaraṃ tādṛśaṃ sacintaṃ (p.149, l.8)
dṛṣṭvā viṣādakāraṇaṃ pṛcchati sma | tato mantrī yathāsthitam ācaṣṭe | (p.149, l.9)
sutā prāha | tāta mā viṣīda | teṣāṃ nirṇayam ahaṃ kariṣye | te vivādinaḥ (p.149, l.10)
pumāṃso yadā kāraṇāyāgacchanti tadā gṛhe preṣaṇīyāḥ yathāhaṃ (p.149, l.11)
tanmadhyād ratnajātahartāraṃ samarpayāmi | sā āha | putri yan mayā na jñātaṃ (p.149, l.12)
tat tvaṃ kathaṃ jñāsyasi | sā āha | (p.149, l.13)

tato duṣṭena tena lobhābhibhūtena tadratnacatuṣṭayaṃ jaṅghāntare kṣiptvā sīvitam | ekadā anyadā ca mārge phūtkṛtaṃ paścād dūrasthitena vaṇijā muṣito 'smīti vadanaiḥ | tair uktam | kena hetunā | sā āha | mama mūtrotsargārthaṃ paścāt sthitasya caureṇa mātrāpahṛtā viśvāpi | evaṃ ca nivedite tair jñātaṃ paśya dhūrto 'yam | nūnam anena vaṇijā kim api kūṭaṃ kṛtaṃ bhaviṣyatīti manyamānā vivadantaḥ airāvatīṃ purīṃ yayuḥ | tatra ca nītisāra ityākhyāto bhūpatiḥ | tasya ca mantrī buddhisāro nāma jagadvikhyātaḥ | tasyaivaṃ prasiddhir deśe deśāntare ca yad vivādināṃ vacanam uktamātraṃ jānāti | tatas te rājaputrādyās tasmai mantriṇe ācakhyuḥ nijaṃ ratnagamanavṛttāntaṃ yathā jātam | tathaiva nirīkṣyāsmākaṃ madhye ratnajātaṃ vadhabandhaṃ vinā pṛthak pṛthak ekaikaṃ samarpaya | yadi ca nārpayasi tāni jñātvā tadā prasiddhir bhuvi te vyarthatāṃ yāti | buddhisāra iti śrutvā cintāvaṣṭabdhaḥ sthitaḥ | sa ca rājā nītisāraḥ kathaṃ syād iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ prāha | yadā sa mantrī ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ tanmadhye sthitaṃ na janāti tadā viṣaṇṇo gṛham āyayau | atrāntare mantriputrī prāptanavayauvanā pārvatīṃ natvā pitur namaskāraṇāya gatā jayaśrīnāmadheyā | pitaraṃ tādṛśaṃ sacintaṃ dṛṣṭvā viṣādakāraṇaṃ pṛcchati sma | tato mantrī yathāsthitam ācaṣṭe | sutā prāha | tāta mā viṣīda | teṣāṃ nirṇayam ahaṃ kariṣye | te vivādinaḥ pumāṃso yadā kāraṇāyāgacchanti tadā gṛhe preṣaṇīyāḥ yathāhaṃ tanmadhyād ratnajātahartāraṃ samarpayāmi | sā āha | putri yan mayā na jñātaṃ tat tvaṃ kathaṃ jñāsyasi | sā āha |

p.149, l.13

na caitat tāta vaktavyaṃ bhinnā buddhir hi dehiṣu |(p.150, l.1)
 ko 'pi kiṃcid vijānāti jagaty atra kalāparaḥ || 52.5 (= 244) ||(p.150, l.2)
na caitat tāta vaktavyaṃ bhinnā buddhir hi dehiṣu | ko 'pi kiṃcid vijānāti jagaty atra kalāparaḥ || 52.5 (= 244) ||

p.150, l.2

kiṃ ca |

muṇḍe muṇḍe matir bhinnā kuṇḍe kuṇḍe navaṃ payaḥ |(p.150, l.3)
 tuṇḍe tuṇḍe navā vāṇī gehe gehe pativratā || 52.6 (= 245) ||(p.150, l.4)

kiṃ ca |

muṇḍe muṇḍe matir bhinnā kuṇḍe kuṇḍe navaṃ payaḥ | tuṇḍe tuṇḍe navā vāṇī gehe gehe pativratā || 52.6 (= 245) ||
prajñāvisphāritākṣāṇāṃ vidravanti vipattayaḥ |(p.150, l.5)
 hastodyatapradīpānām andhakāra ivāgrataḥ || 52.7 (= 246) ||(p.150, l.6)
prajñāvisphāritākṣāṇāṃ vidravanti vipattayaḥ | hastodyatapradīpānām andhakāra ivāgrataḥ || 52.7 (= 246) ||

p.150, l.6

tasmāt tāta nātra kāpi cintā kāryā | prasthāpyās te 'nyadeśinaḥ yathā (p.150, l.7)
tān prabodhayāmi | prasthāpitās te mantriṇā tayāpi snāpitā bhojitāś ca (p.150, l.8)
pṛthak pṛthak śāyitāḥ | tataḥ sā śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya pradhānaṃ rājaputraṃ (p.150, l.9)
prāha | ahaṃ ratyarthinī tava pārśvaṃ samāgatā | tvaṃ ca mahyaṃ kāñcanaśataṃ (p.150, l.10)
dattvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tenoktam | ahaṃ tava dravyaṃ rājyaṃ copārjya dāsyāmi | (p.150, l.11)
param adhunā na kiṃcana vidyate | iti taṃ nirdravyaṃ jñātvā brāhmaṇaṃ (p.150, l.12)
gatā | brāhmaṇam api pūrvoktam evoktavatī | brāhmaṇo jagāda | yadas matpituḥ (p.150, l.13)
pārśve dravyaṃ śāsanabaddhā bhūmir api tat sarvaṃ tubhyaṃ dāsye | tam api nirdhanaṃ (p.150, l.14)
jñātvā parityajya sūtradhāraṃ yayau | āha ca saḥ | sāṃprataṃ mama pārśve (p.150, l.15)
kiṃcin na vidyate paraṃ paścāl lākṣaṃ dāsyāmi | tam api nirdravyaṃ parityajya (p.151, l.1)
vaṇiksutaṃ yayau | tathaiva gaditavatī | sa āha | svāmini ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ (p.151, l.2)
gṛhītvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tato jaṅghāyāḥ samākṛṣya ratnajātaṃ samarpayām (p.151, l.3)
āsa | tataḥ sā savyājam utthāya śīlarakṣāṃ kurvāṇā jayaśrīr gṛham āyayau | (p.151, l.4)
ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ pitur arpayām āsa | mantry api tān ākārya nijaṃ nijaṃ (p.151, l.5)
ratnaṃ samarpayām āsa | te 'pi svaratnalābhāt kṛtakṛtyā nijaṃ nijaṃ gṛhaṃ (p.151, l.6)
yayuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.151, l.7)
iti śukasaptatī dvipañcāśattamī kathā || (p.151, l.8)

tasmāt tāta nātra kāpi cintā kāryā | prasthāpyās te 'nyadeśinaḥ yathā tān prabodhayāmi | prasthāpitās te mantriṇā tayāpi snāpitā bhojitāś ca pṛthak pṛthak śāyitāḥ | tataḥ sā śṛṅgāraṃ vidhāya pradhānaṃ rājaputraṃ prāha | ahaṃ ratyarthinī tava pārśvaṃ samāgatā | tvaṃ ca mahyaṃ kāñcanaśataṃ dattvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tenoktam | ahaṃ tava dravyaṃ rājyaṃ copārjya dāsyāmi | param adhunā na kiṃcana vidyate | iti taṃ nirdravyaṃ jñātvā brāhmaṇaṃ gatā | brāhmaṇam api pūrvoktam evoktavatī | brāhmaṇo jagāda | yadas matpituḥ pārśve dravyaṃ śāsanabaddhā bhūmir api tat sarvaṃ tubhyaṃ dāsye | tam api nirdhanaṃ jñātvā parityajya sūtradhāraṃ yayau | āha ca saḥ | sāṃprataṃ mama pārśve kiṃcin na vidyate paraṃ paścāl lākṣaṃ dāsyāmi | tam api nirdravyaṃ parityajya vaṇiksutaṃ yayau | tathaiva gaditavatī | sa āha | svāmini ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ gṛhītvā māṃ bhuṅkṣva | tato jaṅghāyāḥ samākṛṣya ratnajātaṃ samarpayām āsa | tataḥ sā savyājam utthāya śīlarakṣāṃ kurvāṇā jayaśrīr gṛham āyayau | ratnacatuṣṭayaṃ pitur arpayām āsa | mantry api tān ākārya nijaṃ nijaṃ ratnaṃ samarpayām āsa | te 'pi svaratnalābhāt kṛtakṛtyā nijaṃ nijaṃ gṛhaṃ yayuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatī dvipañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 53

p.151, l.8

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ provāca | (p.151, l.9)

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ provāca |

p.151, l.9

vraja rambhoru yuktaṃ te gamanaṃ viṣame sati |(p.151, l.10)
 cet kartum uttaraṃ vetsi carmakārakalatravat || 53.1 (= 247) ||(p.151, l.11)
vraja rambhoru yuktaṃ te gamanaṃ viṣame sati | cet kartum uttaraṃ vetsi carmakārakalatravat || 53.1 (= 247) ||

p.151, l.11

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ | carmaṇvatīnadītīre carmakūṭa (p.151, l.12)
iti grāmaḥ | tatra ca dohaḍo nāma carmakāraḥ | tasya devikā nāma (p.151, l.13)
bhāryā paraṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tataḥ sa carmakāraś carmaṇāṃ krayaṇāya yadā (p.152, l.1)
bahir nirgataḥ tadā tayā upapatiḥ samānītaḥ | tayoś cāntaḥ suratasevinoḥ (p.152, l.2)
patiś carmasamāyukto bahir āgataḥ | tataḥ sa upapatiḥ sā ca kathaṃ (p.152, l.3)
bhavetām | iti praśnaḥ | tatpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā patir (p.152, l.4)
jñātaḥ samāgacchan tadā iti vākyaṃ vadati tvaritaṃ niḥsṛtā | (p.152, l.5)

prabhāvatī pṛcchati | katham etat | śukaḥ | carmaṇvatīnadītīre carmakūṭa iti grāmaḥ | tatra ca dohaḍo nāma carmakāraḥ | tasya devikā nāma bhāryā paraṃ parapuruṣalampaṭā | tataḥ sa carmakāraś carmaṇāṃ krayaṇāya yadā bahir nirgataḥ tadā tayā upapatiḥ samānītaḥ | tayoś cāntaḥ suratasevinoḥ patiś carmasamāyukto bahir āgataḥ | tataḥ sa upapatiḥ sā ca kathaṃ bhavetām | iti praśnaḥ | tatpṛṣṭaḥ śukaḥ prāha | yadā ca tayā patir jñātaḥ samāgacchan tadā iti vākyaṃ vadati tvaritaṃ niḥsṛtā |

p.152, l.7

tatas tad vākyaṃ śrutvā bhīto māntrikam ākaraṇāya sa mūrkho bhramituṃ gato (p.152, l.8)
grāme yāvat tāvat tayā ca niḥsārito jāraḥ svaveśma gataḥ | tatas tvam (p.152, l.9)

iti śukasaptatau tripañcāśattamī kathā ||

tatas tad vākyaṃ śrutvā bhīto māntrikam ākaraṇāya sa mūrkho bhramituṃ gato grāme yāvat tāvat tayā ca niḥsārito jāraḥ svaveśma gataḥ | tatas tvam apy uttaraṃ viṣame yadi vetsi tadā gaccha | anyathā śayanaṃ kuru | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau tripañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 54

(p.153, l.1)

p.153, l.1

athātivāhya dinaṃ prabhāvatī gamanotsukā punaḥ śukaṃ pṛcchati | sa prāha | (p.153, l.2)

athātivāhya dinaṃ prabhāvatī gamanotsukā punaḥ śukaṃ pṛcchati | sa prāha |

p.153, l.2

ko doṣo gamyatāṃ devi yadi tvaṃ vetsi bhāṣitum |(p.153, l.3)
 dūtena bhāṣitaṃ yadvad viṣame nṛpateḥ puraḥ || 54.1 (= 248) ||(p.153, l.4)
ko doṣo gamyatāṃ devi yadi tvaṃ vetsi bhāṣitum | dūtena bhāṣitaṃ yadvad viṣame nṛpateḥ puraḥ || 54.1 (= 248) ||

p.153, l.4

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti śakrāvatī nāma purī | (p.153, l.5)
tasyāṃ dharmadatto nāma rājā dharmādiguṇopetaḥ | tasyāmātyaḥ suśīlo (p.153, l.6)
nāma | tasya ca suto viṣṇunāmā saṃdhivigrahikaḥ pūrvam āsīt | tasmāt (p.153, l.7)
padād yadā bhraṣṭo dravyahīnaḥ kulāmātyo 'ham ity ahaṃkṛtaḥ karkaśaś ca | tato (p.153, l.8)
rājā na kiṃcid vadati | mantrī ca kadācin nṛpam āha | devāsya viṣṇor (p.153, l.9)
upari kim iti ko 'pi prasādo na vidhīyate | rājā ca tasyopari (p.153, l.10)
vimukhas tato na kiṃcid vadati | punar apy uktaṃ mantriṇā | svāminn ayaṃ viṣṇur (p.153, l.11)
bhakto raktaḥ pravīṇo dūtakarmaṇi | tad devapādaiḥ kvāpi preṣayitvā (p.154, l.1)
parīkṣaṇīyaḥ | tato rājā tad vākyaṃ śrutvā tatpratikūlaḥ san bhasmaprābhṛtaṃ (p.154, l.2)
mudrayā mudritaṃ samarpya śatrudamananṛpapārśve vidiśāyāṃ nagaryāṃ taṃ preṣayām (p.154, l.3)
āsa | so 'pi ca tatra gatas tatprābhṛtaṃ bhasmamayam ajānan mudritaṃ rājñaḥ (p.154, l.4)
puro muktavān | tasmiṃś cāmaṅgalakāriṇi prābhṛte rājño 'gre mukte rājā (p.154, l.5)
kopāṭopasahito babhūva | tataḥ sa dūtas tasmin prābhṛte samānīte kathaṃ (p.154, l.6)
kṣemam avāpnotu | iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa viṣṇus taṃ kruddhaṃ (p.154, l.7)
dṛṣṭvā buddhimān idam uvāca | svāmin madīyena nāthenāśvamedho yajñaḥ kṛtaḥ | (p.154, l.8)
tasya kuṇḍasya tretāgnisaṃbhavaṃ pavitraṃ śreyaskaram aghāpahaṃ bhasma vandanāya (p.154, l.9)
samarpitavān | (p.154, l.10)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti śakrāvatī nāma purī | tasyāṃ dharmadatto nāma rājā dharmādiguṇopetaḥ | tasyāmātyaḥ suśīlo nāma | tasya ca suto viṣṇunāmā saṃdhivigrahikaḥ pūrvam āsīt | tasmāt padād yadā bhraṣṭo dravyahīnaḥ kulāmātyo 'ham ity ahaṃkṛtaḥ karkaśaś ca | tato rājā na kiṃcid vadati | mantrī ca kadācin nṛpam āha | devāsya viṣṇor upari kim iti ko 'pi prasādo na vidhīyate | rājā ca tasyopari vimukhas tato na kiṃcid vadati | punar apy uktaṃ mantriṇā | svāminn ayaṃ viṣṇur bhakto raktaḥ pravīṇo dūtakarmaṇi | tad devapādaiḥ kvāpi preṣayitvā parīkṣaṇīyaḥ | tato rājā tad vākyaṃ śrutvā tatpratikūlaḥ san bhasmaprābhṛtaṃ mudrayā mudritaṃ samarpya śatrudamananṛpapārśve vidiśāyāṃ nagaryāṃ taṃ preṣayām āsa | so 'pi ca tatra gatas tatprābhṛtaṃ bhasmamayam ajānan mudritaṃ rājñaḥ puro muktavān | tasmiṃś cāmaṅgalakāriṇi prābhṛte rājño 'gre mukte rājā kopāṭopasahito babhūva | tataḥ sa dūtas tasmin prābhṛte samānīte kathaṃ kṣemam avāpnotu | iti praśnaḥ | śuka uttaraṃ prāha | sa viṣṇus taṃ kruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā buddhimān idam uvāca | svāmin madīyena nāthenāśvamedho yajñaḥ kṛtaḥ | tasya kuṇḍasya tretāgnisaṃbhavaṃ pavitraṃ śreyaskaram aghāpahaṃ bhasma vandanāya samarpitavān |

p.154, l.10

yataḥ |

gajāḥ santi hayāḥ santi vicitrāḥ santi saṃpadaḥ |(p.155, l.1)
 tvadīye ca madīye ca durlabhaṃ bhasma yājñikam || 54.2 (= 249) ||(p.155, l.2)

yataḥ |

gajāḥ santi hayāḥ santi vicitrāḥ santi saṃpadaḥ | tvadīye ca madīye ca durlabhaṃ bhasma yājñikam || 54.2 (= 249) ||

p.155, l.2

ity uktvā sahasotthāya kare bhasma kṛtvā rājñe samarpayām āsa | sa ca (p.155, l.3)
tena vacasā tuṣṭiparo vavande | tenāpi tuṣṭena pratiprābhṛtaṃ mahat preṣitam | (p.155, l.4)
sa ca viṣṇuḥ saṃmānya visarjitaḥ | tatas tvam api bhāmini viṣame uttaraṃ (p.155, l.5)
jānāsi yadi tadā gamyatām anyathā tiṣṭha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī (p.155, l.6)
suptā | (p.155, l.7)
iti śukasaptatau catuḥpañcāśattamī kathā || (p.155, l.8)

ity uktvā sahasotthāya kare bhasma kṛtvā rājñe samarpayām āsa | sa ca tena vacasā tuṣṭiparo vavande | tenāpi tuṣṭena pratiprābhṛtaṃ mahat preṣitam | sa ca viṣṇuḥ saṃmānya visarjitaḥ | tatas tvam api bhāmini viṣame uttaraṃ jānāsi yadi tadā gamyatām anyathā tiṣṭha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catuḥpañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 55

p.155, l.8

anyadā yāminīsamaye prabhāvatī gamanāya śukam āpṛcchati | kīra (p.155, l.9)
uvāca | (p.155, l.10)

anyadā yāminīsamaye prabhāvatī gamanāya śukam āpṛcchati | kīra uvāca |

p.155, l.10

gaccha rambhoru gamanaṃ yujyate gajagāmini |(p.155, l.11)
 yadi vetsy uttaraṃ kartuṃ śrīdharo brāhmaṇo yathā || 55.1 (= 250) ||(p.156, l.1)
gaccha rambhoru gamanaṃ yujyate gajagāmini | yadi vetsy uttaraṃ kartuṃ śrīdharo brāhmaṇo yathā || 55.1 (= 250) ||

p.156, l.1

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuko brūte | carmakūṭe grāme dvijaḥ śrīdharo (p.156, l.2)
nāma | tatraiva candanākhyaś carmakāraḥ | tatpārśvāt śrīdhareṇopānahayugalaṃ (p.156, l.3)
kāritam | carmakāro 'pi nityam eva dravyaṃ yācate | vipro 'pi vadati | (p.156, l.4)
tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣye | evaṃ sumahān kālo yayau | sa vipro (p.156, l.5)
'nyadā carmakāreṇa vidhṛtaḥ | dhanaṃ vinā sa vipraḥ kathaṃ mucyate | tat kathayeti (p.156, l.6)
praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | etasminn antare grāmapālasya gṛhe (p.156, l.7)
suto jātaḥ | tato dvijaḥ prāha chalānveṣī san | carmakṛn mayā pūrvam (p.156, l.8)
uktam | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣyāmi | tad asmin sute jāte tvaṃ hṛṣṭacitto (p.156, l.9)
na veti | yadi sa brūte nāhaṃ hṛṣṭacitta iti tadā rājñā grāhyaḥ (p.156, l.10)
syāt | anyathā ca dravyaṃ yāti | tatas tenoktam | hṛṣṭacitto 'haṃ jātaḥ | (p.157, l.1)
tato dvijaś chalenātmānaṃ vimucya gataḥ | tato bhāmini yady evam uttaraṃ (p.157, l.2)
jānāsi tadā gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.157, l.3)
iti śukasaptatau pañcapañcāśattamī kathā || (p.157, l.4)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śuko brūte | carmakūṭe grāme dvijaḥ śrīdharo nāma | tatraiva candanākhyaś carmakāraḥ | tatpārśvāt śrīdhareṇopānahayugalaṃ kāritam | carmakāro 'pi nityam eva dravyaṃ yācate | vipro 'pi vadati | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣye | evaṃ sumahān kālo yayau | sa vipro 'nyadā carmakāreṇa vidhṛtaḥ | dhanaṃ vinā sa vipraḥ kathaṃ mucyate | tat kathayeti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | etasminn antare grāmapālasya gṛhe suto jātaḥ | tato dvijaḥ prāha chalānveṣī san | carmakṛn mayā pūrvam uktam | tvāṃ hṛṣṭacittaṃ kariṣyāmi | tad asmin sute jāte tvaṃ hṛṣṭacitto na veti | yadi sa brūte nāhaṃ hṛṣṭacitta iti tadā rājñā grāhyaḥ syāt | anyathā ca dravyaṃ yāti | tatas tenoktam | hṛṣṭacitto 'haṃ jātaḥ | tato dvijaś chalenātmānaṃ vimucya gataḥ | tato bhāmini yady evam uttaraṃ jānāsi tadā gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau pañcapañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 56

p.157, l.4

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.157, l.5)

athāparedyuḥ prabhāvatī gamanāya śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.157, l.5

yāhi devi gatā vetsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram |(p.157, l.6)
 viṣame sāntako yadvad vaṇikputraḥ purākarot || 56.1 (= 251) ||(p.157, l.7)
yāhi devi gatā vetsi yadi kartuṃ tvam uttaram | viṣame sāntako yadvad vaṇikputraḥ purākarot || 56.1 (= 251) ||

p.157, l.7

asty atra tripatho nāma grāmaḥ | tatra sāntako nāma vaṇik mahādhanī (p.157, l.8)
kṛpaṇo duṣṭaśīlo grāmāntarapriyaś ca | tataś ca grāmāntarād udgrāhaṇikāṃ (p.157, l.9)
kṛtvā āgacchan pathi caurair dhṛtaḥ sa bhāmini kathaṃ caurabhayān mucyate | (p.157, l.10)
iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | sa vaṇikputra ātmānaṃ caurair dhṛtaṃ jñātvā (p.158, l.1)
galagrahanāmno yakṣasya samīpavartino 'ntikaṃ yayau | tasyāgrataś ca (p.158, l.2)
dravyaṃ muktvā haste ca khaṭikām ādāya yakṣādhīśam idam abravīt | (p.158, l.3)

asty atra tripatho nāma grāmaḥ | tatra sāntako nāma vaṇik mahādhanī kṛpaṇo duṣṭaśīlo grāmāntarapriyaś ca | tataś ca grāmāntarād udgrāhaṇikāṃ kṛtvā āgacchan pathi caurair dhṛtaḥ sa bhāmini kathaṃ caurabhayān mucyate | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | sa vaṇikputra ātmānaṃ caurair dhṛtaṃ jñātvā galagrahanāmno yakṣasya samīpavartino 'ntikaṃ yayau | tasyāgrataś ca dravyaṃ muktvā haste ca khaṭikām ādāya yakṣādhīśam idam abravīt |

p.158, l.3

dhanodgrāhaṇikā deva kṛteyaṃ tava sarvataḥ |(p.158, l.4)
 idaṃ dravyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ tiṣṭhaty anyac ca vṛddhimat || 56.2 (= 252) ||(p.158, l.5)
dhanodgrāhaṇikā deva kṛteyaṃ tava sarvataḥ | idaṃ dravyaṃ mayā labdhaṃ tiṣṭhaty anyac ca vṛddhimat || 56.2 (= 252) ||

p.158, l.5

taṃ lekhakaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā yakṣadhanam iti jñātvā taṃ praṇamya te gatāś caurāḥ | (p.158, l.6)
sa ca dravyaṃ gṛhītvā kṣemeṇa gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī (p.158, l.7)
suptā | (p.158, l.8)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭpañcāśattamī kathā || (p.158, l.9)

taṃ lekhakaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā yakṣadhanam iti jñātvā taṃ praṇamya te gatāś caurāḥ | sa ca dravyaṃ gṛhītvā kṣemeṇa gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭpañcāśattamī kathā ||

tatra nāyakaguṇāḥ |

hato manyusahasrair yaḥ saṃtapto madanāgninā | raktaś ca yo viraktāyāṃ so 'dhamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 57.11 (= 263) ||

 na tāḥ kāmayate namro madhyamo nāyakaḥ smṛtaḥ || 57.12 (= 264) ||(p.162, l.8)

 tayāpi kāmyate 'tyartham uttamaḥ so 'bhidhīyate || 57.13 (= 265) ||(p.162, l.10)

nāyikās tridhā |

 rasajñā kṛtyakuśalā sottamā nāyikā smṛtā || 57.14 (= 266) ||(p.163, l.1)

nāyikās tridhā |

kārye gṛhṇāti roṣaṃ yā gataroṣā priyānugā | rasajñā kṛtyakuśalā sottamā nāyikā smṛtā || 57.14 (= 266) ||

 māninī mānahīnā ca kṣaṇāt sā madhyamā smṛtā || 57.15 (= 267) ||(p.163, l.3)
asthāne kopamānā yā yā duḥkhānunayā tathā | māninī mānahīnā ca kṣaṇāt sā madhyamā smṛtā || 57.15 (= 267) ||
lubdhā yātīva capalā vacane nīrasākṣarā |(p.163, l.4)

p.163, l.5

tayoś ca śayanaṃ tridhā |

 vimardaṃ sahate 'tyarthaṃ suratāsaktayos tayoḥ || 57.17 (= 269) ||(p.163, l.8)

tayoś ca śayanaṃ tridhā |

pārśvayor unnatiṃ nītaṃ nimnamadhye priyasya tat | vimardaṃ sahate 'tyarthaṃ suratāsaktayos tayoḥ || 57.17 (= 269) ||
madhyamasya punaḥ kāryaṃ śayanaṃ samabhūmikam |(p.163, l.9)
 praviralāṅgasaṃsparśā nityaṃ yāti niśā yathā || 57.18 (= 270) ||(p.163, l.10)
madhyamasya punaḥ kāryaṃ śayanaṃ samabhūmikam | praviralāṅgasaṃsparśā nityaṃ yāti niśā yathā || 57.18 (= 270) ||
dveṣyasya tulyam uttuṅgaṃ madhye nīcaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ |(p.164, l.1)
 na śakyeta kalākalpo yatra rantuṃ nirantaram || 57.19 (= 271) ||(p.164, l.2)
dveṣyasya tulyam uttuṅgaṃ madhye nīcaṃ ca pārśvayoḥ | na śakyeta kalākalpo yatra rantuṃ nirantaram || 57.19 (= 271) ||
ity anunnatatalpasthā bhuktā muktā vipaścitā |(p.164, l.3)
 mahiṣī ratisaṃtuṣṭā pratyūṣe svagṛhaṃ yayau || 57.20 (= 272) ||(p.164, l.4)
ity anunnatatalpasthā bhuktā muktā vipaścitā | mahiṣī ratisaṃtuṣṭā pratyūṣe svagṛhaṃ yayau || 57.20 (= 272) ||

p.164, l.4

rājā ca prātaḥ sarvāvasarānantaraṃ paṇḍitaṃ rājñīṃ cājuhāva | siṃhāsane (p.164, l.5)
ca paṇḍitam upaveśayām āsa | śubhaṃkaraṃ prati hasan vārtāprabandheneti (p.164, l.6)
jagāda | kṛtakaṃ manye bhayaṃ yoṣitām iti vacanaṃ śrutvā svadoṣavismitamānasaḥ (p.164, l.7)
saṃjātaḥ | sa rājñā jñātaḥ kathaṃ bhavitv iti praśnaḥ | (p.164, l.8)

rājā ca prātaḥ sarvāvasarānantaraṃ paṇḍitaṃ rājñīṃ cājuhāva | siṃhāsane ca paṇḍitam upaveśayām āsa | śubhaṃkaraṃ prati hasan vārtāprabandheneti jagāda | kṛtakaṃ manye bhayaṃ yoṣitām iti vacanaṃ śrutvā svadoṣavismitamānasaḥ saṃjātaḥ | sa rājñā jñātaḥ kathaṃ bhavitv iti praśnaḥ |

 kiṃ punaḥ pṛthivīpālagṛhe doṣo vimucyate || 57.21 (= 273) ||(p.164, l.10)

yataḥ |

vāṇīm udīrayat | (p.164, l.12)

uttaram | śukaḥ prāha | tataś ca sa budho rājñā jñāto 'ham iti saṃcintyeti vāṇīm udīrayat |

p.164, l.12

ugragrāham udanvato jalam atikrāmaty anālambane(p.165, l.1)
vyomnisthāpi ca durgam akṣitibhṛtāṃ mūrdhānam ārohati |(p.165, l.2)
 vyāptaṃ yāti viṣākulair ahikulaiḥ pātālam ekākinī(p.165, l.3)
kīrtis te madanāvatāra kṛtakaṃ manye bhayaṃ yoṣitām || 57.22 (= 274) ||(p.165, l.4)
ugragrāham udanvato jalam atikrāmaty anālambane vyomnisthāpi ca durgam akṣitibhṛtāṃ mūrdhānam ārohati | vyāptaṃ yāti viṣākulair ahikulaiḥ pātālam ekākinī kīrtis te madanāvatāra kṛtakaṃ manye bhayaṃ yoṣitām || 57.22 (= 274) ||

p.165, l.4

iti paṇḍitapaṭhitaṃ śrutvā rājā taṃ budhaṃ tāṃ ca rājñīṃ dṛṣṭvā iti (p.165, l.5)
cintayām āsa | durlabho 'yaṃ budhaḥ | sulabhāḥ khalu nārya iti vicintya (p.165, l.6)
mahiṣīṃ haste dhṛtvā tasmai viduṣe dadau | uvāca ca | gṛhāṇemāṃ mahiṣīm | (p.165, l.7)
paritoṣitaḥ paṇḍito 'pi mahāprasāda ity avocat | (p.165, l.8)

iti paṇḍitapaṭhitaṃ śrutvā rājā taṃ budhaṃ tāṃ ca rājñīṃ dṛṣṭvā iti cintayām āsa | durlabho 'yaṃ budhaḥ | sulabhāḥ khalu nārya iti vicintya mahiṣīṃ haste dhṛtvā tasmai viduṣe dadau | uvāca ca | gṛhāṇemāṃ mahiṣīm | paritoṣitaḥ paṇḍito 'pi mahāprasāda ity avocat |

p.165, l.8

uktaṃ ca |

guṇadoṣau na śāstrajñaḥ kathaṃ vibhajate janaḥ |(p.165, l.9)
 kim andhasyādhikāro 'sti rūpadoṣopalabdhiṣu || 57.23 (= 275) ||(p.165, l.10)

uktaṃ ca |

guṇadoṣau na śāstrajñaḥ kathaṃ vibhajate janaḥ | kim andhasyādhikāro 'sti rūpadoṣopalabdhiṣu || 57.23 (= 275) ||

p.165, l.10

paṇḍito 'pi rājñaḥ prasādāt sukhaṃ bhuṅkte tayā samam | yady evaṃ prabhāvati (p.165, l.11)
tvam api samaye vaktuṃ jānāsi tadā gamyatām | anyathā sthīyatām | (p.165, l.12)
iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.165, l.13)
iti śukasaptatau saptapañcāśattamī kathā ||

paṇḍito 'pi rājñaḥ prasādāt sukhaṃ bhuṅkte tayā samam | yady evaṃ prabhāvati tvam api samaye vaktuṃ jānāsi tadā gamyatām | anyathā sthīyatām | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptapañcāśattamī kathā ||

§ 58

(p.166, l.1)

p.166, l.1

anyadā pradoṣe calitā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ | (p.166, l.2)

anyadā pradoṣe calitā prabhāvatī śukaṃ pṛcchati | śukaḥ |

p.166, l.2

ratyarthini vrajādya tvaṃ rantuṃ cet samayocitam |(p.166, l.3)
 duḥśīlāpativad vetsi kartuṃ gaṇapateḥ puraḥ || 58.1 (= 276) ||(p.166, l.4)
ratyarthini vrajādya tvaṃ rantuṃ cet samayocitam | duḥśīlāpativad vetsi kartuṃ gaṇapateḥ puraḥ || 58.1 (= 276) ||

p.166, l.4

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti lohapurī nāma nagaram | (p.166, l.5)
tasmiṃś ca rājaḍo nāma pāmaraḥ | tasyāpi patnī parapuruṣalampaṭā duḥśīlety (p.166, l.6)
āhvayā | sā ca sūtravikrayārthaṃ sakhībhiḥ sametya padmāvatīṃ purīṃ (p.166, l.7)
prayāti | tataś ca grāmasamīpasthasya gaṇapates tābhiḥ pṛthak pṛthak upayācitam (p.166, l.8)
uktam | tayā tu cumbanam upayācitam uktaṃ madanākrāntadehayā | sa (p.166, l.9)
ca tāsāṃ prabhūtaṃ lābhaṃ cakre | tataḥ sarvābhir anyābhir ātmīyātmīyam upayācitaṃ (p.166, l.10)
tasmai gaṇeśāya pradattam | tayā ca nagnībhūya cumbanaṃ kṛtam | (p.166, l.11)
tataḥ kelipriyeṇa tena sā adhare dhṛtā | tasmiṃś ca dhṛte sā kukkuṭīva (p.166, l.12)
tatra sthitā | taṃ ca vṛttāntaṃ tanmokṣaṇāya tadbhartuḥ sakhyo 'pahasamānā nivedayām (p.167, l.1)
āsuḥ | so 'pi tad vacanaṃ śrutvā tatrāgamat | tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ (p.167, l.2)
dṛṣṭvā sa vyacintayat | katham iyaṃ mucyata iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tāṃ (p.167, l.3)
tathāsthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ san rāsabhaṃ rantum ārebhe | tataś ca sa gaṇapatis (p.167, l.4)
tathāvidhaṃ kautukaṃ dṛṣṭvā jahāsa | hasatas tasya oṣṭhau śithilau jātau | (p.167, l.5)
tataḥ sā muktā satī praṇamya nijaṃ nāthaṃ tarjayantī gṛhaṃ yayau | (p.167, l.6)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti lohapurī nāma nagaram | tasmiṃś ca rājaḍo nāma pāmaraḥ | tasyāpi patnī parapuruṣalampaṭā duḥśīlety āhvayā | sā ca sūtravikrayārthaṃ sakhībhiḥ sametya padmāvatīṃ purīṃ prayāti | tataś ca grāmasamīpasthasya gaṇapates tābhiḥ pṛthak pṛthak upayācitam uktam | tayā tu cumbanam upayācitam uktaṃ madanākrāntadehayā | sa ca tāsāṃ prabhūtaṃ lābhaṃ cakre | tataḥ sarvābhir anyābhir ātmīyātmīyam upayācitaṃ tasmai gaṇeśāya pradattam | tayā ca nagnībhūya cumbanaṃ kṛtam | tataḥ kelipriyeṇa tena sā adhare dhṛtā | tasmiṃś ca dhṛte sā kukkuṭīva tatra sthitā | taṃ ca vṛttāntaṃ tanmokṣaṇāya tadbhartuḥ sakhyo 'pahasamānā nivedayām āsuḥ | so 'pi tad vacanaṃ śrutvā tatrāgamat | tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ dṛṣṭvā sa vyacintayat | katham iyaṃ mucyata iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tāṃ tathāsthitāṃ dṛṣṭvā sakāmaḥ san rāsabhaṃ rantum ārebhe | tataś ca sa gaṇapatis tathāvidhaṃ kautukaṃ dṛṣṭvā jahāsa | hasatas tasya oṣṭhau śithilau jātau | tataḥ sā muktā satī praṇamya nijaṃ nāthaṃ tarjayantī gṛhaṃ yayau |

p.167, l.6

kṛtaṃ tena rataṃ devi samayocitam īdṛśam |(p.167, l.7)
 svakārye mocitā sāpi duḥśīlā vighnanāyakāt || 58.2 (= 277) ||(p.167, l.8)
kṛtaṃ tena rataṃ devi samayocitam īdṛśam | svakārye mocitā sāpi duḥśīlā vighnanāyakāt || 58.2 (= 277) ||
samayocitam ārambhaṃ kurute yas tu kṛtyavit |(p.167, l.9)
 sarvadā tu phalaṃ tasya samayajño hi śiṣyate || 58.3 (= 278) ||(p.167, l.10)
samayocitam ārambhaṃ kurute yas tu kṛtyavit | sarvadā tu phalaṃ tasya samayajño hi śiṣyate || 58.3 (= 278) ||

p.167, l.10

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.167, l.11)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭapañcāśattamī kathā || (p.167, l.12)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭapañcāśattamī kathā ||

p.167, l.12

atha dinānte sā śukaṃ gamanāya pṛcchati sma | śukaḥ | (p.167, l.13)

p.167, l.13

gaccha devi svakāryaṃ ca kuru cintitam adbhutam |(p.167, l.14)
 rukmiṇīvad vijānāsi patiṃ vañcitum uddhatam || 59.1 (= 279) ||(p.168, l.1)
gaccha devi svakāryaṃ ca kuru cintitam adbhutam | rukmiṇīvad vijānāsi patiṃ vañcitum uddhatam || 59.1 (= 279) ||

p.168, l.1

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti saṃgamo nāma grāmaḥ | tatra (p.168, l.2)
rāhaḍo nāma rājaputraḥ sakopaḥ | tasya bhāryā rukmiṇī nāma | sa (p.168, l.3)
ca tayā sārdhaṃ devayātrāyāṃ calitaḥ | sā ca narāntaraṃ kaṭākṣayantī (p.168, l.4)
tena dṛṣṭā pumāṃś ca | tataḥ sa tan mithunaṃ tathāvidhaṃ jñātvā tāṃ tadanuraktāṃ (p.168, l.5)
mene | (p.168, l.6)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti saṃgamo nāma grāmaḥ | tatra rāhaḍo nāma rājaputraḥ sakopaḥ | tasya bhāryā rukmiṇī nāma | sa ca tayā sārdhaṃ devayātrāyāṃ calitaḥ | sā ca narāntaraṃ kaṭākṣayantī tena dṛṣṭā pumāṃś ca | tataḥ sa tan mithunaṃ tathāvidhaṃ jñātvā tāṃ tadanuraktāṃ mene |

baddhabhaṇiāi kanto tahea addhacchipicchiā dhāī |(p.168, l.7)
 ūsasiaṃ pi muṇijjaï chaïllajaṇasaṃkule gāme || 59.2 (= 280) ||

uktaṃ ca |

baddhabhaṇiāi kanto tahea addhacchipicchiā dhāī | ūsasiaṃ pi muṇijjaï chaïllajaṇasaṃkule gāme || 59.2 (= 280) ||

p.169, l.1

tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ vikṛtāṃ jñātvā ca rāhaḍo gṛham agamat | dhikkṛtya paruṣākṣarair (p.169, l.2)
gṛhāntare yantritāṃ dhārayām āsa | sā ca cintayati | mama janma (p.169, l.3)
jīvitaṃ yauvanaṃ ca tadā saphalaṃ yadā etasya pratyakṣaṃ narāntaram upabhokṣye | (p.169, l.4)
pratijñātaṃ ca manasā dṛḍham | tata ātmīyapratijñāṃ kathaṃ nirvāhayatv iti (p.169, l.5)
praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā kadācit taṃ hṛdayasthaṃ naraṃ gṛhapārśve gacchantaṃ (p.169, l.6)
dṛṣṭvā taṃ pratyāha | adya rātrau tvayāsmadgṛhāṅgaṇasthaciñciṇīmūle nijakāyākāragartāyām (p.169, l.7)
ūrdhvaliṅginā śayanaṃ vidheyam iti | sa tatheti pratijñāya (p.169, l.8)
rātrau tathā bhūtvā sthitaḥ | sā ca kāmārtā sarvakaraṇacaturā (p.169, l.9)
tatra yayau | agārabhūmim uddiśya bhartāram āhvayati sma | sā (p.170, l.1)
ciñciṇīcchāyāyāṃ gatvā tasya liṅgasyopari upaviśya satūṇadhanuṣaṃ (p.170, l.2)
tam abravīt | (p.170, l.3)

tāṃ tathāvidhāṃ vikṛtāṃ jñātvā ca rāhaḍo gṛham agamat | dhikkṛtya paruṣākṣarair gṛhāntare yantritāṃ dhārayām āsa | sā ca cintayati | mama janma jīvitaṃ yauvanaṃ ca tadā saphalaṃ yadā etasya pratyakṣaṃ narāntaram upabhokṣye | pratijñātaṃ ca manasā dṛḍham | tata ātmīyapratijñāṃ kathaṃ nirvāhayatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā kadācit taṃ hṛdayasthaṃ naraṃ gṛhapārśve gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ pratyāha | adya rātrau tvayāsmadgṛhāṅgaṇasthaciñciṇīmūle nijakāyākāragartāyām ūrdhvaliṅginā śayanaṃ vidheyam iti | sa tatheti pratijñāya rātrau tathā bhūtvā sthitaḥ | sā ca kāmārtā sarvakaraṇacaturā tatra yayau | agārabhūmim uddiśya bhartāram āhvayati sma | sā ciñciṇīcchāyāyāṃ gatvā tasya liṅgasyopari upaviśya satūṇadhanuṣaṃ tam abravīt |

p.170, l.3

dhānuṣko 'si pradhāno 'si loke khyātiṃ gato 'si ca |(p.170, l.4)
 chindhi me candrikām adya pauruṣaṃ gaṇayāmi te || 59.3 (= 291) ||(p.170, l.5)
dhānuṣko 'si pradhāno 'si loke khyātiṃ gato 'si ca | chindhi me candrikām adya pauruṣaṃ gaṇayāmi te || 59.3 (= 291) ||

p.170, l.5

sa ca mūrkhas tad vacanam idaṃ śrutvā saśaraṃ dhanur ādāya candrikāṃ lakṣīkṛtya (p.170, l.6)
bāṇaṃ mumoca | tena mukto 'pi bāṇo nākāśagatāṃ candrikāṃ bhinatti | (p.170, l.7)
adhaḥ sa vedhyād bhraṣṭaḥ | tasmiṃś ca patyāvaparāddheṣau sati sā viparītaratakṣamā (p.170, l.8)
sahastatālaṃ tam idam āha | (p.170, l.9)

sa ca mūrkhas tad vacanam idaṃ śrutvā saśaraṃ dhanur ādāya candrikāṃ lakṣīkṛtya bāṇaṃ mumoca | tena mukto 'pi bāṇo nākāśagatāṃ candrikāṃ bhinatti | adhaḥ sa vedhyād bhraṣṭaḥ | tasmiṃś ca patyāvaparāddheṣau sati sā viparītaratakṣamā sahastatālaṃ tam idam āha |

 śūro hi kuhito 'si tvaṃ yāsyāmīti jagāda tam || 59.5 (= 293) ||(p.171, l.5)

p.171, l.5

ity uktvopapatyā samānītaṃ hayam āruhya jagāma | gacchantīṃ ca tāṃ tato (p.171, l.6)
dṛṣṭvā rāhaḍo 'pi lajjito viguptaś ca | tataḥ strīṇāṃ vaśagaḥ ko na (p.171, l.7)
viḍambitaḥ | (p.171, l.8)

ity uktvopapatyā samānītaṃ hayam āruhya jagāma | gacchantīṃ ca tāṃ tato dṛṣṭvā rāhaḍo 'pi lajjito viguptaś ca | tataḥ strīṇāṃ vaśagaḥ ko na viḍambitaḥ |

p.171, l.8

yataḥ |

ānanarta purā śaṃbhur govindo rāsakṛt tathā |(p.171, l.9)
 brahmā paśutvam āpannaḥ strībhiḥ ko na viḍambitaḥ || 59.6 (= 294) ||(p.171, l.10)

yataḥ |

ānanarta purā śaṃbhur govindo rāsakṛt tathā | brahmā paśutvam āpannaḥ strībhiḥ ko na viḍambitaḥ || 59.6 (= 294) ||
saṃsāravṛkṣamūlaṃ yāḥ pāpakandalabhūmikā |(p.171, l.11)
 saṃtāpaphalapuṣpāṇi yoṣitaḥ kiṃ sukhāvahāḥ || 59.7 (= 295) ||(p.171, l.12)
saṃsāravṛkṣamūlaṃ yāḥ pāpakandalabhūmikā | saṃtāpaphalapuṣpāṇi yoṣitaḥ kiṃ sukhāvahāḥ || 59.7 (= 295) ||
māyāmūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ tasyā mūlaṃ hi yoṣitaḥ |(p.171, l.13)
 saṃyogo yoṣitāṃ mūlaṃ taṃ tyaktvā ca sukhāni naḥ || 59.8 (= 296) ||(p.172, l.1)
māyāmūlam idaṃ sarvaṃ tasyā mūlaṃ hi yoṣitaḥ | saṃyogo yoṣitāṃ mūlaṃ taṃ tyaktvā ca sukhāni naḥ || 59.8 (= 296) ||

p.172, l.1

tasyedaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā prabhāvatī prāha | (p.172, l.2)

tasyedaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā prabhāvatī prāha |

p.172, l.2

utpattikāraṇaṃ tanvī tanvī vṛddheś ca kāraṇam |(p.172, l.3)
 sukhasya kāraṇaṃ tanvī sā kathaṃ kīra duṣyate || 59.9 (= 297) ||(p.172, l.4)
utpattikāraṇaṃ tanvī tanvī vṛddheś ca kāraṇam | sukhasya kāraṇaṃ tanvī sā kathaṃ kīra duṣyate || 59.9 (= 297) ||
vinā tābhir na saṃbhogo vinā tābhiḥ sukhaṃ na ca |(p.172, l.5)
 vinā tābhir na cātmānaṃ kṛtārthaṃ manyate janaḥ || 59.10 (= 298) ||(p.172, l.6)

kacchādhipatinā devi tasya rājñaḥ sabhā śrutā |(p.173, l.6)
 vicitrā devanirmitā sarvaratnavibhūṣitā || 60.2 (= 303) ||(p.173, l.7)

p.173, l.9

sa dūtas tatpurīṃ gatvā nṛpaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ jagāda | matsvāmināhaṃ sacitrāṃ (p.173, l.10)
tava sabhām avalokayitum utkalitaḥ | rājā prāha | prātar darśayiṣye | (p.174, l.1)
tato rājñā dvitīyadine dūta ākāritaḥ | sa ca sahasāgatas tāṃ sabhāṃ (p.174, l.2)
vicitraratnakhacitāṃ dṛṣṭvā jalamayīṃ sthalamayīṃ veti niścetum aśaktaḥ kathaṃ (p.174, l.3)
bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sa pūgīphalaṃ puraḥ kṣiptvā sthalaṃ jñātvā (p.174, l.4)
gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.174, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭitamī kathā || (p.174, l.6)

sa dūtas tatpurīṃ gatvā nṛpaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ jagāda | matsvāmināhaṃ sacitrāṃ tava sabhām avalokayitum utkalitaḥ | rājā prāha | prātar darśayiṣye | tato rājñā dvitīyadine dūta ākāritaḥ | sa ca sahasāgatas tāṃ sabhāṃ vicitraratnakhacitāṃ dṛṣṭvā jalamayīṃ sthalamayīṃ veti niścetum aśaktaḥ kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tataḥ sa pūgīphalaṃ puraḥ kṣiptvā sthalaṃ jñātvā gṛhaṃ yayau | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

p.174, l.6

anyadā sā śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka prāha | (p.174, l.7)

anyadā sā śukaṃ pṛcchati sma | śuka prāha |

p.174, l.7

gaccha devi gatā vetsi rantuṃ cet tvaṃ nijaṃ naram |(p.174, l.8)
 yathā tejukayā pūrvaṃ kṛtaṃ ciram ākāṅkṣitam || 61.1 (= 305) ||(p.175, l.1)
gaccha devi gatā vetsi rantuṃ cet tvaṃ nijaṃ naram | yathā tejukayā pūrvaṃ kṛtaṃ ciram ākāṅkṣitam || 61.1 (= 305) ||

p.175, l.1

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti khorasamābhidhāno (p.175, l.2)
grāmaḥ | tatra vaṇikputraḥ pārśvanāganāmā | tasya bhāryā rūpasaṃpannā ratalolupā (p.175, l.3)
kulaṭā tejukā nāma | sānyadā sakhībhir vṛtā devayātrālokanāya (p.175, l.4)
gatā surūpasyaikasya puṃsaḥ rūpaṃ prekṣya saṃgamāya manaś cakre | (p.175, l.5)

prabhāvaty āha | katham etat | śukaḥ kathayati | asti khorasamābhidhāno grāmaḥ | tatra vaṇikputraḥ pārśvanāganāmā | tasya bhāryā rūpasaṃpannā ratalolupā kulaṭā tejukā nāma | sānyadā sakhībhir vṛtā devayātrālokanāya gatā surūpasyaikasya puṃsaḥ rūpaṃ prekṣya saṃgamāya manaś cakre |

p.175, l.5

yataḥ |

vivāhe devayātrāyāṃ rājaveśmani saṃkaṭe |(p.175, l.6)
 paragehe vivāde ca devi nārī vinaśyati || 61.2 (= 306) ||(p.175, l.7)

yataḥ |

vivāhe devayātrāyāṃ rājaveśmani saṃkaṭe | paragehe vivāde ca devi nārī vinaśyati || 61.2 (= 306) ||

uktaṃ ca |

gṛhe 'raṇye tathā deve havye tīrthe jalāśaye |(p.175, l.8)
 vivāhe cotsave nityaṃ mālinīnilaye tathā || 61.3 (= 307) ||(p.175, l.9)

uktaṃ ca |

gṛhe 'raṇye tathā deve havye tīrthe jalāśaye | vivāhe cotsave nityaṃ mālinīnilaye tathā || 61.3 (= 307) ||
yātrāyāṃ strīsamūhe ca nirjane janasaṃkule |(p.175, l.10)
 pattane ca tathā grāme svacchandā dvāravartinī || 61.4 (= 308) ||(p.176, l.1)
yātrāyāṃ strīsamūhe ca nirjane janasaṃkule | pattane ca tathā grāme svacchandā dvāravartinī || 61.4 (= 308) ||
khale kṣetre pravāse ca mārge veśmani catvare |(p.176, l.2)
 praveśe nirgame rājñāṃ sadā yā kautukapriyā || 61.5 (= 309) ||(p.176, l.3)
khale kṣetre pravāse ca mārge veśmani catvare | praveśe nirgame rājñāṃ sadā yā kautukapriyā || 61.5 (= 309) ||
prativeśmagṛhe śūnye rajakīsūcikīgṛhe |(p.176, l.4)
 divārātrau ca saṃdhyāyāṃ durdine rājacatvare |(p.176, l.5)
 śoke ca vyasane bhartuḥ svacchandā strī vinaśyati || 61.6 (= 310) ||(p.176, l.6)
prativeśmagṛhe śūnye rajakīsūcikīgṛhe | divārātrau ca saṃdhyāyāṃ durdine rājacatvare | śoke ca vyasane bhartuḥ svacchandā strī vinaśyati || 61.6 (= 310) ||

p.176, l.6

tejukā ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhrūsaṃjñayā āhūyedam abravīt | ahaṃ tavāsaktā paraṃ (p.176, l.7)
madīyo bhartā duḥsaho niṣṭhuraś ca gṛhād bahir nirgantuṃ notsahe | ato yasmiṃs (p.176, l.8)
tasmin divase 'smadgṛhadvāri ghaṭe kṣiptvā vṛściko moktavyaḥ | tadāhaṃ (p.176, l.9)
vṛścikadaṣṭā bhaviṣyāmi | tvayāsmadgṛhadvāri vaidyena bhāvyam | iti saṃketaṃ (p.176, l.10)
vidhāya svagṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tenāpi tathā kṛtam | sāpi ghaṭaṃ khaṭvocchīrṣake (p.176, l.11)
kṣiptvā iti jagāda | aham anena vṛścikena ghaṭasthena daṣṭā | (p.177, l.1)
iti rāraṭīti | so 'pi ca puruṣas tadā vaidyo bhūtvā tadgṛhadvāri (p.177, l.2)
tasthau | tāḍaṃ bandhaü poṭṭaṃ malaü sūlaṃ pheḍaü visaṃ haraü iti jalpati | (p.177, l.3)
tadā ca sā bhartāraṃ jagāda | (p.177, l.4)

tejukā ca taṃ dṛṣṭvā bhrūsaṃjñayā āhūyedam abravīt | ahaṃ tavāsaktā paraṃ madīyo bhartā duḥsaho niṣṭhuraś ca gṛhād bahir nirgantuṃ notsahe | ato yasmiṃs tasmin divase 'smadgṛhadvāri ghaṭe kṣiptvā vṛściko moktavyaḥ | tadāhaṃ vṛścikadaṣṭā bhaviṣyāmi | tvayāsmadgṛhadvāri vaidyena bhāvyam | iti saṃketaṃ vidhāya svagṛhaṃ jagmatuḥ | tenāpi tathā kṛtam | sāpi ghaṭaṃ khaṭvocchīrṣake kṣiptvā iti jagāda | aham anena vṛścikena ghaṭasthena daṣṭā | iti rāraṭīti | so 'pi ca puruṣas tadā vaidyo bhūtvā tadgṛhadvāri tasthau | tāḍaṃ bandhaü poṭṭaṃ malaü sūlaṃ pheḍaü visaṃ haraü iti jalpati | tadā ca sā bhartāraṃ jagāda |

p.177, l.4

dehi kāṣṭhāni me nātha mariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ |(p.177, l.5)
 āhūya māntrikān vaidyān gatārtiṃ vā kuruṣva mām || 61.7 (= 311) ||(p.177, l.6)
dehi kāṣṭhāni me nātha mariṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ | āhūya māntrikān vaidyān gatārtiṃ vā kuruṣva mām || 61.7 (= 311) ||

p.177, l.6

tatas tadbhartā gṛhād bahiḥ sthitaṃ tam ākārayām āsa | vaidyo 'pi tāṃ dṛṣṭvā (p.177, l.7)
tatpatiṃ jagāda | yady eṣā kāladaṣṭā jīvati tatas tvaṃ bhāgyavān aham api (p.177, l.8)
yaśaḥpātraṃ bhavāmi | vaṇig āha | vaidya prasādaṃ vidhāya enāṃ viṣarahitāṃ (p.177, l.9)
kuru | tataḥ sa vaidyaḥ kenāpi kaṭukabhaiṣajyena vanitauṣṭham ālipya tatpatim (p.178, l.1)
āha | aho vaṇik sarveṣām api viṣāṇāṃ samadhikaṃ mānuṣaviṣam eva | (p.178, l.2)
tato viṣasya viṣam auṣadham iti kṛtvā tvam asyā oṣṭhaṃ dhāva | tato (p.178, l.3)
vaṇik tathā kartum ārebhe | kṣaṇamātreṇa tasya vaṇijaḥ kaṭukauṣadhamiśrauṣṭhāsvādena (p.178, l.4)
mukhaṃ kaṭukaṃ saṃjātam | tato vaṇig āha | tvam evauṣṭhaṃ dhāvety uktvā (p.178, l.5)
vaṇik sthitaḥ | vaṇijo 'pi viṣaśaṅkārūḍhā | tato bahir gate vaṇiji (p.178, l.6)
vaidyena sā kāmārtā yathecchaṃ bhojitā | tad anantaraṃ sā māyinī svasthābhūt | (p.178, l.7)
vaṇig api kṣaṇena svastho babhūva | upakṛtaś ca vaidyas tena caraṇaiḥ (p.178, l.8)
spṛṣṭvā tvadīyo 'smīti | tataḥ sa vaidyacchadmanā gṛham āyāti satataṃ (p.179, l.1)
vaṇiji bahir gate bhuṅkte ca tāṃ nityam | tato bhāmini evaṃ kartuṃ vaktuṃ (p.179, l.2)
ca yadi jānāsi tato yāhi | (p.179, l.3)

tatas tadbhartā gṛhād bahiḥ sthitaṃ tam ākārayām āsa | vaidyo 'pi tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatpatiṃ jagāda | yady eṣā kāladaṣṭā jīvati tatas tvaṃ bhāgyavān aham api yaśaḥpātraṃ bhavāmi | vaṇig āha | vaidya prasādaṃ vidhāya enāṃ viṣarahitāṃ kuru | tataḥ sa vaidyaḥ kenāpi kaṭukabhaiṣajyena vanitauṣṭham ālipya tatpatim āha | aho vaṇik sarveṣām api viṣāṇāṃ samadhikaṃ mānuṣaviṣam eva | tato viṣasya viṣam auṣadham iti kṛtvā tvam asyā oṣṭhaṃ dhāva | tato vaṇik tathā kartum ārebhe | kṣaṇamātreṇa tasya vaṇijaḥ kaṭukauṣadhamiśrauṣṭhāsvādena mukhaṃ kaṭukaṃ saṃjātam | tato vaṇig āha | tvam evauṣṭhaṃ dhāvety uktvā vaṇik sthitaḥ | vaṇijo 'pi viṣaśaṅkārūḍhā | tato bahir gate vaṇiji vaidyena sā kāmārtā yathecchaṃ bhojitā | tad anantaraṃ sā māyinī svasthābhūt | vaṇig api kṣaṇena svastho babhūva | upakṛtaś ca vaidyas tena caraṇaiḥ spṛṣṭvā tvadīyo 'smīti | tataḥ sa vaidyacchadmanā gṛham āyāti satataṃ vaṇiji bahir gate bhuṅkte ca tāṃ nityam | tato bhāmini evaṃ kartuṃ vaktuṃ ca yadi jānāsi tato yāhi |

p.179, l.3

evaṃ kartuṃ ca vaktuṃ ca yo jānāti chalapriyaḥ |(p.179, l.4)
 sa karotu sa yātv evaṃ kartuṃ bhoktuṃ nijaṃ hitam || 61.8 (= 312) ||(p.179, l.5)
evaṃ kartuṃ ca vaktuṃ ca yo jānāti chalapriyaḥ | sa karotu sa yātv evaṃ kartuṃ bhoktuṃ nijaṃ hitam || 61.8 (= 312) ||

p.179, l.5

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.179, l.6)
iti śukasaptatau ekaṣaṣṭitamī kathā || (p.179, l.7)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

§ 62

p.179, l.7

anyadā sā prabhāvatī śukam āpṛcchati | śukaḥ prāha | (p.179, l.8)

anyadā sā prabhāvatī śukam āpṛcchati | śukaḥ prāha |

p.179, l.8

priyam evānubhoktavyaṃ yāhi devi tadarthinī |(p.179, l.9)
 kuhanasya yathā kānte saṃkaṭe 'si kṣamottare || 62.1 (= 313) ||(p.180, l.1)
priyam evānubhoktavyaṃ yāhi devi tadarthinī | kuhanasya yathā kānte saṃkaṭe 'si kṣamottare || 62.1 (= 313) ||

p.180, l.1

asti gambhīrākhyo grāmaḥ | tatra kuhano nāma rājaputra īrṣyāluḥ śūro (p.180, l.2)
jaḍaḥ strīpriyo durdharaś ca | tasyābhūtāṃ dve kalatre śobhikātejikākhye (p.180, l.3)
ratalolupe parapuruṣalampaṭe surūpe | tadbhartā tadrakṣaṇāya grāmād bahir nadītīre (p.180, l.4)
gṛhaṃ cakre | dvārasthas te rakṣayati | anyadā sa tābhyām uktaḥ | yadā (p.180, l.5)
kaścin nāpitaḥ samabhyeti tadā bhavyaṃ bhavati | tatas tenāpi bhrāmako nāpitaḥ (p.180, l.6)
preṣitaḥ pratisīrāntarais tayor nakhakalpanāya | tataś ca tayoś caraṇān (p.180, l.7)
tiras kariṇībahiḥsthān nāpitaḥ prakṣālayati | patiś cādūre pathi niviṣṭaḥ | (p.180, l.8)
tābhyāṃ ca sa nāpitaḥ suvarṇakaṭakam arpayitvā pracchannam evam uktaḥ | etad dravyaṃ (p.180, l.9)
gṛhītvā āvayoḥ kenāpi sārdhaṃ saṃyogaṃ vidhehi | divākīrtir api (p.180, l.10)
tatheti pratijñāya rājaputram āpṛcchya jagāma | anyadātmamitraṃ navayauvanaṃ (p.181, l.1)
kalāpātram anudgataśmaśruṃ strīveṣaṃ kārayitvā tayoḥ patyuḥ pārśve tena saha (p.181, l.2)
samāgatya nāpita idam āha | mameyaṃ vallabhā | ahaṃ ca grāmāntaraṃ jigamiṣur (p.181, l.3)
yuṣmadgṛhaṃ vinānyatra moktuṃ na śaknomi | yato bhavatāṃ gṛhe strīyantraṇā (p.181, l.4)
bhavyā | ity ukte tena pratipannaṃ muñceti | tataś caṇḍālo 'pi taṃ (p.181, l.5)
muktvā tayoḥ pārśve gato jagāda yad iyaṃ yuṣmābhir ātmīyā karaṇīyā | (p.181, l.6)
tatas te taṃ caṇḍālānītaṃ jñātvā bahu menāte | sa ca divā strīrūpī (p.181, l.7)
rātrau ca kāmukaḥ rājaputrakalatre prativāraṃ bhuṅkte | sa ca rājaputraḥ (p.181, l.8)
strīlolupas tatsaṅgamāya spṛhayati | yayāce ca tāṃ nityam | sā tu (p.181, l.9)
kapaṭastrī neti jagāda | tato rājaputrasya strītve bhrāntir utpannā | tadbhrāntim (p.181, l.10)
apanetuṃ nijakalatre jagāda | devyādeśān mayā prātar mahotsavo vidheyaḥ | (p.182, l.1)
tatra bhavatībhir vivastrābhis tisṛbhir api nartitavyam | tataḥ sa strīcchadmā (p.182, l.2)
kathaṃ nṛtyatu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tantryā liṅgāgraṃ niyamya (p.182, l.3)
gudamadhyagam ānamya sphuṭāṃ bhagākṛtiṃ kṛtvā patyau samāgate sahastatālaṃ (p.182, l.4)
sarvā evaṃ vadantyo nanṛtuḥ | (p.182, l.5)

asti gambhīrākhyo grāmaḥ | tatra kuhano nāma rājaputra īrṣyāluḥ śūro jaḍaḥ strīpriyo durdharaś ca | tasyābhūtāṃ dve kalatre śobhikātejikākhye ratalolupe parapuruṣalampaṭe surūpe | tadbhartā tadrakṣaṇāya grāmād bahir nadītīre gṛhaṃ cakre | dvārasthas te rakṣayati | anyadā sa tābhyām uktaḥ | yadā kaścin nāpitaḥ samabhyeti tadā bhavyaṃ bhavati | tatas tenāpi bhrāmako nāpitaḥ preṣitaḥ pratisīrāntarais tayor nakhakalpanāya | tataś ca tayoś caraṇān tiras kariṇībahiḥsthān nāpitaḥ prakṣālayati | patiś cādūre pathi niviṣṭaḥ | tābhyāṃ ca sa nāpitaḥ suvarṇakaṭakam arpayitvā pracchannam evam uktaḥ | etad dravyaṃ gṛhītvā āvayoḥ kenāpi sārdhaṃ saṃyogaṃ vidhehi | divākīrtir api tatheti pratijñāya rājaputram āpṛcchya jagāma | anyadātmamitraṃ navayauvanaṃ kalāpātram anudgataśmaśruṃ strīveṣaṃ kārayitvā tayoḥ patyuḥ pārśve tena saha samāgatya nāpita idam āha | mameyaṃ vallabhā | ahaṃ ca grāmāntaraṃ jigamiṣur yuṣmadgṛhaṃ vinānyatra moktuṃ na śaknomi | yato bhavatāṃ gṛhe strīyantraṇā bhavyā | ity ukte tena pratipannaṃ muñceti | tataś caṇḍālo 'pi taṃ muktvā tayoḥ pārśve gato jagāda yad iyaṃ yuṣmābhir ātmīyā karaṇīyā | tatas te taṃ caṇḍālānītaṃ jñātvā bahu menāte | sa ca divā strīrūpī rātrau ca kāmukaḥ rājaputrakalatre prativāraṃ bhuṅkte | sa ca rājaputraḥ strīlolupas tatsaṅgamāya spṛhayati | yayāce ca tāṃ nityam | sā tu kapaṭastrī neti jagāda | tato rājaputrasya strītve bhrāntir utpannā | tadbhrāntim apanetuṃ nijakalatre jagāda | devyādeśān mayā prātar mahotsavo vidheyaḥ | tatra bhavatībhir vivastrābhis tisṛbhir api nartitavyam | tataḥ sa strīcchadmā kathaṃ nṛtyatu | iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tantryā liṅgāgraṃ niyamya gudamadhyagam ānamya sphuṭāṃ bhagākṛtiṃ kṛtvā patyau samāgate sahastatālaṃ sarvā evaṃ vadantyo nanṛtuḥ |

p.182, l.5

p.182, l.7

rājaputro 'rthaṃ papraccha | tābhyām uktam | markaṭī kaṭisaṃdhir ucyate | tatas (p.182, l.8)

ucchedya duḥkhaśamanaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā tvam eva ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● (p.183, l.12)
● ● ● ● ● ● tasmāt tava paragṛhaṃ gantuṃ na yujyate | (p.184, l.1)

yathā śakaṭālena nijakuṭumbamaraṇāya samudbhavad duḥkhaṃ cāṇakyapārśvāt nandakulam ucchedya duḥkhaśamanaṃ kṛtaṃ tathā tvam eva ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● ● tasmāt tava paragṛhaṃ gantuṃ na yujyate |

p.184, l.1

uktaṃ ca |

uḍugaṇaparivāro nāyako 'py oṣadhīnām(p.184, l.2)
amṛtamayaśarīraḥ kāntiyukto 'pi candraḥ |(p.184, l.3)
 bhavati vikalamūrtir maṇḍalaṃ prāpya bhānoḥ(p.184, l.4)
parasadananiviṣṭaḥ ko na dhatte laghutvam || 63.2 (= 317) ||(p.184, l.5)

uktaṃ ca |

uḍugaṇaparivāro nāyako 'py oṣadhīnām amṛtamayaśarīraḥ kāntiyukto 'pi candraḥ | bhavati vikalamūrtir maṇḍalaṃ prāpya bhānoḥ parasadananiviṣṭaḥ ko na dhatte laghutvam || 63.2 (= 317) ||

p.184, l.5

p.184, l.10

prabhāvatī prāha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti kūṭapurābhidho grāmaḥ | (p.185, l.1)
tatra rājaputraḥ somarājaḥ | tasya maṇḍukā nāma patnī priyadarśanā (p.185, l.2)
narāntaralolupā | tāṃ caiko naraḥ kṛtasaṃketaḥ saghaṇṭako rātrau gṛhāṅgaṇe (p.185, l.3)
bhuṅkte | tatpatir ghaṇṭāśabdaṃ śṛṇvann ekadā laguḍam ādāya pradhāvitaḥ ṣaṇḍaśaṅkayā | (p.185, l.4)
tataḥ ṣaṇḍaveṣadhārī upapatiḥ kathaṃ bhavitv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | (p.185, l.5)
devikā nāma sakhī maṇḍukāyāḥ patiṃ ghaṇṭāśabdānusāriṇam āgacchantaṃ (p.185, l.6)
dṛṣṭvā jārasya naśyato ghaṇṭālālāṃ haste dhṛtvā taṃ prati jagāda | bhāvuka (p.185, l.7)
kāṃdiśīko vṛṣo naṣṭaḥ | tataḥ sa vyāvṛtya nijapauruṣaṃ patnyai kathayām (p.185, l.8)
āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.185, l.9)
iti śukasaptatau catuḥṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

prabhāvatī prāha | katham etat | śukaḥ | asti kūṭapurābhidho grāmaḥ | tatra rājaputraḥ somarājaḥ | tasya maṇḍukā nāma patnī priyadarśanā narāntaralolupā | tāṃ caiko naraḥ kṛtasaṃketaḥ saghaṇṭako rātrau gṛhāṅgaṇe bhuṅkte | tatpatir ghaṇṭāśabdaṃ śṛṇvann ekadā laguḍam ādāya pradhāvitaḥ ṣaṇḍaśaṅkayā | tataḥ ṣaṇḍaveṣadhārī upapatiḥ kathaṃ bhavitv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | devikā nāma sakhī maṇḍukāyāḥ patiṃ ghaṇṭāśabdānusāriṇam āgacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā jārasya naśyato ghaṇṭālālāṃ haste dhṛtvā taṃ prati jagāda | bhāvuka kāṃdiśīko vṛṣo naṣṭaḥ | tataḥ sa vyāvṛtya nijapauruṣaṃ patnyai kathayām āsa | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau catuḥṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

jahasuḥ | pṛṣṭaḥ sarvair jagāda | īdṛśo 'yaṃ śiṣyaḥ | mayoktaṃ māṃ saṃvartata (p.186, l.10)

p.188, l.3

tatra gavyūtivistīrṇe śītacchāye jalāśayatīrasthite vaṭe śaṅkhadhavalo (p.188, l.4)
nāma haṃsarāṭ sakuṭumbo medinīṃ bhrāntvā dinātyaye śete | (p.189, l.1)
anyadā teṣu haṃseṣu bhramaṇāya gateṣu pāparddhinā jālaṃ baddham | pradoṣāgatāḥ (p.189, l.2)
patitāḥ sarve 'pi kathaṃ mucyante | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tatas tu (p.189, l.3)
svaṃ kuṭumbaṃ tathā baddhaṃ jñātvā rātrau śaṅkhadhavalaḥ prāha | re re putrā (p.189, l.4)
yadāsau lubdhakaḥ prātar bhūruhaṃ samāruhya yuṣmān avalokayati tadā bhavadbhir (p.189, l.5)
mṛtakalpair ucchvāsaniḥśvāsarahitaiḥ sthātavyam | so 'pi yuṣmān mṛtān (p.189, l.6)
iti jñātvā yadā bhūmau sarvān kṣipati tadā sarvair apy uḍḍīya gantavyam | (p.189, l.7)
iti kṛte lubdhakaḥ prātaḥ samāyayau | tena te mṛtā iti (p.189, l.8)
jñātvā bhūmau kṣiptāḥ tadā te uḍḍīya kāṅkṣitaṃ deśaṃ yayuḥ | iti (p.189, l.9)
kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.189, l.10)
iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

tatra gavyūtivistīrṇe śītacchāye jalāśayatīrasthite vaṭe śaṅkhadhavalo nāma haṃsarāṭ sakuṭumbo medinīṃ bhrāntvā dinātyaye śete | anyadā teṣu haṃseṣu bhramaṇāya gateṣu pāparddhinā jālaṃ baddham | pradoṣāgatāḥ patitāḥ sarve 'pi kathaṃ mucyante | iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | tatas tu svaṃ kuṭumbaṃ tathā baddhaṃ jñātvā rātrau śaṅkhadhavalaḥ prāha | re re putrā yadāsau lubdhakaḥ prātar bhūruhaṃ samāruhya yuṣmān avalokayati tadā bhavadbhir mṛtakalpair ucchvāsaniḥśvāsarahitaiḥ sthātavyam | so 'pi yuṣmān mṛtān iti jñātvā yadā bhūmau sarvān kṣipati tadā sarvair apy uḍḍīya gantavyam | iti kṛte lubdhakaḥ prātaḥ samāyayau | tena te mṛtā iti jñātvā bhūmau kṣiptāḥ tadā te uḍḍīya kāṅkṣitaṃ deśaṃ yayuḥ | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||
