p.191, l.10

ity uktvā punaḥ prāha | mitra tvam adyātithir asmākaṃ bhava | iti bhaṇitvā (p.192, l.1)
amṛtasadṛśāni pakvaphalāni dadau | tataḥ prabhṛti pratidinaṃ kadalīphalāni (p.192, l.2)
yacchati | makaro 'pi nijadayitāyā arpayati | sā ca patiṃ (p.192, l.3)
tatphalavṛttāntaṃ pṛcchati | sa ca sarvaṃ yathāsthitaṃ nivedayati | tataḥ sā (p.192, l.4)
garbhānubhāvataś cintayām āsa | yo vānaro nityam īdṛśāni phalāni bhuṅkte (p.192, l.5)
tasyaurasyaṃ māṃsam amṛtopamaṃ syāt | iti vicintya patiṃ prāha | mama (p.192, l.6)
garbhānubhāvato vānarahṛdayapiśitabhakṣaṇe dohado vidyate | tad yadi pūrayasi (p.192, l.7)
tadā jīvāmi | anyathāsaṃśayaṃ mama mṛtyur bhaviṣyati | iti śrutvā (p.192, l.8)
dayitāgrahāc ca samudrataṭam āgatya vānaraṃ prāha | mitra tvadīyabhrātuḥ priyā (p.192, l.9)
tvām ākārayati | asmadīyo gṛhopacāro vilokanīyaḥ | ity uktvā (p.192, l.10)
viśvāsya pṛṣṭhe cāropya pracalitaḥ | vānaras taṃ gacchantaṃ śaṅkitaḥ prāha | (p.192, l.11)
tatra gatena mayā kiṃ vidheyam | ity ākarṇya makareṇa cintitam | vānaro (p.192, l.12)
'sau tasmāt sthānān mayā nītaḥ katham ambhonidhitaṭaṃ yāsyati tasmāt (p.192, l.13)
kathayāmi | ity avadhārya yathāsthitaṃ jagāda | tato vānaraḥ kathaṃ (p.193, l.1)
bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | vānaraḥ prāha | bho makara | tarhi tvaṃ māṃ (p.193, l.2)
tatra vṛthā nayasi yato 'haṃ hṛdayahīno bhavāmi | mama hṛdayaṃ mama (p.193, l.3)
pārśve nāsti | makaraḥ | kva muktaṃ tvayā | vānaraḥ | mitra kiṃ na (p.193, l.4)
śrutaṃ tvayā | (p.193, l.5)

ity uktvā punaḥ prāha | mitra tvam adyātithir asmākaṃ bhava | iti bhaṇitvā amṛtasadṛśāni pakvaphalāni dadau | tataḥ prabhṛti pratidinaṃ kadalīphalāni yacchati | makaro 'pi nijadayitāyā arpayati | sā ca patiṃ tatphalavṛttāntaṃ pṛcchati | sa ca sarvaṃ yathāsthitaṃ nivedayati | tataḥ sā garbhānubhāvataś cintayām āsa | yo vānaro nityam īdṛśāni phalāni bhuṅkte tasyaurasyaṃ māṃsam amṛtopamaṃ syāt | iti vicintya patiṃ prāha | mama garbhānubhāvato vānarahṛdayapiśitabhakṣaṇe dohado vidyate | tad yadi pūrayasi tadā jīvāmi | anyathāsaṃśayaṃ mama mṛtyur bhaviṣyati | iti śrutvā dayitāgrahāc ca samudrataṭam āgatya vānaraṃ prāha | mitra tvadīyabhrātuḥ priyā tvām ākārayati | asmadīyo gṛhopacāro vilokanīyaḥ | ity uktvā viśvāsya pṛṣṭhe cāropya pracalitaḥ | vānaras taṃ gacchantaṃ śaṅkitaḥ prāha | tatra gatena mayā kiṃ vidheyam | ity ākarṇya makareṇa cintitam | vānaro 'sau tasmāt sthānān mayā nītaḥ katham ambhonidhitaṭaṃ yāsyati tasmāt kathayāmi | ity avadhārya yathāsthitaṃ jagāda | tato vānaraḥ kathaṃ bhavatv iti praśnaḥ | śukaḥ | vānaraḥ prāha | bho makara | tarhi tvaṃ māṃ tatra vṛthā nayasi yato 'haṃ hṛdayahīno bhavāmi | mama hṛdayaṃ mama pārśve nāsti | makaraḥ | kva muktaṃ tvayā | vānaraḥ | mitra kiṃ na śrutaṃ tvayā |

p.193, l.5

sarvadodumbare vṛkṣe hṛdayaṃ vaṭabhūruhe |(p.193, l.6)
 cittam asti gṛhītvā tad āgacchāmi punar jalam || 67.7 (= 327) ||(p.193, l.7)
sarvadodumbare vṛkṣe hṛdayaṃ vaṭabhūruhe | cittam asti gṛhītvā tad āgacchāmi punar jalam || 67.7 (= 327) ||

p.193, l.7

ity ukte tadā makaro mūrkhaḥ samudrāntam āyayau | vānaro 'pi tatpṛṣṭhataḥ (p.193, l.8)
samuttīrya śākhinam ārohati sma | tato makaraṃ jagāda | gaccha gaccha | (p.193, l.9)
nāhaṃ bhāvadṛśair atrastho gṛhītuṃ śakyaḥ | (p.193, l.10)

ity ukte tadā makaro mūrkhaḥ samudrāntam āyayau | vānaro 'pi tatpṛṣṭhataḥ samuttīrya śākhinam ārohati sma | tato makaraṃ jagāda | gaccha gaccha | nāhaṃ bhāvadṛśair atrastho gṛhītuṃ śakyaḥ |

p.193, l.10

 sthalajaiḥ saṃgatir na syāt dhruveti munibhāṣitam || 67.8 (= 328) ||(p.194, l.1)

utpannā yuktikāryeṣu buddhir yasya na hīyate | sa eva tarate durgaṃ jalānte vānaro yathā || 67.9 (= 329) ||

p.194, l.4

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.194, l.5)
iti śukasaptatau saptaṣaṣṭitamī kathā || (p.194, l.6)

iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau saptaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

p.194, l.6

athānyedyuḥ śukaṃ prāha prabhāvatī | śukaḥ | (p.194, l.7)

athānyedyuḥ śukaṃ prāha prabhāvatī | śukaḥ |

p.194, l.7

yāhi devi sukhaṃ bhuṅkṣva yadi te 'sti sahāyinī |(p.194, l.8)
 vitarkasadṛśī kāle viṣame varavarṇini || 68.1 (= 330) ||(p.194, l.9)
yāhi devi sukhaṃ bhuṅkṣva yadi te 'sti sahāyinī | vitarkasadṛśī kāle viṣame varavarṇini || 68.1 (= 330) ||

p.194, l.9

asti vidyāsthānaṃ nāma grāmaḥ brāhmaṇānām | tatra keśavo brāhmaṇaḥ | (p.194, l.10)
tena ca snānāya gatena taṭāke ramyā vaṇikputrī dṛṣṭā | sa ca tāṃ (p.194, l.11)
rantum icchati | anyadā tayā prokto dvijaḥ snānād utthitaḥ | yat tvaṃ mama (p.195, l.1)
śirasi dvitīyaṃ ghaṭam āropaya | atas tena ghaṭam āropayatā tasyā oṣṭhaś cumbitaḥ | (p.195, l.2)
sa ca tathā kurvan patinā dṛṣṭaḥ | nīto rājakulaṃ kathaṃ mucyatām | (p.195, l.3)
iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ | śukaḥ prāha | atha tanmitraṃ vitarko (p.195, l.4)
nāma | sa ca tatsamīpam āgagatyedam abravīt | mitra tvayā rājakulagatena (p.195, l.5)
vacacety eva vākyaṃ jalpanīyaṃ nānyat | tathā kṛte ca mantriṇoktam | (p.195, l.6)
nāyaṃ doṣabhāk | prakṛtir evaṃvidhaivāsya | tenaiva cottareṇa loke sādhutāṃ (p.195, l.7)
gato vitarkasāhāyikabuddhyā | yadi tvam api tathā jānāsi tadā (p.195, l.8)
gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī supta | (p.195, l.9)
iti śukasaptatau aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

asti vidyāsthānaṃ nāma grāmaḥ brāhmaṇānām | tatra keśavo brāhmaṇaḥ | tena ca snānāya gatena taṭāke ramyā vaṇikputrī dṛṣṭā | sa ca tāṃ rantum icchati | anyadā tayā prokto dvijaḥ snānād utthitaḥ | yat tvaṃ mama śirasi dvitīyaṃ ghaṭam āropaya | atas tena ghaṭam āropayatā tasyā oṣṭhaś cumbitaḥ | sa ca tathā kurvan patinā dṛṣṭaḥ | nīto rājakulaṃ kathaṃ mucyatām | iti praśnaḥ | uttaraṃ | śukaḥ prāha | atha tanmitraṃ vitarko nāma | sa ca tatsamīpam āgagatyedam abravīt | mitra tvayā rājakulagatena vacacety eva vākyaṃ jalpanīyaṃ nānyat | tathā kṛte ca mantriṇoktam | nāyaṃ doṣabhāk | prakṛtir evaṃvidhaivāsya | tenaiva cottareṇa loke sādhutāṃ gato vitarkasāhāyikabuddhyā | yadi tvam api tathā jānāsi tadā gaccha | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī supta | iti śukasaptatau aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamī kathā ||

(p.196, l.1)

p.196, l.2

kuru jāraṃ viśālākṣi vijāraṃ kuruṣe yadi |(p.196, l.3)
 yathā vejikayā pūrvam ardhasnāte patau kṛtam || 69.1 (= 331) ||(p.196, l.4)
kuru jāraṃ viśālākṣi vijāraṃ kuruṣe yadi | yathā vejikayā pūrvam ardhasnāte patau kṛtam || 69.1 (= 331) ||

p.196, l.4

asti sthānaṃ kalāsthānaṃ nāma | tatraiko vaṇiksutaḥ | tasya bhāryā ca (p.196, l.5)
vejikā nāmātivallabhā | anyadā ca taṃ bhartāraṃ snāpayantī upapatiṃ (p.196, l.6)
pūrvakṛtasaṃketaṃ pathi gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā nātra pānīyaṃ pracuram iti miṣāntaraṃ (p.196, l.7)
kṛtvā pānīyānayanavyājād gṛhān nirgatā jāreṇa sākaṃ bahukālaṃ ca sthitā | (p.197, l.1)
tato 'rdhasnātaṃ patiṃ muktvā tathā sthitā kim uttaraṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | (p.197, l.2)
uttaram | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā jāreṇa bhuktā svapativañcanaṃ vicintyātmānaṃ (p.197, l.3)
kūpe cikṣepa | tataḥ kolāhalaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | kūpe kāpi varākī patitāstīti (p.197, l.4)
pravādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | tena tatpatis tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyacintayat | nūnaṃ (p.197, l.5)
sā matpatnī kūpe patitā bhaviṣyati | iti drutaṃ gatvāvalokayām āsa | (p.197, l.6)
tatas tāṃ kūpād ākṛṣyānīyāmānayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | (p.197, l.7)
iti śukasaptatau ekonasaptatitamī kathā || (p.197, l.8)

asti sthānaṃ kalāsthānaṃ nāma | tatraiko vaṇiksutaḥ | tasya bhāryā ca vejikā nāmātivallabhā | anyadā ca taṃ bhartāraṃ snāpayantī upapatiṃ pūrvakṛtasaṃketaṃ pathi gacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā nātra pānīyaṃ pracuram iti miṣāntaraṃ kṛtvā pānīyānayanavyājād gṛhān nirgatā jāreṇa sākaṃ bahukālaṃ ca sthitā | tato 'rdhasnātaṃ patiṃ muktvā tathā sthitā kim uttaraṃ karotv iti praśnaḥ | uttaram | śukaḥ | tataḥ sā jāreṇa bhuktā svapativañcanaṃ vicintyātmānaṃ kūpe cikṣepa | tataḥ kolāhalaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ | kūpe kāpi varākī patitāstīti pravādaḥ saṃjātaḥ | tena tatpatis tadvacanaṃ śrutvā vyacintayat | nūnaṃ sā matpatnī kūpe patitā bhaviṣyati | iti drutaṃ gatvāvalokayām āsa | tatas tāṃ kūpād ākṛṣyānīyāmānayat | iti kathāṃ śrutvā prabhāvatī suptā | iti śukasaptatau ekonasaptatitamī kathā ||

p.202, l.7

śukaḥ kathāṃ madanāgre kathayām āsa | asti jagatītale malayo nāma (p.202, l.8)
parvataḥ | tasya śṛṅge manoharaṃ nāma gandharvapuram | tatra madano nāma (p.202, l.9)
gandharvaḥ | tasya bhāryā ratnāvalī | tayoḥ sutā madanamañjarī | tasyā (p.202, l.10)
rūpasaṃpadaṃ dṛṣṭvā devo vā dānavo vādhomukho muhyati | na ko 'pi (p.203, l.1)
tadanurūpo varo labhyate yasya sā dīyate | athānyadā nāradaḥ samāyātaḥ | (p.203, l.2)
so 'py asyā rūpam avalokya mūrcchitaḥ sakāmo 'bhūt | paścāl labdhasaṃjñena (p.203, l.3)
ṛṣiṇā sā śaptā | (p.203, l.4)

śukaḥ kathāṃ madanāgre kathayām āsa | asti jagatītale malayo nāma parvataḥ | tasya śṛṅge manoharaṃ nāma gandharvapuram | tatra madano nāma gandharvaḥ | tasya bhāryā ratnāvalī | tayoḥ sutā madanamañjarī | tasyā rūpasaṃpadaṃ dṛṣṭvā devo vā dānavo vādhomukho muhyati | na ko 'pi tadanurūpo varo labhyate yasya sā dīyate | athānyadā nāradaḥ samāyātaḥ | so 'py asyā rūpam avalokya mūrcchitaḥ sakāmo 'bhūt | paścāl labdhasaṃjñena ṛṣiṇā sā śaptā |

p.203, l.4

uktaṃ ca |

 yadi sā subhagā hṛdaye nihitā kva jayaḥ kva ● ● ● ● ● || 70.17 (= 348) ||(p.203, l.6)

uktaṃ ca |

taruṇī ramaṇī ratiramyatarā pramadā sukhadā ca sadā samadā | yadi sā subhagā hṛdaye nihitā kva jayaḥ kva ● ● ● ● ● || 70.17 (= 348) ||

p.203, l.6

yad etasyā rūpe dṛṣṭe me smarajvaro jātaḥ tad iyaṃ śīlaviḍambanāṃ prāpsyate | (p.203, l.7)
tato rājā praṇamya prāha | svāmin prasanno bhūtvā prasādaṃ kuru | (p.203, l.8)
nārada āha | nāsyāḥ śīlakhaṇḍane doṣo bhaviṣyati na ca pativirahaḥ | (p.203, l.9)
meruparvate vipulāpurīnivāsī kanakaprabho nāma gandharvaḥ | sa (p.203, l.10)
tava putryā varo bhaviṣyati | ity uktvā nārado yayau | tato munivacanena (p.204, l.1)
tena gandharveṇa sodvāhitā | so 'nyadā tāṃ muktvā kailāsaṃ yayau | (p.204, l.2)
sāpi tadviyogārtā śilāpaṭṭe luṭhantī vastrādirahitā kenacid vidyādhareṇa (p.204, l.3)
rūpātiśayam avalokya saṃyogārthaṃ prārthitā | sā taṃ na vāñchati | (p.204, l.4)
tatas tena tadbhartur gandharvarūpaṃ kṛtvā sā bhuktā | tataḥ kālakrameṇa tasyā (p.204, l.5)
bhartā gṛham āgataḥ | tāṃ suratasukhasaṃtuṣṭām apaśyat | paropabhuktadeheyam (p.204, l.6)
iti tāṃ duṣṭāṃ matvā sāvaśyaṃ vadhyeti niścitya caṇḍikālayaṃ yayau | (p.204, l.7)
yāvat tadagrato mārayati tāvad anayā phūtkṛtam | svāmini mama tvayā (p.204, l.8)
varo datto yat tava gandharvacakravartī putro bhaviṣyati | tat kathaṃ putramukham (p.204, l.9)
adṛṣṭvā vipatsye | evaṃ vilapantyās tasyāḥ puratas tāṃ prati devī prāha | (p.204, l.10)
he gandharvavīra nāsyāḥ ko 'pi doṣaḥ | kiṃ tu vidyādhareṇeyaṃ tvadīyarūpam (p.204, l.11)
ayena māyayā bhuktā | tato 'jānantyā asyā na doṣaḥ | anyac ca (p.204, l.12)
muniśāpo vidyate | tata idaṃ saṃjātam | śāpavṛttāntaś ca niveditaḥ | (p.205, l.1)
tato munivacanād iyaṃ nirdoṣā tvayā grāhyā | iti gaurīvacanaṃ śrutvā (p.205, l.2)
sa niḥśaṅkaṃ tayā saha svasthānaṃ gatas tathaiva sukhito 'bhūt | tato vaṇikputra (p.205, l.3)
yadi madvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadainām aduṣṭāṃ prati prasādaṃ kartum arhasi | (p.205, l.4)
iti kīravacanān madanenānugṛhītā | tato haridatto 'pi putrāgamanatuṣṭo (p.205, l.5)
mahotsavaṃ cakāra | tasmin mahotsave divyamālā patitā | taddarśane (p.205, l.6)
śukasārikātrivikramāṇāṃ śāpamokṣāt svargagamanaṃ babhūva | madano 'pi (p.205, l.7)
priyayā prabhāvatyā saha sukhāni bhuṅkte | (p.205, l.8)
iti śukasaptatiḥ samāptā || (p.205, l.9)

yad etasyā rūpe dṛṣṭe me smarajvaro jātaḥ tad iyaṃ śīlaviḍambanāṃ prāpsyate | tato rājā praṇamya prāha | svāmin prasanno bhūtvā prasādaṃ kuru | nārada āha | nāsyāḥ śīlakhaṇḍane doṣo bhaviṣyati na ca pativirahaḥ | meruparvate vipulāpurīnivāsī kanakaprabho nāma gandharvaḥ | sa tava putryā varo bhaviṣyati | ity uktvā nārado yayau | tato munivacanena tena gandharveṇa sodvāhitā | so 'nyadā tāṃ muktvā kailāsaṃ yayau | sāpi tadviyogārtā śilāpaṭṭe luṭhantī vastrādirahitā kenacid vidyādhareṇa rūpātiśayam avalokya saṃyogārthaṃ prārthitā | sā taṃ na vāñchati | tatas tena tadbhartur gandharvarūpaṃ kṛtvā sā bhuktā | tataḥ kālakrameṇa tasyā bhartā gṛham āgataḥ | tāṃ suratasukhasaṃtuṣṭām apaśyat | paropabhuktadeheyam iti tāṃ duṣṭāṃ matvā sāvaśyaṃ vadhyeti niścitya caṇḍikālayaṃ yayau | yāvat tadagrato mārayati tāvad anayā phūtkṛtam | svāmini mama tvayā varo datto yat tava gandharvacakravartī putro bhaviṣyati | tat kathaṃ putramukham adṛṣṭvā vipatsye | evaṃ vilapantyās tasyāḥ puratas tāṃ prati devī prāha | he gandharvavīra nāsyāḥ ko 'pi doṣaḥ | kiṃ tu vidyādhareṇeyaṃ tvadīyarūpam ayena māyayā bhuktā | tato 'jānantyā asyā na doṣaḥ | anyac ca muniśāpo vidyate | tata idaṃ saṃjātam | śāpavṛttāntaś ca niveditaḥ | tato munivacanād iyaṃ nirdoṣā tvayā grāhyā | iti gaurīvacanaṃ śrutvā sa niḥśaṅkaṃ tayā saha svasthānaṃ gatas tathaiva sukhito 'bhūt | tato vaṇikputra yadi madvacaḥ pramāṇaṃ tadainām aduṣṭāṃ prati prasādaṃ kartum arhasi | iti kīravacanān madanenānugṛhītā | tato haridatto 'pi putrāgamanatuṣṭo mahotsavaṃ cakāra | tasmin mahotsave divyamālā patitā | taddarśane śukasārikātrivikramāṇāṃ śāpamokṣāt svargagamanaṃ babhūva | madano 'pi priyayā prabhāvatyā saha sukhāni bhuṅkte | iti śukasaptatiḥ samāptā ||
